śrīśivamahāpurāṇam

atha śrīśivamahāpurāṇaṃ vidyeśvarasaṃhitā prārabhyate

śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ // śrīgurubhyo namaḥ // śrisarasvatyai namaḥ // atha śivapuraṇe prathamā vidyeśvarasaṃhitāprārabhyate // ādyantamaṃgalamajātasamānabhāvamāryaṃ tamīśamajarāmaramātmadevam

paṃcānanaṃ prabalapaṃcavinodaśīlaṃ saṃbhāvaye manasiśaṃkaramambikeśam || 1 ||

vyāsa uvāca |

dharmakṣetre mahākṣetre gaṃgākālindisaṃgame |
prayāge parame puṇye brahmalokasya vartmani || 1 ||

munayaḥ śaṃsitātmanassatyavrataparāyaṇāḥ |
mahaujaso mahābhāgā mahāsatraṃ vitenire || 2 ||

tatra satraṃ samākarṇya vyāsaśiṣyo mahāmuniḥ |
ājagāma munīndraṣṭuṃ sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ || 3 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvā sūtamāyāntaṃ harṣitā munayastadā |
cetasā suprasannena pūjāṃ cakruryathāvidhi || 4 ||

tato vinayasaṃyuktā procuḥ sāṃjalayaścate |
suprasannā mahātmānaḥ stutiṃ kṛtvāyathāvidhi || 5 ||

romaharṣaṇa sarvajña bhavānvai bhāgyagauravāt |
purāṇavidyāmakhilāṃ vyāsātpratyarthamīyivān || 6 ||

tasmādāścaryyabhūtānāṃ kathānāṃ tvaṃ hi bhājanam |
ratnānāmurusārāṇāṃ ratnākara ivārṇavaḥ || 7 ||

yacca bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca yaccānyadvastu vartate |
na tvayā .aviditaṃ kiṃcittriṣu lokeṣu vidyate || 8 ||

tvaṃ maddiṣṭavaśādasya darśanārthamihāgataḥ |
kurvankimapi naḥ śreyo na vṛthā gantumarhasi || 9 ||

tattvaṃ śrutaṃ sma naḥ sarvaṃ pūrvameva śubhāśubham |
na tṛptimadhigacchāmaḥ śravaṇecchā muhurmuhuḥ || 10 ||

idānīmekamevāsti śrotavyaṃ sūta sanmate |
tadrahasyamapi brūhi yadi te .anugraho bhavet || 11 ||

prāpte kaliyuge ghore narāḥ puṇyavivarjitāḥ |
durācāraratāḥ sarve satyavārtāparāṅmukhāḥ || 12 ||

parāpavādaniratāḥ paradravyābhilāṣiṇaḥ |
parastrīsaktamanasaḥ parahiṃsāparāyaṇāḥ || 13 ||

dehātmadṛṣṭayā mūḍhā nāstikāḥ paśubuddhayaḥ |
mātṛpitṛkṛtadveṣāḥ strīdevāḥ kāmakiṃkarāḥ || 14 ||

viprā lobhagrahagrastā vedavikrayajīvinaḥ |
dhanārjanārthamabhyastavidyā madavimohitāḥ || 15 ||

tyaktasvajātikarmāṇaḥ prāyaśaḥparavaṃcakāḥ |
trikālasaṃdhyayā hīnā brahmabodhavivarjitāḥ || 16 ||

adayāḥ paṃḍitaṃmanyāssvācāravratalopakāḥ |
kṛṣyudyamaratāḥ krūrasvabhāvā malināśayāḥ || 17 ||

kṣatriyāśca tathā sarve svadharmatyāgaśīlinaḥ |
asatsaṃgāḥ pāparatā vyabhicāraparāyaṇāḥ || 18 ||

aśūrā araṇaprītāḥ palāyanaparāyaṇāḥ |
kucauravṛttayaḥ śūdrāḥ kāmakiṃkaracetasaḥ || 19 ||

śastrāstravidyayā hīnā dhenuviprāvanojjhitāḥ |
śaraṇyāvanahīnāśca kāminyūtimṛgāssadā || 20 ||

prajāpālanasaddharmavihīnā bhogatatparāḥ |
prajāsaṃhārakā duṣṭā jīvahiṃsākarā mudā || 21 ||

vaiśyāḥ saṃskārahīnāste svadharmatyāgaśīlinaḥ |
kupathāḥ svārjanaratāstulākarmakuvṛttayaḥ || 22 ||

gurudevadvijātīnāṃ bhaktihīnāḥ kubuddhayaḥ |
abhojitadvijāḥ prāyaḥ kṛpaṇā baddhamuṣṭayaḥ || 23 ||

kāminījārabhāveṣu suratā malināśayāḥ |
lobhamohavicetaskāḥ pūrtādisuvṛṣojjhitāḥ || 24 ||

tadvacchūdrāśca ye kecidbrāhmaṇācāratatparāḥ |
ujjvalākṛtayo mūḍhāḥ svadharmatyāgaśīlinaḥ || 25 ||

kartārastapasāṃ bhūyo dvijatejopahārakāḥ |
śiśvalpamṛtyukārāśca mantroccāraparāyaṇāḥ || 26 ||

śāligrāmaśilādīnāṃ pūjakāhomatatparāḥ |
pratikūlavicārāśca kuṭilā dvijadūṣakāḥ || 27 ||

dhanavantaḥ kukarmmāṇo vidyāvanto vivādinaḥ |
ākhyāyopāsanā dharmavaktāro dharmalopakāḥ || 28 ||

subhūpākṛtayo daṃbhāḥ sudātāro mahāmadāḥ |
viprādīnsevakānmatvā manyamānā nijaṃ prabhum || 29 ||

svadharmarahitā mūḍhāḥ saṃkarāḥ krūrabuddhayaḥ |
mahābhimānino nityaṃ caturvarṇavilopakāḥ || 30 ||

sukulīnānnijānmatvā caturvarṇairvivartanāḥ |
sarvavarṇabhraṣṭakarā mūḍhāssatkarmakāriṇaḥ || 31 ||

striyaśca prāyaśo bhraṣṭā bhartravajñānakārikāḥ |
śvaśuradrohakāriṇyo nirbhayā malināśanāḥ || 32 ||

kuhāvabhāvaniratāḥ kuśīlāssmaravihvalāḥ |
jārasaṃgaratā nityaṃ svasvāmivimukhāstathā || 33 ||

tanayā mātṛpitrośca bhaktihīnā durāśayāḥ |
avidyāpāṭhakā nityaṃ rogagrasitadehakāḥ || 34 ||

eteṣāṃ naṣṭabuddhīnāṃ svadharmatyāgaśīlinām |
paralokepīha loke kathaṃ sūta gatirbhavet || 35 ||

iti ciṃtākulaṃ cittaṃ jāyate satataṃ hi naḥ |
paropakārasadṛśo nāsti dharmo paraḥ khalu || 36 ||

laghūpāyena yenaiṣāṃ bhavetsadyoghanāśanam |
sarvvasiddhāntavittvaṃ hi kṛpayā tadvadādhunā || 37 ||

vyāsa uvāca |

ityākarṇya vacasteṣāṃ munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām |
manasā śaṃkaraṃ smṛtvā sūtaḥ provāca tānmunīn || 38 ||

iti śrīśaivemahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ munipraśnavarṇanonāmaprathamo .adhyāyaḥ || 1 ||

sūta uvāca |

sādhupṛṣṭaṃ sādhavo vastrailokyahitakārakam |
guruṃ smṛtvā bhavatsnehādvakṣye tacchṛṇutādarāt || 1 ||

vedāntasārasarvasvaṃ purāṇaṃ śaivamuttamam |
sarvāghaughoddhārakaraṃ paratra paramārthadam || 2 ||

kalikalmaṣavidhvaṃsi yasmiñchivayaśaḥ param |
vijṛmbhate sadā viprāścaturvargaphalapradam || 3 ||

tasyādhyayanamātreṇa purāṇasya dvijottamāḥ |
sarvottamasya śaivasya te yāsyanti susadgatim || 4 ||

tāvadvijṛṃbhate pāpaṃ brahmahatyāpurassaram |
yāvacchivapurāṇaṃ hi nodeṣyati jagatyaho || 5 ||

tāvatkalimahotpātāḥ saṃcariṣyanti nirbhayāḥ |
yāvacchivapurāṇaṃ hi nodeṣyati jagatyaho || 6 ||

tāvatsarvāṇi śāstrāṇi vivadanti parasparam |
yāvacchivapurāṇaṃ hi nodeṣyati jagatyaho || 7 ||

tāvatsvarūpaṃ durbodhaṃ śivasya mahatāmapi |
yāvacchivapurāṇaṃ hi no deṣyati jagatyaho || 8 ||

tāvadyamabhaṭāḥ krūrāḥ saṃcariṣyanti nirbhayāḥ |
yāvacchivapurāṇaṃ hi nodeṣyati jagatyaho || 9 ||

tāvatsarvapurāṇāni pragarjanti mahītale |
yāvacchivapurāṇaṃ hi nodeṣyati jagatyaho || 10 ||

tāvatsarvāṇi tīrthāni vivadanti mahītale |
yāvachivapurāṇaṃ hi nodeṣyati jagatyaho || 11 ||

tāvatsarvāṇi mantrāṇi vivadanti mahītale |
yāvacchivapurāṇaṃ hi nodeṣyati mahītale || 12 ||

tāvatsarvāṇi kṣetrāṇi vivadanti mahītale |
yāvacchivapurāṇaṃ hi nodeṣyati mahītale || 13 ||

tāvatsarvāṇi pīṭhāni vivadanti mahītale |
yāvacchivapurāṇaṃ hi nodeṣyati mahītale || 14 ||

tāvatsarvāṇi dānāni vivadanti mahītale |
yāvacchivapurāṇaṃ hi nodeṣyati mahītale || 15 ||

tāvatsarve ca te devā vivadanti mahītale |
yāvacchivapurāṇaṃ hi nodeṣyati mahītale || 16 ||

tāvatsarve ca siddhāntā vivadanti mahītale |
yāvacchivapurāṇaṃ hi nodeṣyati mahītale || 17 ||

asya śaivapurāṇasya kīrtanaśravaṇāddvijāḥ |
phalaṃ vaktuṃ na śaknomi kārtsnyena munisattamāḥ || 18 ||

tathāpi tasya māhātmyaṃ vakṣye kiṃcittu vonaghāḥ |
cittamādhāya śṛṇuta vyāsenoktaṃ purā mama || 19 ||

etacchivapurāṇaṃ hi ślokaṃ ślokārddhameva ca |
yaḥ paṭhedbhaktisaṃyuktassa pāpānmucyate kṣaṇāt || 20 ||

etacchivapurāṇaṃ hi yaḥ pratyahamataṃdritaḥ |
yathāśakti paṭhedbhaktyā sa jīvanmukta ucyate || 21 ||

etacchivapurāṇaṃ hi yo bhaktyārcayate sadā |
dine dine .aśvamedhasya phalaṃ prāpnotyasaṃśayam / || 22 ||

etacchivapurāṇaṃ yassādhāraṇapadecchayā |
anyataḥ śṛṇuyātso .api matto mucyeta pātakāt || 23 ||

etacchivapurāṇaṃ yo namaskuryādadūrataḥ |
sarvadevārcanaphalaṃ sa prāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ || 24 ||

etacchivapurāṇaṃ vai likhitvā pustakaṃ svayam |
yo dadyācchivabhaktebhyastasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu || 25 ||

adhīteṣu ca śāstreṣu vedeṣu vyākṛteṣu ca |
yatphalaṃ durlabhaṃ loke tatphalaṃ tasya saṃbhavet || 26 ||

etacchivapurāṇaṃ hi caturdaśyāmupoṣitaḥ |
śivabhaktasabhāyāṃ yo vyākaroti sa uttamaḥ || 27 ||

pratyakṣaraṃ tu gāyatrīpuraścaryyāphalaṃ labhet |
iha bhuktvākhilānkāmānante nirvāṇatāṃ vrajet || 28 ||

upoṣitaścaturdaśyāṃ rātrau jāgaraṇānvitaḥ |
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi tasya puṇyaṃ vadāmyaham || 29 ||

kurukṣetrādinikhilapuṇyatīrtheṣvanekaśaḥ |
ātmatulyadhanaṃ sūryyagrahaṇe sarvatomukhe || 30 ||

viprebhyo vyāsamukhyebhyo dattvāyatphalamaśnute |
tatphalaṃ saṃbhavettasya satyaṃ satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ || 31 ||

etacchivapurāṇaṃ hi gāyate yopyaharniśam |
ājñāṃ tasya pratīkṣerandevā indrapurogamāḥ || 32 ||

etacchivapurāṇaṃ yaḥ paṭhañchṛṇvanhi nityaśaḥ |
yadyatkaroti satkarma tatkoṭiguṇitaṃ bhavet || 33 ||

samāhitaḥ paṭhedyastu tatra śrīrudrasaṃhitām |
sa brahmaghno.api pūtātmā tribhireva dinairbhavet || 34 ||

tāṃ rudrasaṃhitāṃ yastu bhairavapratimāntike |
triḥ paṭhetpratyahaṃ maunī sa kāmānakhilĀllabhet || 35 ||

tāṃ rudrasaṃhitāṃ yastu sapaṭhedvaṭabilvayoḥ |
pradakṣiṇāṃ prakurvāṇo brahmahatyā nivartate || 36 ||

kailāsasaṃhitā tatra tato.api paramasmṛtā |
brahmasvarūpiṇī sākṣātpraṇavārthaprakāśikā || 37 ||

kailāsasaṃhitāyāstu māhātmyaṃ vetti śaṃkaraḥ |
kṛtsnaṃ tadarddhaṃ vyāsaśca tadarddhaṃ vedmyahaṃ dvijāḥ || 38 ||

tatra kiṃcitpravakṣyāmi kṛtsnaṃ vaktuṃ na śakyate |
yajjñātvā tatkṣaṇāllokaścittaśuddhimavāpnuyāt || 39 ||

na nāśayati yatpāpaṃ sā raudrī saṃhitā dvijāḥ |
tanna paśyāmyahaṃ loke mārgamāṇo.api sarvadā || 40 ||

śivenopaniṣatsiṃdhumanthanotpāditāṃ mudā |
kumārāyārpitāṃ tāṃ vai sudhāṃ pītvā .amaro bhavet || 41 ||

brahmahatyādipāpānāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ kartumudyataḥ |
māsamātraṃ saṃhitāṃ tāṃ paṭhitvā mucyate tataḥ || 42 ||

duṣpratigrahadurbhojyadurālāpādisaṃbhavam |
pāpaṃ sakṛtkīrtanena saṃhitā sā vināśayet || 43 ||

śivālaye bilvavane saṃhitāṃ tāṃ paṭhettu yaḥ |
sa tatphalamavāpnoti yadvāco .api na gocare || 44 ||

saṃhitāṃ tāṃ paṭhanbhaktyā yaḥ śrāddhe bhojayeddvijān |
tasya ye pitaraḥ sarve yānti śaṃbhoḥ paraṃ padam || 45 ||

caturdaśyāṃ nirāhāro yaḥ paṭhetsaṃhitāṃ ca tām |
bilvamūle śivaḥ sākṣātsa devaiśca prapūjyate || 46 ||

anyāpi saṃhitā tatra sarvakāmaphalapradā |
ubhe viśiṣṭe vijñeye līlāvijñānapūrite || 47 ||

tadidaṃ śaivamākhyātaṃ purāṇaṃ vedasaṃmitam |
nirmitaṃ tacchivenaiva prathamaṃ brahmasaṃmitam || 48 ||

vidyeśaṃca tathāraudraṃ vaināyakamathaumikam |
mātraṃ rudraikādaśakaṃ kailāsaṃ śatarudrakam || 49 ||

koṭirudrasahasrādyaṃ koṭirudraṃ tathaiva ca |
vāyavīyaṃ dharmasaṃjñaṃ purāṇamiti bhedataḥ || 50 ||

saṃhitā dvādaśamitā mahāpuṇyatarā matā |
tāsāṃ saṃkhyāṃ bruve viprāḥ śṛṇutādaratokhilam || 51 ||

vidyeśaṃ daśāsāhasraṃ rudraṃ vaināyakaṃ tathā |
aumaṃ mātṛpurāṇākhyaṃ pratyekāṣṭasahasrakam || 52 ||

trayodaśasahasraṃ hi rudraikādaśakaṃ dvijāḥ |
ṣaṭsahasraṃ ca kailāsaṃ śatarudraṃ tadarddhakam || 53 ||

koṭirudraṃ triguṇitamekādaśasahasrakam |
sahasrakoṭirudrākhyamuditaṃ granthasaṃkhyayā || 54 ||

vāyavīyaṃ khābdhiśataṃ gharmaṃ ravisahasrakam |
tadevaṃ lakṣasaṃkhyākaṃ śaivasaṃkhyāvibhedataḥ || 55 ||

vyāsena tattu saṃkṣiptaṃ caturviṃśatsahasrakam |
śaivaṃ tatra caturthaṃ vai purāṇaṃ saptasaṃhitam || 56 ||

śive saṃkalpitaṃ pūrvaṃ purāṇaṃ granthasaṃkhyayā |
śatakoṭipramāṇaṃ hi purā sṛṣṭau suvismṛtam || 57 ||

vyasteṣṭādaśadhā caiva purāṇe dvāparādiṣu |
caturlakṣeṇa saṃkṣipte kṛte dvaipāyanādibhiḥ || 58 ||

proktaṃ śivapurāṇaṃ hi caturviṃśatsahasrakam |
ślokānāṃ saṃkhyayā saptasaṃhitaṃ brahmasaṃmitam || 59 ||

vidyeśvarākhyā tatrādyā raudrī jñeyā dvitīyikā |
tṛtīyā śatarudrākhyā koṭirudrā caturthikā || 60 ||

paṃcamī caiva maumākhyā ṣaṣṭhī kailāsasaṃjñikā |
saptamī vāyavīyākhyā saptaivaṃ saṃhitāmatāḥ || 61 ||

sasaptasaṃhitaṃ divyaṃ purāṇaṃ śivasaṃjñakam |
varīvarti brahmatulyaṃ sarvopari gatipradam || 62 ||

etacchivapurāṇaṃ hi saptasaṃhitamādarāt |
paripūrṇaṃ paṭhedyastu sa jīvanmukta ucyate || 63 ||

śrutismṛtipurāṇetihāsāgamaśatāni ca |
etacchivapurāṇasya nārhantyalpāṃ kalāmapi || 64 ||

śaivaṃ purāṇamamalaṃ śivakīrtitaṃ tadvyāsena śaivapravaṇena na saṃgṛhītam |
saṃkṣepataḥ sakalajīvaguṇopakāre tāpatrayaghnamatulaṃ śivadaṃ satāṃ hi || 65 ||

vikaitavo dharma iha pragīto vedāntavijñānamayaḥ pradhānaḥ |
amatsarāntarbudhavedyavastu satkLptamatraiva trivargayuktam || 66 ||

śaivaṃ purāṇatilakaṃ khalu satpurāṇaṃ vedāntavedavilasatparavastugītam |
yo vai paṭhecca śṛṇuyātparamādareṇa śaṃbhupriyaḥ sa hi labhetparamāṃ gatiṃ vai || 67 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ dvidīyo .adhyāyaḥ || 2 ||

vyāsa uvāca |

ityākarṇya vacaḥ sautaṃ procuste paramarṣayaḥ |
vedāntasārasarvasvaṃ purāṇaṃ śrāvayādbhutam || 1 ||

iti śrutvā munīnāṃ sa vacanaṃ supraharṣitaḥ |
saṃsmarañchaṃkaraṃ sūtaḥ provāca munisattamān || 2 ||

sūta uvāca |

śṛṇvantu ṛṣayaḥ sarve smṛtvā śivamanāmayam |
purāṇapravaṇaṃ śaivaṃ purāṇaṃ vedasārajam || 3 ||

yatra gītaṃ trikaṃ prītyā bhaktijñānavirāgakam || 4 ||

vedāntavedyaṃ sadvastu viśeṣeṇa pravarṇitam || 5 ||

sūta uvāca |

śṛṇvantu ṛṣayaḥ sarve purāṇaṃ vedasārajam |
purā kālena mahatā kalpe .atīte punaḥpunaḥ || 6 ||

asminnupasthite kalpe pravṛtte sṛṣṭikarmaṇi |
munīnāṃ ṣaṭkulīnānāṃ bruvatāmitaretaram || 7 ||

idaṃ paramidaṃ neti vivādaḥ sumahānabhūt |
te .abhijagmurvidhātāraṃ brahmāṇaṃ praṣṭumavyayam || 8 ||

vāgbhirvinayagarbhābhiḥ sarve prāṃjalayo .abruvan |
tvaṃ hi sarvajagaddhātā sarvakāraṇakāraṇam || 9 ||

kaḥ pumānsarvatattvebhyaḥ purāṇaḥ parataḥ paraḥ |

brahmovāca |

yato vāco nivartante aprāpya manasā saha || 10 ||

yasmātsarvamidaṃ brahmaviṣṇurudreṃdrapūrvakam |
sahabhūteṃdriyaiḥ sarvaiḥ prathamaṃ saṃprasūyate || 11 ||

eṣa devo mahādevaḥ sarvajño jagadīśvaraḥ |
ayaṃ tu parayā bhaktyā dṛśyate nā .anyathā kvacit || 12 ||

rudro harirharaścaiva tathānye ca sureśvarāḥ |
bhaktyā paramayā tasya nityaṃ darśanakāṃkṣiṇaḥ || 13 ||

bahunātra kimuktena śive bhaktyā vimucyate |
prasādāddevatābhaktiḥ prasādo bhaktisaṃbhavaḥ |
yathehāṃkurato bījaṃ bījato vā yathāṃkuraḥ || 14 ||

tasmādīśaprasādārthaṃ yūyaṃ gatvā bhuvaṃ dvijāḥ |
dīrghasatraṃ samākṛdhvaṃ yūyaṃ varṣasahasrakam || 15 ||

amuṣyaivādhvareśasya śivasyaiva prasādataḥ |
vedoktavidyāsāraṃ tu jñāyate sādhyasādhanaṃ || 16 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

atha kiṃ paramaṃ sādhyaṃ kiṃvā tatsādhanaṃ param |
sādhakaḥ kīdṛśastatra tadidaṃ brūhi tattvataḥ || 17 ||

brahmovāca |

sādhyaṃ śivapadaprāptiḥ sādhanaṃ tasya sevanam |
sādhakastatprasādādyo.anityādiphalaniḥspṛhaḥ || 18 ||

karma kṛtvā tu vedoktaṃ tadarpitamahāphalam |
parameśapadaprāptaḥ sālokyādikramāttataḥ || 19 ||

tattadbhaktyanusāreṇa sarveṣāṃ paramaṃ phalam |
tatsādhanaṃ bahuvidhaṃ sākṣādīśena bodhitam || 20 ||

saṃkṣipya tatra vaḥ sāraṃ sādhanaṃ prabravīmyaham |
śrotreṇa śravaṇaṃ tasya vacasā kīrtanaṃ tathā || 21 ||

manasā mananaṃ tasya mahāsādhanamucyate |
śrotavyaḥ kīrtitavyaśca mantavyaśca maheśvaraḥ || 22 ||

iti śrutipramāṇaṃ naḥ sādhanenā.amunā param |
sādhyaṃ vrajata sarvārthasādhanaikaparāyaṇāḥ || 23 ||

pratyakṣaṃ cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭvā tatra lokaḥ pravartate |
apratyakṣaṃ hi sarvatra jñātvā śrotreṇa ceṣṭate || 24 ||

tasmācchravaṇamevādau śrutvā gurumukhādbudhaḥ |
tataḥ saṃsādhayedanyatkīrtanaṃ mananaṃ sudhīḥ || 25 ||

kramānmananaparyante sādhane .asminsusādhite |
śivayogo bhavettena sālokyādikramācchanaiḥ || 26 ||

sarvāṃgavyādhayaḥ paścātsarvānaṃdaśca līyate |
abhyāsātkleśametadvai paścādādyantamaṃgalam || 27 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ sādhyasādhanakhaṇḍe tṛtīyo .adhyāyaḥ || 3 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

mananaṃ kīdṛśaṃ brahmañchravaṇaṃ cāpi kīdṛśam |
kīrtanaṃ vā kathaṃ tasya kīrtayaitadyathāyatham || 1 ||

brahmovaca

pūjājapeśaguṇarūpavilāsanāmnāṃ yuktipriyeṇa manasā pariśodhanaṃ yat |
tatsantataṃ mananamīśvaradṛṣṭilabhyaṃ sarveṣu sādhanavareṣvapi mukhyamukhyam || 2 ||

gītātmanā śrutipadena ca bhāṣayā vā śaṃbhupratāpaguṇarūpavilāsanāmnām |
vācā sphuṭaṃ tu rasavatstavanaṃ yadasya tatkīrtanaṃ bhavati sādhanamatra madhyam || 3 ||

yenāpi kena karaṇena ca śabdapuṃjaṃ yatra kvacicchivaparaṃ śravaṇeṃdriyeṇa |
strīkelivaddṛḍhataraṃ praṇidhīyate yattadvai budhāḥ śravaṇamatra jagatprasiddham || 4 ||

satsaṃgamena bhavati śravaṇaṃ purastātsaṃkīrtanaṃ paśupateratha taddṛḍhaṃ syāt |
sarvottamaṃ bhavati tanmananaṃ tadante sarvaṃ hi saṃbhavati śaṃkaradṛṣṭipāte || 5 ||

sūta uvāca |

asminsādhanamāhatmye purā vṛttaṃ munīśvarāḥ |
yuṣmadarthaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvamavadhānataḥ || 6 ||

purā mama gururvyāsaḥ parāśaramuneḥ sutaḥ |
tapaścacāra saṃbhrāntaḥ sarasvatyāstaṭe śubhe || 7 ||

gacchanyadṛchayā tatra vimānenārkarociṣā |
sanatkumāro bhagavāndadarśa mama deśikam || 8 ||

dhyānārūḍhaḥ prabuddho .asau dadarśa tamajātmajam |
praṇipatyāha saṃbhrāntaḥ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ muniḥ || 9 ||

dattvārghyamasmai pradadau devayogyaṃ ca viṣṭiram |
prasannaḥ prāha taṃ prahvaṃ prabhurgaṃbhīrayā girā || 10 ||

sanatkumāra uvāca |

satyaṃ vastu mune dadhyāḥ sākṣātkaraṇagocaraḥ |
sa śivothāsahāyotra tapaścarasi kiṃ kṛte || 11 ||

evamuktaḥ kumāreṇa provāca svāśayaṃ muniḥ |
dharmārthakāmamokṣāśca vedamārge kṛtādarāḥ || 12 ||

bahudhā sthāpitā loke mayā tvatkṛpayā tathā |
evaṃ bhutasya mepyevaṃ gurubhūtasya sarvataḥ || 13 ||

muktisādhanakaṃ jñānaṃ nodeti paramādbhutam |
tapaścarāmi muktyarthaṃ na jāne tatra kāraṇam || 14 ||

itthaṃ kumāro bhagavānvyāsena muninārthitaḥ |
samarthaḥ prāha vipreṃdrā niścayaṃ muktikāraṇam || 15 ||

śravaṇaṃ kīrtanaṃ śaṃbhormananaṃ ca mahattaram |
trayaṃ sādhanamuktaṃ ca vidyate vedasaṃmatam || 16 ||

purāhamatha saṃbhrānto hyanyasādhanasaṃbhramaḥ |
acale maṃdare śaile tapaścaraṇamācaram || 17 ||

śivājñayā tataḥ prāpto bhagavānnaṃdikeśvaraḥ |
sa me dayālurbhagavānsarvasākṣī gaṇeśvaraḥ || 18 ||

uvāca mahyaṃ sasnehaṃ muktisādhanamuttamam |
śravaṇaṃ kīrtanaṃ śaṃbhormananaṃ vedasaṃmatam || 19 ||

trikaṃ ca sādhanaṃ muktau śivena mama bhāṣitam |
śravaṇādiṃ trikaṃ brahmankuruṣveti muhurmuhuḥ || 20 ||

evamuktvā tato vyāsaṃ sānugo vidhinaṃdanaḥ |
jagāma svavimānena padaṃ paramaśobhanam || 21 ||

evamuktaṃ samāsena pūrvavṛttāntamuttamam |

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

śravaṇāditrayaṃ sūta muktyopāyastvayeritaḥ || 22 ||

śravaṇāditrike .aśaktaḥ kiṃ kṛtvā mucyate janaḥ |
ayatnenaiva muktiḥ syātkarmaṇā kena hetunā || 23 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe prathamāyāṃ vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyaṃ sādhyasādhanakhaṇḍe caturtho .adhyāyaḥ || 4 ||

sūta uvāca |

śravaṇāditrike .aśakto liṃgaṃ beraṃ ca śāṃkaram |
saṃsthāpya nityamabhyarcya taretsaṃsārasāgaram || 1 ||

api dravyaṃ vahedeva yathābalamavaṃcayan |
arpayelliṃgaberārthamarcayedapi santatam || 2 ||

maṃḍapaṃ gopuraṃ tīrthaṃ maṭhaṃ kṣetraṃ tathotsavam |
vastraṃ gaṃdhaṃ ca mālyaṃ ca dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ ca bhaktitaḥ || 3 ||

vividhānnaṃ ca naivedyamapūpavyaṃjanairyutam |
chatraṃ dhvajaṃ ca vyajanaṃ cāmaraṃ cāpi sāṃgakam || 4 ||

rājopacāravatsarvaṃ dhārayelliṃgaberayoḥ |
pradakṣiṇāṃ namaskāraṃ yathāśakti japaṃ tathā || 5 ||

āvāhanādisargāntaṃ nityaṃ kuryātsubhaktitaḥ |
itthamabhyarcya yandevaṃ liṃgebere ca śāṃkare || 6 ||

siddhimeti śivaprītyā hitvāpi śravaṇādikam |
liṃgaberārcanāmātrānmuktāḥ pūrve mahājanāḥ || 7 ||

manuya ūcuḥ |

beramātre tu sarvatra pūjyante devatāgaṇāḥ |
liṃgebere ca sarvatra kathaṃ saṃpūjyate śivaḥ || 8 ||

sūta uvāca |

aho munīśvarāḥ puṇyaṃ praśnametanmahādbhutam |
atra vaktā mahādevo nānyo .asti puruṣaḥ kvacit || 9 ||

śivenoktaṃ pravakṣyāmi kramādgurumukhācchrutam |
śivaiko brahmarūpatvānniṣkalaḥ parikīrtitaḥ || 10 ||

rūpitvātsakalastadvattasmātsakalaniṣkalaḥ |
niṣkalatvānnirākāraṃ liṃgaṃ tasya samāgatam || 11 ||

sakalatvāttathā beraṃ sākāraṃ tasya saṃgatam |
sakalākalarūpatvādbrahmaśabdābhidhaḥ paraḥ || 12 ||

api liṃge ca bere ca nityamabhyarcyate janaiḥ |
abrahmatvāttadanyeṣāṃ niṣkalatvaṃ na hi kvacit || 13 ||

tasmātte niṣkale liṃge nārādhyante sureśvarāḥ |
abrahmatvācca jīvatvāttathānye devatāgaṇāḥ || 14 ||

tūṣṇīṃ sakalamātratvādarcyante beramātrake |
jīvatvaṃ śaṃkarānyeṣāṃ brahmatvaṃ śaṃkarasya ca || 15 ||

vedāntasārasaṃsiddhaṃ praṇavārthe prakāśanāt |
evameva purā pṛṣṭo maṃdare naṃdikeśvaraḥ || 16 ||

sanatkumāramuninā brahmaputreṇa dhīmatā / |

sanatkumāra uvāca |

śivānyadevavaśyānāṃ sarveṣāmapi sarvataḥ || 17 ||

beramātraṃ ca pūjārthaṃ śrutaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ ca bhūriśaḥ |
śivamātrasya pūjāyāṃ liṃgaṃ beraṃ ca dṛśyate || 18 ||

atastadbrūhi kalyāṇa tattvaṃ me sādhubodhanam |

naṃdikeśvara uvāca |

anuttaramimaṃ praśnaṃ rahasyaṃ brahmalakṣaṇam || 19 ||

kathayāmi śivenoktaṃ bhaktiyuktasya te .anagha |
śivasya brahmarūpatvānniṣkalatvācca niṣkalam || 20 ||

liṃgaṃ tasyaiva pūjāyāṃ sarvavedeṣu saṃmatam |
tasyaiva sakalatvācca tathā sakalaniṣkalam || 21 ||

sakalaṃ ca tathā beraṃ pūjāyāṃ lokasaṃmatam |
śivānyeṣāṃ ca jīvatvātsakalatvācca sarvataḥ || 22 ||

beramātraṃ ca pūjāyāṃ saṃmataṃ vedanirṇaye |
svāvirbhāve ca devānāṃ sakalaṃ rūpameva hi || 23 ||

śivasya liṃgaṃ beraṃ ca darśane dṛśyate khalu |

sanatkumāra uvāca |

uktaṃ tvayā mahābhāga liṃgaberapracāraṇam || 24 ||

śivasya ca tadanyeṣāṃ vibhajya paramārthataḥ |
tasmāttadeva paramaṃ liṃgaberādisaṃbhavam || 25 ||

śrotumicchāmi yogīṃdra liṃgāvirbhāvalakṣaṇam |

naṃdikeśvara uvāca |

śṛṇu vatsa bhavatprītyā vakṣyāmi paramārthataḥ || 26 ||

purā kalpe mahākāle prapanne lokaviśrute |
āyudhyetāṃ mahātmānau brahmaviṣṇū parasparam || 27 ||

tayormānaṃ nirākartuṃ tanmadhye parameśvaraḥ |
niṣkalastaṃbharūpeṇa svarūpaṃ samadarśayat || 28 ||

tataḥ svaliṃgacihnatvātstaṃbhato niṣkalaṃ śivaḥ |
svaliṃgaṃ darśayāmāsa jagatāṃ hitakāmyayā || 29 ||

tadāprabhṛti lokeṣu niṣkalaṃ liṃgamaiśvaram |
sakalaṃ ca tathā beraṃ śivasyaiva prakalpitam || 30 ||

śivānyeṣaḥ tu devānāṃ beramātraṃ prakalpitam |
tattadberaṃ tu devānāṃ tattadbhogapradaṃ śubham |
śivasya liṃgaberatvaṃ bhogamokṣapradaṃ śubham || 31 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ paṃcamo .adhyāyaḥ || 5 ||

naṃdikeśvara uvāca |

purā kadācidyogīṃdra viṣṇurviṣadharāsanaḥ |
suṣvāpa parayā bhūtyā svānugairapi saṃvṛtaḥ || 1 ||

yadṛcchayā gatastatra brahmā brahmavidāṃvaraḥ |
apṛcchatpuṃḍarīkākṣaṃ śayanaṃ sarvasundaram || 2 ||

kastvaṃ puruṣavaccheṣe dṛṣṭvā māmapi dṛptavat |
uttiṣṭha vatsa māṃ paśya tava nāthamihāgatam || 3 ||

āgataṃ gurumārādhyaṃ dṛṣṭvā yo dṛptavaccaret |
drohiṇastasya mūḍhasya prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate || 4 ||

iti śrutvā vacaḥ kruddho bahiḥ śāntavadācarat |
svasti te svāgataṃ vatsa tiṣṭha pīṭhamito viśa || 5 ||

kimu te vyāgravadvaktraṃ vibhāti viṣamekṣaṇam |

brahmovāca |

vatsa viṣṇo mahāmānamāgataṃ kālavegataḥ || 6 ||

pitāmahaśca jagataḥ pātā ca tava vatsaka |

viṣṇuruvāca |

matsthaṃ jagadidaṃ vatsa manuṣe tvaṃ hi coravat || 7 ||

mannābhikamalājjātaḥ putrastvaṃ bhāṣase vṛthā |

naṃdikeśvara uvāca |

evaṃ hi vadatostatra mugdhayorajayostadā || 8 ||

ahameva baro na tvamahaṃ prabhurahaṃ prabhuḥ |
parasparaṃ hantukāmau cakratuḥ samarodyamam || 9 ||

yuyudhāte .amarau vīrau haṃsapakṣīṃdravāhanau |
vairaṃcyā vaiṣṇavāścaivaṃ mitho yuyudhire tadā || 10 ||

tāvadvimānagatayaḥ sarvā vai devajātayaḥ |
didṛkṣavaḥ samājagmuḥ samaraṃ taṃ mahādbhutam || 11 ||

kṣipantaḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi paśyantaḥ svairamaṃbare |
suparṇavāhanastatra kruddho vai brahmavakṣasi || 12 ||

mumoca bāṇānasahānastrāṃśca vividhānbahūn |
mumocā.atha vidhiḥ kruddho viṣṇorurasi duḥsahān || 13 ||

bāṇānanalasaṃkāśānastrāṃśca bahuśastadā |
tadāścaryamiti spaṣṭaṃ tayoḥ samaragocaram || 14 ||

samīkṣya daivatagaṇāḥ śaśaṃsurbhṛśamākulāḥ |
tato viṣṇuḥ susaṃkruddhaḥ śvasanvyasanakarśitaḥ || 15 ||

māheśvarāstraṃ matimān saṃdadhe brahmaṇopari |
tato brahmā bhṛśaṃ kruddhaḥ kaṃpayanviśvameva hi || 16 ||

astraṃ pāśupataṃ ghoraṃ saṃdadhe viṣṇuvakṣasi |
tatastadutthitaṃ vyomni tapanāyutasannibham || 17 ||

sahasramukhamatyugraṃ caṃḍavātabhayaṃkaram |
astradvayamidaṃ tatra brahmaviṣṇvorbhayaṃkaram || 18 ||

itthaṃ babhūva samaro brahmaviṣṇvoḥ parasparam |
tato devagaṇāḥ sarve viṣaṇṇā bhṛśamākulāḥ |
ūcuḥ parasparaṃ tāta rājakṣobhe yathā dvijāḥ || 19 ||

sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiśca saṃhārastiro bhāvopyanugrahaḥ |
yasmātpravartate tasmai brahmaṇe ca triśūline || 20 ||

aśakyamanyairyadanugrahaṃ vinā tṛṇakṣayopyatra yadṛcchayā kvacit |

iti devābhayaṃ kṛtvā vicinvantaḥ śivakṣayam |
jagmuḥ kailāsaśikharaṃ yatrāste caṃdraśekharaḥ || 22 ||

dṛṣṭvaivamamarā hṛṣṭāḥ padantatpārameśvaram |
praṇemuḥ praṇavākāraṃ praviṣṭāstatra sadmani || 23 ||

tepi tatra sabhāmadhye maṃḍape maṇiviṣṭare |
virājamānamumayā dadṛśurdevapuṃgavam || 24 ||

savyottaretarapadaṃ tadarhitakarāṃ bujam |
svagaṇaiḥ sarvato juṣṭaṃ sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam || 25 ||

vījyamānaṃ viśeṣajaiḥ strījanaistīvrabhāvanaiḥ |
śasyamānaṃ sadāvedairanugṛhṇantamīśvaram || 26 ||

dṛṣṭvaivamīśamamarāḥ santoṣasalilekṣaṇāḥ |
daṃḍavaddūrato vatsa namaścakrurmahāgaṇāḥ || 27 ||

tānavekṣya patirdevānsamīpe cāhvayadgaṇaiḥ |
atha saṃhlādayandevāndevo devaśikhāmaṇiḥ |
avocadarthagaṃbhīraṃ vacanaṃ madhumaṃgalam || 28 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ ṣaṣṭho .adhyāyaḥ || 6 ||

īśvara uvāca |

vatsakāḥ svastivaḥ kaccidvartate mama śāsanāt |
jagacca devatāvaṃśaḥ svasvakarmaṇi kiṃ navā || 1 ||

prāgeva viditaṃ yuddhaṃ brahmaviṣṇvormayāsurāḥ |
bhavatāmabhitāpena paunaruktyena bhāṣitam || 2 ||

iti sasmitayā mādhvyā kumāraparibhāṣayā |
samatoṣayadaṃbāyāḥ sa patistatsuravrajam || 3 ||

atha yuddhāṃgaṇaṃ gantuṃ haridhātroradhīśvaraḥ |
ājñāpayadgaṇeśānāṃ śataṃ tatraiva saṃsadi || 4 ||

tato vādyaṃ bahuvidhaṃ prayāṇāya pareśituḥ |
gaṇeśvarāśca saṃnaddhā nānāvāhanabhūṣaṇāḥ || 5 ||

praṇavākāramādyantaṃ paṃcamaṃḍalamaṃḍitam |
āruroha rathaṃ bhadramaṃbikāpatirīśvaraḥ |
sasūnugaṇamiṃdrādyāḥ sarvepyanuyayuḥ surāḥ || 6 ||

citradhvajavyajanacāmarapuṣpavarṣasaṃgatinṛtyanivahairapi vādyavargaiḥ |
saṃmānitaḥ paśupatiḥ parayā ca devyā sākaṃ tayoḥ samarabhūmimagātsasainyaḥ || 7 ||

samīkṣyaṃ tu tayoryuddhaṃ nigūḍho .abhraṃ samāsthitaḥ |
samāptavādyanirghoṣaḥ śāntorugaṇaniḥsvanaḥ || 8 ||

atha brahmācyutau vīrau hantukāmau parasparam |
māheśvareṇa cā.astreṇa tathā pāśupatena ca || 9 ||

astrajvālairatho dagdhaṃ brahmaviṣṇvorjagattrayam |
īśopi taṃ nirīkṣyātha hyakālapralayaṃ bhṛśam || 10 ||

mahānalastaṃbhavibhīṣaṇākṛtirbabhūva tanmadhyatale sa niṣkalaḥ |

te astre cāpi sajvāle lokasaṃharaṇakṣame |
nipatetuḥ kṣaṇe naiva hyāvirbhūte mahānale || 12 ||

dṛṣṭvā tadadbhutaṃ citramastraśāntikaraṃ śubham |
kimetadadbhutākāramityūcuśca parasparam || 13 ||

atīṃdriyamidaṃ staṃbhamagnirūpaṃ kimutthitam |
asyordhvamapi cādhaśca āvayorlakṣyameva hi || 14 ||

iti vyavasitau vīrau militau vīramāninau |
tatparau tatparīkṣārthaṃ pratasthāte .atha satvaram || 15 ||

āvayormiśrayostatra kāryamekaṃ na saṃbhavet |
ityuktvā sūkaratanurviṣṇustasyādimīyivān || 16 ||

tathā brahmāhaṃ satanustadantaṃ vīkṣituṃ yayau |
bhittvā pātālanilayaṃ gatvā dūrataraṃ hariḥ || 17 ||

nā.apśyāttasya saṃsthānaṃ staṃbhasyānalavarcasaḥ |
śrāntaḥ sa sūkarahariḥ prāpa pūrvaṃ raṇāṃgaṇam || 18 ||

atha gacchaṃstu vyomnā ca vidhistāta pitā tava |
dadarśa ketakī puṣpaṃ kiṃcidvicyutamadbhutam || 19 ||

atisaurabhyamamlānaṃ bahuvarṣacyutaṃ tathā |
anvīkṣya ca tayoḥ kṛtyaṃ bhagavānparameśvaraḥ || 20 ||

parihāsaṃ tu kṛtavānkaṃpanāccalitaṃ śiraḥ |
tasmāttāvanugṛhṇātuṃ cyutaṃ ketakamuttamam || 21 ||

kiṃ tvaṃ patasi puṣpeśa puṣparāṭ kena vā dhṛtam |
ādimasyāprameyasya staṃbhamadhyāccyutaściram || 22 ||

na saṃpaśyāmi tasmāttvaṃ jahyāśāmantadarśane |
asyāṃ tasya ca sevārthaṃ haṃsamūrtirihāgataḥ || 23 ||

itaḥ paraṃ sakhe me .adya tvayā kartavyamīpsitam |
mayā saha tvayā vācyametadviṣṇośca sannidhau || 24 ||

staṃbhānto vīkṣito dhātrā tatra sākṣyahamacyuta |
ityuktvā ketakaṃ tatra praṇanāma punaḥ naḥ |
asatyamapi śastaṃ syādāpadītyanuśāsanam || 25 ||

samīkṣya tatrā.acyutamāyataśramaṃ pranaṣṭaharṣaṃ tu nanarta harṣāt |
uvāca cainaṃ paramārthamacyutaṃ ṣaṃḍhāttavādaḥ sa vidhistato .acyutam || 26 ||

staṃbhāgrametatsamudīkṣitaṃ hare tatraiva sākṣī nanu ketakaṃ tvidam |
tato .avadattatra hi ketakaṃ mṛṣā tatheti taddhātṛvacastadantike || 27 ||

hariśca tatsatyamitīva ciṃtayaṃścakāra tasmai vidhaye namaḥ svayam |
ṣoḍaśairupacāraiśca pūjayāmāsa taṃ vidhim || 28 ||

vidhiṃ prahartuṃ śaṭhamagniliṃgataḥ sa īśvarastatra babhūva sākṛtiḥ |
samutthitaḥ svāmi vilokanātpunaḥ prakaṃpapāṇiḥ parigṛhya tatpadam || 29 ||

ādyantahīnavapuṣi tvayi mohabuddhyā bhūyādvimarśa iha nāvati kāmanotthaḥ |
sa tvaṃ prasīda karuṇākara kaśmalaṃ nau mṛṣṭaṃ kṣamasva vihitaṃ bhavataiva kelyā || 30 ||

īśvara uvāca |

vatsaprasanno .asmi hare yatastvamīśatvamicchannapi satyavākyam |
brūyāstataste bhavitā janeṣu sāmyaṃ mayā satkṛtirapyalapthāḥ || 31 ||

itaḥ paraṃ te pṛthagātmanaśca kṣetrapratiṣṭhotsavapūjanaṃ ca // 32 |

iti devaḥ purā prītaḥ satyena haraye param |
dadau svasāmyamatyarthaṃ devasaṃghe ca paśyati || 33 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ saptamo .adhyāyaḥ || 7 ||

naṃdikeśvara uvāca |

sasarjātha mahādevaḥ puruṣaṃ kaṃcidadbhutam |
bhairavākhyaṃ bhruvormadhyādbrahmadarpajighāṃsayā || 1 ||

sa vai tadā tatra patiṃ praṇamya śivamaṃgaṇe |
kiṃ kāryaṃ karavāṇyatra śīghramājñāpaya prabho || 2 ||

vatsayo .ayaṃ vidhiḥ sākṣājjagatāmādyadaivatam |
nūnamarcaya khaḍgena tigmena javasā param || 3 ||

sa vai gṛhītvaikakareṇa keśaṃ tatpaṃcamaṃ dṛptamasatyabhāṣaṇam |
chittvā śirāṃsyasya nihantumudyataḥ prakaṃpayankhaḍgamatisphuṭaṃ karaiḥ || 4 ||

pitā tavotsṛṣṭavibhūṣaṇāṃbarasraguttarīyāmalakeśasaṃhatiḥ |
pravātaraṃbheva lateva caṃcalaḥ papāta vai bhairavapādapaṃkaje || 5 ||

tāvadvidhiṃ tāta didṛkṣuracyutaḥ kṛpālurasmatpatipādapallavam |
niṣicya bāṣpairavadatkṛtāṃjaliryathā śiśuḥ svaṃ pitaraṃ kalākṣaram || 6 ||

acyuta uvāca |

tvayā prayatnena purā hi dattaṃ yadasya paṃcānanamīśacihnam |
tasmātkṣamasvādyamanugrahārhaṃ kuru prasādaṃ vidhaye hyamuṣmai || 7 ||

ityarthito .acyuteneśastuṣṭaḥ suragaṇāṃgaṇe |
nivartayāmāsa tadā bhairavaṃ brahmadaṃḍataḥ || 8 ||

athāha devaḥ kitavaṃ vidhiṃ vigatakaṃdharam |
brahmaṃstvamarhaṇākāṃkṣī śaṭhamīśatvamāsthitaḥ || 9 ||

nātaste satkṛtirloke bhūyātsthānotsavādikam |

brahmovaca

svāminprasīdādya mahāvibhūte manye varaṃ varada me śirasaḥ pramokṣam || 10 ||

namastubhyaṃ bhagavate baṃdhave viśvayonaye |
sahiṣṇave sarvadoṣāṇāṃ śaṃbhave śailadhanvane || 11 ||

īśvara uvāca |

arājabhayametadvai jagatsarvaṃ na śiṣyati |
tatastvaṃ jahi daṃḍārhaṃ vaha lokadhuraṃ śiśo || 12 ||

varaṃ dadāmi te tatra gṛhāṇa durlabhaṃ param |
vaitānikeṣu gṛhyeṣu yajñe ca bhavān guruḥ || 13 ||

niṣphalastvadṛte yajñaḥ sāṃgaśca sahadakṣiṇaḥ |
athāha devaḥ kitavaṃ ketakaṃ kūṭasākṣiṇam || 14 ||

re re ketaka duṣṭastvaṃ śaṭha dūramito vraja |
mamāpi prema te puṣpe mā bhūtpūjāsvitaḥ param || 15 ||

ityukte tatra devena ketakaṃ devajātayaḥ |
sarvāni vārayāmāsustatpārśvādanyatastadā || 16 ||

ketaka uvāca |

namaste nātha me janmaniṣphalaṃ bhavadājñayā |
saphalaṃ kriyatāṃ tāta kṣamyatāṃ mama kilbiṣam || 17 ||

jñānājñānakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ nāśayatyeva te smṛtiḥ |
tādṛśe tvayi dṛṣṭe me mithyādoṣaḥ kuto bhavet || 18 ||

tathā stutastu bhagavānketakena sabhātale |
na me tvaddhāraṇaṃ yogyaṃ satyavāgahamīśvaraḥ || 19 ||

madīyāstvāṃ dhariṣyanti janma te saphalaṃ tataḥ |
tvaṃ vai vitānavyājena mamopari bhaviṣyasi || 20 ||

ityanugṛhya bhagavānketakaṃ vidhimādhavau |
virarāja sabhāmadhye sarvadevairabhiṣṭutaḥ || 21 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāmaṣṭamo .adhyāyaḥ || 8 ||

naṃdikeśvara uvāca |

tatrāntare tau ca nāthaṃ praṇamya vidhimādhavau |
baddhāṃjalipuṭau tūṣṇīṃ tasthaturdakṣavāmagau || 1 ||

tatra saṃsthāpya tau devaṃ sakuṭuṃbaṃ varāsane |
pūjayāmāsatuḥ pūjyaṃ puṇyaiḥ puruṣavastubhiḥ || 2 ||

pauruṣaṃ prākṛtaṃ vastujñeyaṃ dīrghālpakālikam |
hāranūpurakeyūrakirīṭamaṇikuṃḍalaiḥ || 3 ||

yajñasūtrottarīyasrakkṣaumamālyāṃgulīyakaiḥ |
puṣpatāṃbūlakarpūracaṃdanāgurulepanaiḥ || 4 ||

dhūpadīpasitacchatravyajanadhvajacāmaraiḥ |
anyairdivyopahāraiśca vāṅmanotītavaibhavaiḥ || 5 ||

patiyogyaiḥ paśvalabhyaistau samarcayatāṃ patim |
yadyacchreṣṭhatamaṃ vastu patiyogyaṃ hitaddhvaje || 6 ||

tadvastvakhilamīśopi pāraṃ paryacikīrṣayā |
sabhyānāṃ pradadau hṛṣṭaḥ pṛthaktatra yathākramam || 7 ||

kolāhalo mahānāsīttatra tadvastu gṛhṇatām |
tatraiva brahmaviṣṇubhyāṃ cārcitaḥ śaṃkaraḥ purā || 8 ||

prasannaḥ prāha tau namrau sasmitaṃ bhaktivardhanaḥ |

īśvara uvāca |

tuṣṭo .ahamadya vāṃ vatsau pūjayā .asminmahādine || 9 ||

dinametattataḥ puṇyaṃ bhaviṣyati mahattaram |
śivarātririti khyātā tithireṣā mama priyā || 10 ||

etatkāle tu yaḥ kuryātpūjāṃ malliṃgaberayoḥ |
kuryāttu jagataḥ kṛtyaṃ sthitisargādikaṃ pumān || 11 ||

śivarātrāvahorātraṃ nirāhāro jiteṃdriyaḥ / |
arcayedvā yathānyāyaṃ yathābalamavaṃcakaḥ || 12 ||

yatphalaṃ mama pūjāyāṃ varṣamekaṃ nirantaram |
tatphalaṃ labhate sadyaḥ śivarātrau madarcanāt || 13 ||

maddharmavṛddhikālo .ayaṃ caṃdrakāla ivāṃbudheḥ |
pratiṣṭhādyutsavo yatra māmako maṃgalāyanaḥ || 14 ||

yatpunaḥ staṃbharūpeṇa svāvirāsamahaṃ purā |
sa kālo mārgaśīrṣe tu syādārdrā ṛkṣamarbhakau || 15 ||

ārdrāyāṃ mārgaśīrṣe tu yaḥ paśyenmāmumāsakham |
madberamapi vā liṃgaṃ sa guhādapi me priyaḥ || 16 ||

alaṃ darśanamātreṇa phalaṃ tasmindine śubhe |
abhyarcanaṃ cedadhikaṃ phalaṃ vācāmagocaram || 17 ||

raṇaraṃgatale .amuṣminyadahaṃ liṃgavarṣmaṇā |
jṛṃbhito liṃgavattasmālliṃgasthānamidaṃ bhavet || 18 ||

anādyantamidaṃ staṃbhamaṇumātraṃ bhaviṣyati |
darśanārthaṃ hi jagatāṃ pūjanārthaṃ hi putrako || 19 ||

bhogāvahamidaṃ liṃgaṃ bhuktiṃ muktyekasādhanam |
darśanasparśanadhyānājjantūnāṃ janmamocanam || 20 ||

analācalasaṃkāśaṃ yadidaṃ liṃgamutthitam |
aruṇācalamityeva tadidaṃ khyātimeṣyati || 21 ||

atra tīrthaṃ ca bahudhā bhaviṣyati mahattaram |
muktirapyatra jantūnāṃ vāsena maraṇena ca || 22 ||

rathotsavādikalyāṇaṃ janāvāsaṃ tu sarvataḥ |
atra dattaṃ hutaṃ japtaṃ sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet || 23 ||

matkṣetrādapi sarvasmātkṣetrametanmahattaram |
atra saṃsmṛtimātreṇa muktirbhavati dehinām || 24 ||

tasmānmahattaramidaṃ kṣetramatyantaśobhanam |
sarvakalyāṇasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvamuktikaraṃ śubham || 25 ||

arcayitvā .atra māmeva liṃge liṃginamīśvaram |
sālokyaṃ caiva sāmīpyaṃ sārūpyaṃ sārṣṭireva ca || 26 ||

sāyujyamiti paṃcaite kriyādīnāṃ phalaṃ matam |
sarvepi yūyaṃ sakalaṃ prāpsyathāśu manoratham || 27 ||

naṃdikeśvara uvāca |

ityanugṛhya bhagavānvinītau vidhimādhavau |
yatpūrvaṃ prahataṃ yuddhe tayoḥ sainyaṃ parasparam || 28 ||

tadutthāpayadatyarthaṃ svaśaktyā .amṛtadhārayā |
tayormauḍhyaṃ ca vairaṃ ca vyapanetumuvāca tau || 29 ||

sakalaṃ niṣkalaṃ ceti svarūpadvayamasti me |
nānyasya kasyacittasmādanyaḥ sarvopyanīśvaraḥ || 30 ||

purastātstaṃbharūpeṇa paścādrūpeṇa cārbhakau |
brahmatvaṃ niṣkalaṃ proktamīśatvaṃ sakalaṃ tathā || 31 ||

dvayaṃ mamaiva saṃsiddhaṃ na madanyasya kasyacit |
tasmādīśatvamanyeṣāṃ yuvayorapi na kvacit || 32 ||

tadajñānena vāṃ vṛttamīśamānaṃ mahādbhutam |
tannirākartumatraivamutthito .ahaṃ raṇakṣitau || 33 ||

tyajataṃ mānamātmīyaṃ mayīśe kurutaṃ matim |
matprasādena lokeṣu sarvopyarthaḥ prakāśate || 34 ||

gurūktirvyaṃjakaṃ tatra pramāṇaṃ vā punaḥ punaḥ |
brahmatattvamidaṃ gūḍhaṃ bhavatprītyā bhaṇāmyaham || 35 ||

ahameva paraṃ brahma matsvarūpaṃ kalākalam |
brahmatvādīśvaraścāhaṃ kṛtyaṃ menugrahādikam || 36 ||

bṛhattvādbṛṃhaṇatvācca brahmāhaṃ brahmakeśavau |
samatvādvyāpakatvācca tathaivātmāhamarbhakau || 37 ||

anātmānaḥ pare sarve jīvā eva na saṃśayaḥ |
anugrahādyaṃ sargāntaṃ jagatkṛtyaṃ ca paṃkajam || 38 ||

īśatvādeva me nityaṃ na madanyasya kasyacit |
ādau brahmattvabuddhyarthaṃ niṣkalaṃ liṃgamutthitam || 39 ||

tasmādajñātamīśatvaṃ vyaktaṃ dyotayituṃ hi vām |
sakalohamato jātaḥ sākṣādīśastu tatkṣaṇāt || 40 ||

sakalatvamato jñeyamīśatvaṃ mayi satvaram |
yadidaṃ niṣkalaṃ staṃbhaṃ mama brahmatvabodhakam || 41 ||

liṃgalakṣaṇayuktatvānmama liṃgaṃ bhavedidam |
tadidaṃ nityamabhyarcyaṃ yuvābhyāmatra putrakau || 42 ||

madātmakamidaṃ nityaṃ mama sānnidhyakāraṇam |
mahatpūjyamidaṃ nityamabhedālliṃgasiṃginoḥ || 43 ||

yatrapratiṣṭhitaṃ yena madīyaṃ liṃgamīdṛśam |
tatra pratiṣṭhitaḥ sohamapratiṣṭhopi vatsakau || 44 ||

matsāmyamekaliṃgasya sthāpane phalamīritam |
dvitīye sthāpite liṃge madaikyaṃ phalameva hi || 45 ||

liṃgaṃ prādhānyataḥ sthāpyaṃ tathāberaṃ tu gauṇakam |
liṃgābhāvena tatkṣetraṃ saberamapi sarvataḥ || 46 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ navamo .adhyāyaḥ || 9 ||

brahmaviṣṇū ūcatuḥ

sargādipaṃcakṛtyasya lakṣaṇaṃ brūhi nau prabho |

śiva uvāca |

matkṛtyabodhanaṃ guhyaṃ kṛpayā prabravīmi vām || 1 ||

sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiśca saṃhārastirobhāvo .apyanugrahaḥ |
paṃcaiva me jagatkṛtyaṃ nityasiddhamajācyutau || 2 ||

sargaḥ saṃsārasaṃraṃbhastatpratiṣṭhā sthitirmatā |
saṃhāro mardanaṃ tasya tirobhāvastadutkramaḥ || 3 ||

tanmokṣo .anugrahastanme kṛtyamevaṃ hi paṃcakam |
kṛtyametadvahatyanyastūṣṇīṃ gopurabiṃbavat || 4 ||

sargādi yaccatuṣkṛtyaṃ saṃsāraparijṛṃbhaṇam |
paṃcamaṃ muktiheturvai nityaṃ mayi ca susthiram || 5 ||

tadidaṃ paṃcabhūteṣu dṛśyate māmakairjanaiḥ |
sṛṣṭirbhūmau sthitistoye saṃhāraḥ pāvake tathā || 6 ||

tirobhāvo .anile tadvadanugraha ihāmbare |
sṛjyate dharayā sarvamadbhiḥ sarvaṃ pravarddhate || 7 ||

ardyate tejasā sarvaṃ vāyunā cāpanīyate |
vyomnānugṛhyate sarvaṃ jñeyamevaṃ hi sūribhiḥ || 8 ||

paṃcakṛtyamidaṃ boḍhuṃ mamāsti mukhapaṃcakam |
caturdikṣu caturvaktraṃ tanmadhye paṃcamaṃ mukham || 9 ||

yuvābhyāṃ tapasā labdhametatkṛtyadvayaṃ sutau |
sṛṣṭisthityabhidhaṃ bhāgyaṃ mattaḥ prītādatipriyam || 10 ||

tathā rudramaheśābhyāmanyatkṛtyadvayaṃ param |
anugrahākhyaṃ kenāpi labdhuṃ naiva hi śakyate || 11 ||

tatsarvaṃ paurvikaṃ karma yuvābhyāṃ kālavismṛtam |
na tadrudra maheśābhyāṃ vismṛtaṃ karma tādṛśam || 12 ||

rūpe veśe ca kṛtye ca vāhane cāsane tathā |
āyudhādau ca matsāmyamasmābhistatkṛte kṛtam || 13 ||

maddhyānavirahādvatsau mauḍhyaṃ vāmevamāgatam |
majjñāne sati naivaṃ syānmānaṃ rūpe maheśavat || 14 ||

tasmānmajjñānasiddhyarthaṃ mantramoṃkāranāmakam |
itaḥ paraṃ prajapataṃ māmakaṃ mānabhaṃjanam || 15 ||

upādiśaṃ nijaṃ mantramoṃkāramurumaṃgalam |
oṃkāro manmukhājjajñe prathamaṃ matprabodhakaḥ || 16 ||

vācako .ayamahaṃ vācyo mantro .ayaṃ hi madātmakaḥ |
tadanusmaraṇaṃ nityaṃ mamānusmaraṇaṃ bhavet || 17 ||

akāra uttarātpūrvamukāraḥ paścimānanāt |
makāro dakṣiṇamukhādbiṃduḥ prāṅmukhatastathā || 18 ||

nādo madhyamukhādevaṃ paṃcadhā .asau vijṛṃbhitaḥ |
ekībhūtaḥ punastadvadomityekākṣaro bhavet || 19 ||

nāmarūpātmakaṃ sarvaṃ vedabhūtakuladvayam |
vyāptametena mantreṇa śivaśaktyośca bodhakaḥ || 20 ||

asmātpaṃcākṣaraṃ jajñe bodhakaṃ sakalasyatat |
ākārādikrameṇaiva nakārādiyathākramam || 21 ||

asmātpaṃcākṣarājjātā mātṛkāḥ paṃcabhedataḥ |
tasmācchiraścaturvaktrāttripādgāya trireva hi || 22 ||

vedaḥ sarvastato jajñe tato vai mantrakoṭayaḥ |
tattanmantreṇa tatsiddhiḥ sarvasiddhirito bhavet || 23 ||

anena mantrakaṃdena bhogo mokṣaśca siddhyati |
sakalā mantrarājānaḥ sākṣādbhogapradāḥ śubhāḥ || 24 ||

naṃdikeśvara uvāca |

punastayostatra tiraḥ paṭaṃ guruḥ prakalpya mantraṃ ca samādiśatparam |
nidhāya tacchīrṣṇi karāṃbujaṃ śanairudaṅmukhaṃ saṃsthitayoḥ sahāṃbikaḥ || 25 ||

triruccāryāgrahīnmantraṃ yantratantroktipūrvakam |
śiṣyau ca tau dakṣiṇāyāmātmānaṃ ca samarpayat || 26 ||

prabaddhahastau kila tau tadantike tameva devaṃ jagaturjagadgurum // 27 |

brahmācyutāvūcatuḥ

namo niṣkalarūpāya namo niṣkalatejase |
namaḥ sakalanāthāya namaste sakalātmane || 28 ||

namaḥ praṇavavācyāya namaḥ praṇavaliṃgine |
namaḥ sṛṣṭyādikartre ca namaḥ paṃcamukhāyate || 29 ||

paṃcabrahmasvarūpāya paṃca kṛtyāyate namaḥ |
ātmane brahmaṇe tubhyamanantaguṇaśaktaye || 30 ||

sakalākalarūpāya śaṃbhave gurave namaḥ |
iti stutvā guruṃ padyairbrahmā viṣṇuśca nematuḥ || 31 ||

īśvara uvāca |

vatsakau sarvatattvaṃ ca kathitaṃ darśitaṃ ca vām |
japataṃ praṇavaṃ mantraṃ devīdiṣṭaṃ madātmakam || 32 ||

jñānaṃ ca susthiraṃ bhāgyaṃ sarvaṃ bhavati śāśvatam |
ārdrāyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ tajjāpyaṃ tvakṣayaṃ bhavet || 33 ||

sūryagatyā mahārdrāyāmekaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet |
mṛgaśīrṣāntimo bhāgaḥ punarvasvādimastathā || 34 ||

ārdrāsamaḥ sadā jñeyaḥ pūjāhomāditarpaṇe |
darśanaṃ tu prabhāte ca prātaḥsaṃgavakālayoḥ || 35 ||

caturdaśī tathā grāhyā niśīthavyāpinī bhavet |
pradoṣavyāpinī caiva parayuktā praśasyate || 36 ||

liṃgaṃ beraṃ ca metulyaṃ yajatāṃ liṃgamuttamam |
tasmālliṃgaṃ paraṃ pūjyaṃ berādapi mumukṣubhiḥ || 37 ||

liṃgamoṃkāramantreṇa beraṃ paṃcākṣareṇa tu |
svayameva hi saddravyaiḥ pratiṣṭhāpyaṃ parairapi || 38 ||

pūjayedupacāraiśca matpadaṃ sulabhaṃ bhavet |
iti śāsya tathā śiṣyau tatraivāṃ.atarhitaḥ śivaḥ || 39 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ daśamo .adhyāyaḥ || 10 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

kathaṃ liṃgaṃ pratiṣṭhāpyaṃ kathaṃ vātasya lakṣaṇam |
kathaṃ vā tatsamabhyarcyaṃ deśe kāle ca kena hi || 1 ||

sūta uvāca |

yuṣmadarthaṃ pravakṣyāmi buddhyatāmavadhānataḥ |
anukūle śubhe kāle puṇye tīrthe taṭe tathā || 2 ||

yatheṣṭaṃ liṃgamāropyaṃ yatra syānnityamarcanam |
pārthivena tathāpyenaṃ taijasena yathāruci || 3 ||

kalpalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ liṃgaṃ pūjāphalaṃ labhet |
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sadyaḥ pūjāphalapradam || 4 ||

care viśiṣyate sūkṣmaṃ sthāvare sthūlameva hi |
salakṣaṇaṃ sapīṭhaṃ ca sthāpayecchivanirmitam || 5 ||

maṃḍalaṃ caturasraṃ vā trikoṇamathavā tathā |
khaṭvāṃgavanmadhyasūkṣmaṃ liṃgapīṭhaṃ mahāphalaṃ || 6 ||

prathamaṃ mṛcchilādibhyo ligaṃ lohādibhiḥ kṛtam |
yena liṃgaṃ tena pīṭhaṃ sthāvare hi viśiṣyate || 7 ||

liṃgaṃ pīṭhaṃ care tvekaṃ liṃgaṃ bāṇakṛtaṃ vinā |
liṃgapramāṇaṃ kartṝṇāṃ dvādaśāṃgulamuttamam || 8 ||

nyūnaṃ cetphalamalpaṃ syādadhikaṃ naiva dūṣyate |
karturekāṃgulanyūnaṃ carepi ca tathaiva hi || 9 ||

ādau vimānaṃ śilpena kāryaṃ devagaṇairyutam |
tatra garbhagṛhe ramye dṛḍhe darpaṇasaṃnibhe || 10 ||

bhūṣite navaratnaiśca digdvāre ca pradhānakaiḥ |
nīlaṃ raktaṃ ca vai dūryaṃ śyāmaṃ mārakataṃ tathā || 11 ||

muktāpravālagomedavajrāṇi navaratnakam |
madhye liṃgaṃ mahaddravyaṃ nikṣipetsahavaidike || 12 ||

saṃpūjya liṃgaṃ sadyādyaiḥ paṃcasthāne yathākramam |
agnau ca hutvā bahudhā haviṣāsa kalaṃ ca mām || 13 ||

abhyarcya gurumācāryamarthaiḥ kāmaiśca bāṃdhavam |
dadyādaiśvaryamarthibhyo jaḍamapyajaḍaṃ tathā || 14 ||

sthāvaraṃ jaṃgamaṃ jīvaṃ sarvaṃ santoṣya yatnataḥ |
suvarṇapūrite śvabhre navaratnaiśca pūrite || 15 ||

sadyādi brahma coccārya dhyātvā devaṃ paraṃ śubham |
udīrya ca mahāmantramoṃkāraṃ nādaghoṣitam || 16 ||

liṃgaṃ tatra pratiṣṭhāpya ligaṃ pīṭhena yojayet |
liṃgaṃ sapīṭhaṃ nikṣipya nityalepena baṃdhayet || 17 ||

evaṃ beraṃ ca saṃsthāpyaṃ tatraiva paramaṃ śubham |
paṃcākṣareṇa beraṃ tu utsavārthaṃ vahistathā || 18 ||

beraṃ gurubhyo gṛhṇīyātsādhubhiḥ pūjitaṃ tu vā |
evaṃ liṃge ca bere ca pūjā śivapadapradā || 19 ||

punaśca dvividhaṃ proktaṃ sthāvaraṃ jaṃgamaṃ tathā |
sthāvaraṃ liṃgamityāhustarugulmādikaṃ tathā || 20 ||

jaṃgamaṃ liṃgamityāhuḥ kṛmikīṭādikaṃ tathā |
sthāvarasya ca śuśrūṣā jaṃgamasya ca tarpaṇam || 21 ||

tattatsukhānurāgeṇa śivapūjāṃ vidurbudhāḥ |
pīṭhamaṃbāmayaṃ sarvaṃ śivaliṃgaṃ ca cinmayam || 22 ||

yathā devīmumāmaṃke dhṛtvā tiṣṭhati śaṃkaraḥ |
tathā liṃgamidaṃ pīṭhaṃ dhṛtvā tiṣṭhati santatam || 23 ||

evaṃ sthāpya mahāliṃgaṃ pūjayedupacārakaiḥ |
nityapūjā yathā śaktidhvajādikaraṇaṃ tathā || 24 ||

iti saṃsthāpayelliṃgaṃ sākṣācchivapadapradam |
athavā caraliṃgaṃ tu ṣoḍaśairupacārakaiḥ || 25 ||

pūjayecca yathānyāyaṃ kramācchivapadapradam |
āvāhanaṃ cāsanaṃ ca arghyaṃ pādyaṃ tathaiva ca || 26 ||

tadaṃgācamanaṃ caiva snānamabhyaṃgapūrvakam |
vastraṃ gaṃdhaṃ tathā puṣpaṃ dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ nivedanam || 27 ||

nīrājanaṃ ca tāṃbūlaṃ namaskāro visarjanam |
athavā .arghyādikaṃ kṛtvā naivedyāṃ taṃ yathāvidhi || 28 ||

athābhiṣekaṃ naivedyaṃ namaskāraṃ ca tarpaṇam |
yathāśakti sadākuryātkramācchivapadapradam || 29 ||

athavā mānuṣe liṃgepyārṣe daive svayaṃbhuvi |
sthāpite .apūrvake liṃge sopacāraṃ yathā tathā || 30 ||

pūjopakaraṇe datte yatkiṃcitphalamaśnute |
pradakṣiṇānamaskāraiḥ kramācchivapadapradam || 31 ||

liṃgaṃ darśanamātraṃ vā niyamena śivapradam |
mṛtpiṣṭagośakṛtpuṣpaiḥ karavīreṇa vā phalaiḥ || 32 ||

guḍena navanītena bhasmanānnairyathāruci |
liṃgaṃ yatnena kṛtvānte yajettadanusārataḥ || 33 ||

aṃguṣṭhādāvapi tathā pūjāmicchanti kecana |
liṃgakarmaṇi sarvatra niṣedhosti na karhicit || 34 ||

sarvatra phaladātā hi prayāsānuguṇaṃ śivaḥ |
athavā liṃgadānaṃ vā liṃgamaulyamathāpi vā || 35 ||

śraddhayā śivabhaktāya dattaṃ śivapadapradam |
athavā praṇavaṃ nityaṃ japeddaśasahasrakam || 36 ||

saṃdhyayośca sahasraṃ vā jñeyaṃ śivapadapradam |
japakāle makārāntaṃ manaḥśuddhikaraṃ bhajet || 37 ||

samādhau mānasaṃ proktamupāṃśu sārvakālikam |
samānapraṇavaṃ cemaṃ biṃdunādayutaṃ viduḥ || 38 ||

atha paṃcākṣaraṃ nityaṃ japedayutamādarāt |
saṃdhyayośca sahasraṃ vā jñeyaṃ śivapadapradam || 39 ||

praṇavenādisaṃyuktaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ viśiṣyate |
dīkṣāyuktaṃ gurorgrāhyaṃ mantraṃ hyatha phalāptaye || 40 ||

kuṃbhasnānaṃ mantradīkṣāṃ mātṛkānyāsameva ca |
brāhmaṇaḥ satyapūtātmā gururjñānī viśiṣyate || 41 ||

dvijānāṃ ca namaḥpūrvamanyeṣāṃ ca namontakam |
strīṇāṃ ca kvacidicchanti namo taṃ ca yathāvidhi || 42 ||

viprastrīṇāṃ namaḥ pūrvamidamicchanti kecana |
paṃcakoṭijapaṃ kṛtvā sadā śivasamo bhavet || 43 ||

ekadvitricatuḥkoṭyābrahmādīnāṃ padaṃ vrajet |
japedakṣaralakṣaṃvā akṣarāṇāṃ pṛthakpṛthak || 44 ||

athavākṣaralakṣaṃ vā jñeyaṃ śivapadapradam |
sahasraṃ tu sahasrāṇāṃ sahasreṇa dinena hi || 45 ||

japenmantrādiṣṭasiddhirnityaṃ brāhmaṇabhojanāt |
aṣṭottarasahasraṃ vai gāyatrīṃ prātareva hi || 46 ||

brāhmaṇastu japennityaṃ kramācchivapadapradān |
vedamantrāṃstu sūktāni japenniyamamāsthitaḥ || 47 ||

ekaṃ daśārṇaṃ mantraṃ ca śatonaṃ ca tadūrdhvakam |
ayutaṃ ca sahasraṃ ca śatamekaṃ vinā bhavet || 48 ||

vedapārāyaṇaṃ caiva jñeyaṃ śivapadapradam |
anyānbahutarānmantrāñjapedakṣaralakṣataḥ || 49 ||

ekākṣarāṃstathā mantrāñjapedakṣarakoṭitaḥ |
tataḥ paraṃ japeccaiva sahasraṃ bhaktipūrvakam || 50 ||

evaṃ kuryādyathāśakti kramācchiva padaṃ labhet |
nityaṃ rucikaraṃ tvekaṃ mantramāmaraṇāntikam || 51 ||

japetsahasramomiti sarvābhīṣṭaṃ śivājñayā |
puṣpārāmādikaṃ vāpi tathā saṃmārjanādikam || 52 ||

śivāya śivakāryāthe kṛtvā śivapadaṃ labhet |
śivakṣetre tathā vāsaṃ nityaṃ kuryācca bhaktitaḥ || 53 ||

jaḍānāmajaḍānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ bhuktimuktidam |
tasmādvāsaṃ śivakṣetre kuryadāmaraṇaṃ budhaḥ || 54 ||

liṃgāddhastaśataṃ puṇyaṃ kṣetre mānuṣake viduḥ |
sahasrāratnimātraṃ tu puṇyakṣetre tathārṣake || 55 ||

daivaliṃge tathā jñeyaṃ sahasrāratnimānataḥ |
dhanuṣpramāṇasāhasraṃ puṇyaṃ kṣetre svayaṃ bhuvi || 56 ||

puṇyakṣetre sthitā vāpī kūpādyaṃ puṣkarāṇi ca |
śivagaṃgeti vijñeyaṃ śivasya vacanaṃ yathā || 57 ||

tatra snātvā tathā dattvā japitvā hi śivaṃ vrajet |
śivakṣetraṃ samāśritya vasedāmaraṇaṃ tathā || 58 ||

dāhaṃ daśāhaṃ māsyaṃ vā sapiṃḍīkaraṇaṃ tu vā |
ābdikaṃ vā śivakṣetre kṣetre piṃḍamathāpi vā || 59 ||

sarvapāpa vinirmuktaḥ sadyaḥ śivapadaṃ labhet |
athavā saptarātraṃ vā vasedvā paṃcarātrakam || 60 ||

trirātramekarātraṃ vā kramācchivapadaṃ labhet |
svavarṇānuguṇaṃ loke svācārātprāpnute naraḥ || 61 ||

varṇoddhāreṇa bhaktyā ca tatphalātiśayaṃ naraḥ |
sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ kāmanayā sadyaḥ phalamavāpnuyāt || 62 ||

sarvaṃ kṛtamakāmena sākṣācchivapadapradam |
prātarmadhyāhnasāyāhnamahastriṣvekataḥ kramāt || 63 ||

prātarvidhikaraṃ jñeyaṃ madhyāhnaṃ kāmikaṃ tathā |
sāyāhnaṃ śāntikaṃ jñeyaṃ rātrāvapi tathaiva hi || 64 ||

kālo niśītho vai proktomadhyayāmadvayaṃ niśi |
śivapūjā viśeṣeṇa tatkāle .abhīṣṭasiddhidā || 65 ||

evaṃ jñātvā naraḥ kurvanyathoktaphalabhāgbhavet |
kalau yuge viśeṣeṇa phalasiddhistu karmaṇā || 66 ||

uktena kenacidvāpi adhikāravibhedataḥ |
sadvṛttiḥ pāpabhīruścettatatphalamavāpnuyāt || 67 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

atha kṣetrāṇi puṇyāni samāsātkathayasva naḥ |
sarvāḥ striyaśca puruṣā yānyāśritya padaṃ labhet || 68 ||

sūta yogivaraśreṣṭha śivakṣetrāgamāṃstathā |

sūta uvāca |

śṛṇuta śraddhayā sarvakṣetrāṇi ca tadāgamān || 69 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃekadaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 11 ||

sūta uvāca |

śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ prājñāḥ śivakṣetraṃ vimuktidam |
tadāgamāṃstato vakṣye lokarakṣārthameva hi || 1 ||

paṃcāśatkoṭivistīrṇā saśailavanakānanā |
śivājñayā hi pṛthivī lokaṃ dhṛtvā ca tiṣṭhati || 2 ||

tatra tatra śivakṣetraṃ tatra tatra nivāsinām |
mookṣārthaṃ kṛpayā devaḥ kṣetraṃ kalpitavānprabhuḥ || 3 ||

parigrahādṛṣīṇāṃ ca devānāṃ parigrahāt |
svayaṃbhūtānyathānyāni lokarakṣārthameva hi || 4 ||

tīrthe kṣetre sadākāryaṃ snānadānajapādikam |
anyathā rogadāridryamūkatvādyāpnuyānnaraḥ || 5 ||

athāsminbhārate varṣe prāpnoti maraṇaṃ naraḥ |
svayaṃbhūsthānavāsena punarmānuṣyamāpnuyāt || 6 ||

kṣetre pāpasya karaṇaṃ dṛḍhaṃ bhavati bhūsurāḥ |
puṇyakṣetre nivāse hi pāpamaṇvapi nācaret || 7 ||

yena kenāpyupāyena puṇyakṣetre vasennaraḥ |
siṃdhoḥ śatanadītīre santi kṣetrāṇyanekaśaḥ || 8 ||

sarasvatī nadī puṇyā proktā ṣaṣṭimukhā tathā |
tattattīre vasetprājñaḥ kramādbrahmapadaṃ labhet || 9 ||

himavadgirijā gaṃgā puṇyā śatamukhā nadī |
tattīre caiva kāśyādipuṇyakṣetrāṇyanekaśaḥ || 10 ||

tatra tīraṃ praśastaṃ hi mṛge mṛgabṛhaspatau |
śoṇabhadro daśamukhaḥ puṇyobhīṣṭaphalapradaḥ || 11 ||

tatra snānopavāsena padaṃ vaināyakaṃ labhet |
caturvīṃśamukhā puṇyā narmadā ca mahānadī || 12 ||

tasyāṃ snānena vāsena padaṃ vaiṣṇavamāpnuyāt |
tamasā dvādaśamukhā revā daśamukhā nadī || 13 ||

godāvarī mahāpuṇyā brahmagovadhanāśinī |
ekaviṃśamukhā proktā rudralokapradāyinī || 14 ||

kṛṣṇaveṇī puṇyanadī sarvapāpakṣayāvahā |
sāṣṭādaśamukhāproktā viṣṇulokapradāyinī || 15 ||

tuṃgabhadrā daśamukhā brahmalokapradāyinī |
suvarṇamukharī puṇyā proktā navamukhā tathā || 16 ||

tatraiva suprajāyante brahmalokacyutāstathā |
sarasvatī ca paṃpā ca kanyāśvetanadī śubhā || 17 ||

etāsāṃ tīravāsena iṃdralokamavāpnuyāt |
sahyādrijā mahāpuṇyā kāverīti mahānadī || 18 ||

saptaviṃśamukhā proktā sarvābhīṣṭaṃ pradāyinī |
tattīrāḥ svargadāścaiva brahmaviṣṇupadapradāḥ || 19 ||

śivalokapradā śaivāstathā .abhīṣṭaphalapradāḥ |
naimiṣe badare snāyānmeṣage ca gurau ravau || 20 ||

brahmalokapradaṃ vidyāttataḥ pūjādikaṃ tathā |
siṃdhunadyāṃ tathā snānaṃ siṃhe karkaṭage ravau || 21 ||

kedārodakapānaṃ ca snānaṃ ca jñānadaṃ viduḥ |
godāvaryāṃ siṃhamāse snāyātsiṃhabṛhaspatau || 22 ||

śivalokapradamiti śivenoktaṃ tathā purā |
yamunāśoṇayoḥ snāyādgurau kanyāgate ravau || 23 ||

dharmaloke dantiloke mahābhogapradaṃ viduḥ |
kāveryāṃ ca tathāsnāyāttulāge tu ravau gurau || 24 ||

viṣṇorvacanamāhātmyātsarvābhīṣṭapradaṃ viduḥ |
vṛścike māsi saṃprāpte tathārke guruvṛścike || 25 ||

narmadāyāṃ nadīsnānādviṣṇulokamavāpnuyāt |
suvarṇamukharīsnānaṃ cāpage ca gurau ravau || 26 ||

śivalokapradamiti brāhmaṇo vacanaṃ yathā |
mṛgamāsi tathā snāyājjāhnavyāṃ mṛgage gurau || 27 ||

śivalokapradamiti brahmaṇo vacanaṃ yathā |
brahmaviṣṇvoḥ pade bhuktvā tadante jñānamāpnuyāt || 28 ||

gaṃgāyāṃ māghamāse tu tathākuṃbhagate ravau |
śrāddhaṃ vā piṃḍadānaṃ vā tilodakamathāpivā || 29 ||

vaṃśadvayapitṝṇāṃ ca kulakoṭyuddharaṃ viduḥ |
kṛṣṇaveṇyāṃ praśaṃsanti mīnage ca gurau ravau || 30 ||

tattattīrthe ca tanmāsi snānamiṃdrapadapradam |
gaṃgāṃ vā sahyajāṃ vāpi samāśritya vasedbudhaḥ || 31 ||

tatkālakṛtapāpasya kṣayo bhavati niścitam |
rudralokapradānyeva santi kṣetrāṇyanekaśaḥ || 32 ||

tāmraparṇī vegavatī brahmalokaphalaprade |
tayostīre hi santyeva kṣetrāṇi svargadāni ca || 33 ||

santi kṣetrāṇi tanmadhye puṇyadāni ca bhūriśaḥ |
tatra tatra vasanprājñastādṛśaṃ ca phalaṃ labhet || 34 ||

sadācāreṇa sadvṛttyā sadā bhāvanayāpi ca |
vaseddayāluḥ prājño vai nānyathā tatphalaṃ labhet || 35 ||

puṇyakṣetre kṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ bahudhā ṛddhimṛcchati |
puṇyakṣetre kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ mahadaṇvapi jāyate || 36 ||

tatkālaṃ jīvanārthaścetpuṇyena kṣayameṣyati |
puṇyamaiśvaryadaṃ prāhuḥ kāyikaṃ vācikaṃ tathā || 37 ||

mānasaṃ ca tathā pāpaṃ tādṛśaṃ nāśayeddvijāḥ |
mānasaṃ vajralepaṃ tu kalpakalpānugaṃ tathā || 38 ||

dhyānādeva hi tannaśyennānyathā nāśamṛcchati |
vācikaṃ japajālena kāyikaṃ kāyaśoṣaṇāt || 39 ||

dānāddhanakṛtaṃ naśyennā .anyathākalpakoṭibhiḥ |
kvacitpāpena puṇyaṃ ca vṛddhipūrveṇa naśyati || 40 ||

bījāṃśaścaiva vṛddhyaṃśo bhogāṃśaḥ puṇyapāpayoḥ |
jñānanāśyo hi bījāṃśo vṛddhiruktaprakārataḥ || 41 ||

bhogāṃśo bhoganāśyastu nānyathā puṇyakoṭibhiḥ |
bījaprarohe naṣṭe tu śeṣo bhogāya kalpate || 42 ||

devānāṃ pūjayā caiva brahmaṇānāṃ ca dānataḥ |
tapodhikyācca kālena bhogaḥ sahyo bhavennṛṇām |
tasmātpāpamakṛtvaiva vastavyaṃ sukhamicchatā || 43 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ dvādaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 12 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

sadācāraṃ śrāvayāśu yena lokāñjayedbudhaḥ |
dharmādharmamayānbrūhi svarganārakadāṃstathā || 1 ||

sūta uvāca |

sadācārayuto vidvānbrāhmaṇo nāma nāmataḥ |
vedācārayuto vipro hyetairekaikavāndvijaḥ || 2 ||

alpācārolpavedaśca kṣatriyo rājasevakaḥ |
kiṃcidācāravānvaiśyaḥ kṛṣivāṇijyakṛttayā || 3 ||

śūdrabrāhmaṇa ityuktaḥ svayameva hi karṣakaḥ |
asūyāluḥ paradrohī caṃḍāladvija ucyate || 4 ||

pṛthivīpālako rājā itarekṣatriyā matāḥ |
dhānyādikrayavānvaiśya itaro vaṇigucyate || 5 ||

brahmakṣatriyavaiśyānāṃ śuśrūṣuḥ śūdra ucyate |
karṣako vṛṣalo jñeya itare caiva dasyavaḥ || 6 ||

sarvo hyuṣaḥprācīmukhaścintayeddevapūrvakān |
dharmānarthāṃśca tatkleśānāyaṃ ca vyayameva ca || 7 ||

āyurdveṣaśca maraṇaṃ pāpaṃ bhāgyaṃ tathaiva ca |
vyādhiḥ puṣṭistathā śaktiḥ prātarutthānadikphalam || 8 ||

niśāntyāyāmoṣā jñeyā yāmārdhaṃ saṃdhirucyate |
tatkāle tu samutthāya viṇmūtre visṛjeddvijaḥ || 9 ||

gṛhāddūraṃ tato gatvā bāhyataḥ pravṛtastathā |
udaṅmukhaḥ samāviśya pratibaṃdhe .anyadiṅmukhaḥ || 10 ||

jalāgnibrāhmaṇādīnāṃ devānāṃ nābhimukhyataḥ |
liṃgaṃ pidhāya vāmena mukhamanyena pāṇinā || 11 ||

malamutsṛjya cotthāya na paśyeccaiva tanmalam |
uddhṛtena jalenaiva śaucaṃ kuryājjalādbahiḥ || 12 ||

athavā devapitrārṣatīrthāvataraṇaṃ vinā |
sapta vā paṃca vā trīnvā gudaṃ saṃśodhayenmṛdā || 13 ||

liṃge karkoṭamātraṃ tu gude prasṛtiriṣyate |
tata utthāya paddhastaśaucaṃ gaṇḍūṣamaṣṭakam || 14 ||

yena kena ca patreṇa kāṣṭhena ca jalādbahiḥ |
kāryaṃ santyajya tarjjanīṃ dantadhāvanamīritam || 15 ||

jaladevānnamaskṛtya mantreṇa snānamācaret |
aśaktaḥ kaṃṭhadaghnaṃ vā kaṭidaghnamathāpi vā || 16 ||

ājānu jalamāviśya mantrasnānaṃ samācaret |
devādīṃstarpayedvidvāṃstatra tīrthajalena ca || 17 ||

dhautavastraṃ samādāya paṃcakacchena dhārayet |
uttarīyaṃ ca kiṃ caiva dhāryaṃ sarveṣu karmasu || 18 ||

nadyāditīrthasnāne tu snānavastraṃ na śodhayet |
vāpīkūpagṛhādau tu snānādūrdhvaṃ nayedbudhaḥ || 19 ||

śilādārvādike vāpi jale vāpi sthalepi vā |
saṃśodhya pīḍayedvastraṃ pitṝṇāṃ tṛptaye dvijāḥ || 20 ||

jābālakoktamantreṇa bhasmanā ca tripuṃḍrakam |
anyathā cejjale pāta itastannarakamṛcchati || 21 ||

āpohiṣṭheti śirasi prokṣayetpāpaśāntaye |
yasyeti mantraṃ pāde tu saṃdhiprokṣaṇamucyate || 22 ||

pāde mūrdhni hṛdi caiva mūrdhni hṛtpāda eva ca |
hṛtpādamūrdhni saṃprokṣya mantrasnānaṃ vidurbudhāḥ || 23 ||

īṣatsparśe ca dauḥ svāsthye rājarāṣṭrabhaye .api ca |
atyāgatikāle ca mantrasnānaṃ samācaret || 24 ||

prātaḥ sūryānuvākena sāyamagnyanuvākataḥ |
apaḥ pītvā tathāmadhye punaḥ prokṣaṇamācaret || 25 ||

gāyatryā japamantrānte trirūrdhvaṃ prāgvinikṣipet |
mantreṇa saha caikaṃ vai madhye .arghyaṃ tu raverdvijā || 26 ||

atha jāte ca sāyāhne bhuvi paścimadiṅmukhaḥ |
uddhṛtya dadyātprātastu madhyāhneṃgulibhistathā || 27 ||

aṃgulīnāṃ ca raṃdhreṇa laṃbaṃ paśyeddivākaram |
ātmapradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā śuddhācamanamācaret || 28 ||

sāyaṃ muhūrtādarvāktu kṛtā saṃdhyā vṛthā bhavet |
akālātkāla ityukto dine .atīte yathākramam || 29 ||

divā .atīte ca gāyatrīṃ śataṃ nitye kramājjapet |
ādarśāhātparā.atīte gāyatrīṃ lakṣamabhyaset || 30 ||

māsātīte tu nitye hi punaścopanayaṃ caret |
īśo gaurīguho viṣṇurbrahmā ceṃdraśca vai yamaḥ || 31 ||

evaṃ rūpāṃśca vai devāṃstarpayedarthasiddhaye |
brahmārpaṇaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā śuddhācamanamācaret || 32 ||

tīrthadakṣiṇataḥ śaste maṭhe mantrālaye budhaḥ |
tatra devālaye vāpi gṛhe vā niyatasthale || 33 ||

sarvāndevānnamaskṛtya sthirabuddhiḥ sthirāsanaḥ |
praṇavaṃ pūrvamabhyasya gāyatrīmabhyasettataḥ || 34 ||

jīvabrahmaikyaviṣayaṃ buddhvā praṇavamabhyaset |
trailokyasṛṣṭikarttāraṃ sthitikartāramacyutam || 35 ||

saṃhartāraṃ tathā rudraṃ svaprakāśamupāsmahe |
jñānakarmeṃdriyāṇāṃ ca manovṛttīrdhiyastathā || 36 ||

bhogamokṣaprade dharme jñāne ca prerayetsadā |
itthamarthaṃ dhiyādhyāyanbrahmaprāpnoti niścayaḥ || 37 ||

kevalaṃ vā japennityaṃ brāhmaṇyasya ca pūrtaye |
sahasramabhyasennityaṃ prātarbrāhmaṇapuṃgavaḥ || 38 ||

anyeṣāṃ ca yathā śaktimadhyāhne ca śataṃ japet |
sāyaṃ dvidaśakaṃ jñeyaṃ śikhāṣṭakasamanvitam || 39 ||

mūlādhāraṃ samārabhya dvādaśāntasthitāṃstathā |
vidyeśabrahmaviṣṇvīśajīvātmaparameśvarān || 40 ||

brahmabuddhyā tadaikyaṃ ca sohaṃ bhāvanayā japet |
tāneva brahmaraṃdhrādau kāyādbāhye ca bhāvayet || 41 ||

mahattattvaṃ samārabhya śarīraṃ tu sahasrakam |
ekaikasmājjapādekamatikramya śanaiḥ śanaiḥ || 42 ||

parasminyojayejjīvaṃ japatattvamudāhṛtam |
śatadvidaśakaṃ dehaṃ śikhāṣṭakasamanvitam || 43 ||

mantrāṇāṃ japa evaṃ hi japamādikramādviduḥ |
sahasraṃ brāhmadaṃ vidyācchatamaiṃdrapradaṃ viduḥ || 44 ||

itarattvātmarakṣārthaṃ brahmayoniṣu jāyate |
divākaramupasthāya nityamitthaṃ samācaret || 45 ||

lakṣadvādaśayuktastu pūrṇabrāhmaṇa īritaḥ |
gāyatryā lakṣahīnaṃ tu vedakāryena yojayet || 46 ||

āsaptatestu niyamaṃ paścātpravrājanaṃ caret |
prātardvādaśasāhasraṃ pravrājīpraṇavaṃ japet || 47 ||

dine dine tvatikrānte nityamevaṃ kramājjapet |
māsādau kramaśo .atīte sārdhalakṣajapena hi || 48 ||

ata ūrdhvamatikrānte punaḥ praiṣaṃ samācaret |
evaṃ kṛtvā doṣaśāntiranyathā rauravaṃ vrajet || 49 ||

dharmārthayostato yatnaṃ kuryātkāmī na cetaraḥ |
brāhmaṇo muktikāmaḥ syādbrahmajñānaṃ sadābhyaset || 50 ||

dharmādartho .arthato bhogo bhogādvairāgyasaṃbhavaḥ |
dharmārjitārthabhogena vairāgyamupajāyate || 51 ||

viparītārthabhogena rāga eva prajāyate |
dharmaśca dvividhaḥ prokto dravyadehadvayena ca || 52 ||

dravyamijyādirūpaṃ syāttīrthasnānādi daihikam |
dhanena dhanamāpnoti tapasā divyarūpatām || 53 ||

niṣkāmaḥ śuddhimāpnoti śuddhyā jñānaṃ na saṃśayaḥ |
kṛtādau hi tapaḥśloghyaṃ dravyadharmaḥ kalau yuge || 54 ||

kṛtedhyānājjñānasiddhistretāyāṃ tapasā tathā |
dvāpare yajanājjñānaṃ pratimāpūjayā kalau || 55 ||

yādṛśaṃ puṇyaṃ pāpaṃ vā tādṛśaṃ phalameva hi |
dravyadehāṃgabhedena nyūnavṛddhikṣayādikam || 56 ||

adharmo hiṃsikārūpo dharmastu sukharūpakaḥ |
adharmādduḥkhamāpnoti dharmādvai sukhamedhate || 57 ||

vidyādurvṛttito duḥkhaṃ sukhaṃ vidyātsuvṛttitaḥ |
dharmārjanamataḥ kuryādbhogamokṣaprasiddhaye || 58 ||

sakuṭuṃbasya viprasya caturjanayutasya ca |
śatavarṣasya vṛttiṃ tu dadyāttadbrahmalokadam || 59 ||

cāṃdrāyaṇasahasraṃ tu brahmalokapradaṃ viduḥ |
sahasrasya kuṭuṃbasya pratiṣṭhāṃ kṣatriyaścaret || 60 ||

iṃdralokapradaṃ vidyādayutaṃ brahmalokadam |
yāṃ devatāṃ puraskṛtya dānamācarate naraḥ || 61 ||

tattallokamavāpnoti iti vedavido viduḥ |
arthahīnaḥ sadā kuryāttapasā mārjanaṃ tathā || 62 ||

tīrthācca tapasā prāpyaṃ sukhamakṣayyamaśnute |
arthārjanamatho vakṣye nyāyataḥ susamāhitaḥ || 63 ||

kṛtātpratigrahāccaiva yājanācca viśuddhitaḥ |
adainyādanatikleśādbrāhmaṇo dhanamarjayet || 64 ||

kṣatriyo bāhuvīryeṇa kṛṣigorakṣaṇādviśaḥ |
nyāyārjitasya vittasya dānātsiddhiṃ samaśnute || 65 ||

jñānasiddhyā mokṣasiddhiḥ sarveṣāṃ gurvanugrahāt |
mokṣātsvarūpasiddhiḥ syātparānandaṃ samaśnute || 66 ||

satsaṃgātsarvametadvai narāṇāṃ jāyate dvijāḥ |
dhanadhānyādikaṃ sarvaṃ deyaṃ vai gṛhamedhinā || 67 ||

yadyatkāle vastujātaṃ phalaṃ vā dhānyameva ca |
tattatsarvaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo deyaṃ vai hitamicchatā || 68 ||

jalaṃ caiva sadā deyamannaṃ kṣudvyādhiśāntaye |
kṣetraṃ dhānyaṃ tathā.a.amānnamannamevaṃ caturvidham || 69 ||

yāvatkālaṃ yadannaṃ vai bhuktvā śravaṇamedhate |
tāvatkṛtasya puṇyasya tvardhaṃ dāturna saṃśayaḥ || 70 ||

grahītāhigṛhītasya dānādvai tapasā tathā |
pāpasaṃśodhanaṃ kuryādanyathā rauravaṃ vrajet || 71 ||

ātmavittaṃ tridhā kuryāddharmavṛddhyātmabhogataḥ |
nityaṃ naimittakaṃ kāmyaṃ karma kuryāttu dharmataḥ || 72 ||

vittasya vardhanaṃ kuryādvṛddhyaṃśena hi sādhakaḥ |
hitena mitame dhyena bhogaṃ bhogāṃśataścaret || 73 ||

kṛṣyarjite daśāṃśaṃ hi deyaṃ pāpasya śuddhaye |
śeṣeṇa kuryāddharmādi anyathā rauravaṃ vrajet || 74 ||

athavā pāpabuddhiḥ syātkṣayaṃ vā satyameṣyati |
vṛddhivāṇijyake deyaṣṣaḍaṃśo hi vicakṣaṇaiḥ || 75 ||

śuddhapratigrahe deyaścaturthāṃśo dvijottamaiḥ |
akasmādutthite .arthe hi deyamardhaṃ dvijottamaiḥ || 76 ||

asatpratigrahasarvaṃ durdānaṃ sāgare kṣipet |
āhūya dānaṃ kartavyamātmabhogasamṛddhaye || 77 ||

pṛṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ sadā deyamātmaśaktyanusārataḥ |
janmāntare ṛṇī hi syādadatte pṛṣṭavastuni || 78 ||

pareṣāṃ ca tathā doṣaṃ na praśaṃsedvicakṣaṇaḥ |
viśeṣeṇa tathā brahmañchrutaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ ca no vadet || 79 ||

na vadetsarvajantūnāṃ hṛdi roṣakaraṃ budhaḥ |
saṃdhyayoragnikāryaṃ ca kuryādaiśvaryasiddhaye || 80 ||

aśaktastvekakāle vā sūryāgnī ca yathāvidhi |
taṃḍulaṃ dhānyamājyaṃ vā phalaṃ kaṃdaṃ havistathā || 81 ||

sthālīpākaṃ tathā kuryādyathānyāyaṃ yathāvidhi |
pradhānahomamātraṃ vā havyābhāve samācaret || 82 ||

nityasaṃdhānamityuktaṃ tamajasraṃ vidurbudhāḥ |
athavā japamātraṃ vā sūryavaṃdanameva ca || 83 ||

evamātmārthinaḥ kuryurarthārthī ca yathāvidhi |
brahmayajñaratā nityaṃ devapūjāratāstathā || 84 ||

agnipūjāparā nityaṃ gurupūjāratāstathā |
brāhmaṇānāṃ tṛptikarāḥ sarve svargasya bhāginaḥ || 85 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ trayodaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 13 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

agniyajñaṃ devayajñaṃ brahmayajñaṃ tathaiva ca |
gurupūjāṃ brahmatṛptiṃ krameṇa brūhi naḥ prabho || 1 ||

sūta uvāca |

agnau juhoti yaddravyamagniyajñaḥ sa ucyate |
brahmacaryāśramasthānāṃ samidādhānameva hi || 2 ||

samidagrau vratādyaṃ ca viśeṣayajanādikam |
prathamāśramiṇāmevaṃ yāvadaupāsanaṃ dvijāḥ || 3 ||

ātmanyāropitāgnīnāṃ vanināṃ yatināṃ dvijāḥ |
hitaṃ ca mitamedhyānnaṃ svakāle bhojanaṃ hutiḥ || 4 ||

aupāsanāgnisaṃdhānaṃ samārabhya surakṣitam |
kuṃḍe vāpyatha bhāṃḍe vā tadajasraṃ samīritam || 5 ||

agnimātmanyaraṇyāṃ vā rājadaivavaśāddhruvam |
agnityāgabhayāduktaṃ samāropitamucyate || 6 ||

saṃpatkarī tathā jñeyā sāyamagnyāhutirdvijāḥ |
āyuṣkarīti vijñeyā prātaḥ sūryāhutistathā || 7 ||

agniyajño hyayaṃ prokto divā sūryaniveśanāt |
iṃdrādīnsakalāndevānuddiśyāgnau juhotiyat || 8 ||

devayajñaṃ hi taṃ vidyātsthālīpākādikānkratūn |
caulādikaṃ tathā jñeyaṃ laukikāgnau pratiṣṭhitam || 9 ||

brahmayajñaṃ dvijaḥ kuryāddevānāṃ tṛptaye sakṛt |
brahmayajña iti prokto vedasyā.adhyayanaṃ bhavet || 10 ||

nityānantaramāsoyaṃ tatastu na vidhīyate |
anagnau devayajanaṃ śṛṇuta śraddhayādarāt || 11 ||

ādisṛṣṭau mahādevaḥ sarvajñaḥ karuṇākaraḥ |
sarvalokopakārārthaṃ vārānkalpitavānprabhuḥ || 12 ||

saṃsāravaidyaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvabheṣajabheṣajam |
ādāvārogyadaṃ vāraṃ svavāraṃ kṛtavānprabhuḥ || 13 ||

saṃpatkāraṃ svamāyāyā varaṃ ca kṛtavāṃstataḥ |
janane durgatikrānte kumārasya tataḥ param || 14 ||

ālasyaduritakrāntyai vāraṃ kalpitavānprabhuḥ |
rakṣakasya tathā viṣṇorlokānāṃ hitakāmyayā || 15 ||

puṣṭyarthaṃ caiva rakṣārthaṃ vāraṃ kalpitavānprabhuḥ |
āyuṣkaraṃ tato vāramāyuṣāṃ kartureva hi || 16 ||

trailokyasṛṣṭikartturhi brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ |
jagadāyuṣyasiddhyarthaṃ vāraṃ kalpitavānprabhuḥ || 17 ||

ādau trailokyavṛddhyarthaṃ puṇyapāpe prakalpite |
tayoḥ kartrostato vāramiṃdrasya ca yamasya ca || 18 ||

bhogapradaṃ mṛtyuharaṃ lokānāṃ ca prakalpitam |
ādityādīnsvasvarūpānsukhaduḥkhasya sūcakān || 19 ||

vāreśānkalpayitvādau jyotiścakrepratiṣṭhitān |
svasvavāre tu teṣāṃ tu pūjā svasvaphalapradā || 20 ||

ārogyaṃ saṃpadaścaiva vyādhīnāṃ śāntireva ca |
puṣṭirāyustathā bhogo mṛterhāniryathākramam || 21 ||

vārakramaphalaṃ prāhurdevaprītipuraḥsaram |
anyeṣāmapi devānāṃ pūjāyāḥ phaladaḥ śivaḥ || 22 ||

devānāṃ prītaye pūjāpaṃcadhaiva prakalpitā |
tattanmantrajapo homo dānaṃ caiva tapastathā || 23 ||

sthaṃḍile pratimāyāṃ ca hyagnau brāhmaṇavigrahe |
samārādhanamityevaṃ ṣoḍaśairupacārakaiḥ || 24 ||

uttarottaravaiśiṣṭyātpūrvābhāve tathottaram |
netrayoḥ śiraso roge tathā kuṣṭhasya śāntaye || 25 ||

ādityaṃ pūjayitvā tu brāhmaṇānbhojayettataḥ |
dinaṃ māsaṃ tathā varṣaṃ varṣatrayamathavāpi vā || 26 ||

prārabdhaṃ prabalaṃ cetsyānnaśyedrogajarādikam |
japādyamiṣṭadevasya vārādīnāṃ phalaṃ viduḥ || 27 ||

pāpaśāntirviśeṣeṇa hyādivāre nivedayet |
ādityasyaiva devānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ viśiṣṭadam || 28 ||

somavāre ca lakṣmyādīnsaṃpadarthaṃ yajedbudhaḥ |
ājyānnena tathā viprānsapatnīkāṃśca bhojayet || 29 ||

kālyādīnbhauma vāre tu yajedrogapraśāntaye |
māṣamudgāḍhakānnena brahmaṇāṃścaiva bhojayet || 30 ||

saumyavāre tathā viṣṇuṃ dadhyannena yajedbudhaḥ |
putramitrakalatrādipuṣṭirbhavati sarvadā || 31 ||

āyuṣkāmo gurorvāre devānāṃ puṣṭisiddhaye |
upavītena vastreṇa kṣīrājyena yajedbudhaḥ || 32 ||

bhogārthaṃ bhṛgavāre tu yajeddevānsamāhitaḥ |
ṣaḍrasopetamannaṃ ca dadyādbrāhmaṇatṛptaye || 33 ||

strīṇāṃ ca tṛptaye tadvaddeyaṃ vastrādikaṃ śubham |
apamṛtyuhare maṃde rudrādrīṃśca yajedbudhaḥ || 34 ||

tilahomena dānena tilānnena ca bhojayet |
itthaṃ yajecca vibudhānārogyādiphalaṃ labhet || 35 ||

devānāṃ nityayajane viśeṣayajanepi ca |
snāne dāne jape home brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tarpaṇe || 36 ||

tithinakṣatrayoge ca tattaddevaprapūjane |
ādivārādivāreṣu sarvajño jagadīśvaraḥ || 37 ||

tattadrūpeṇa sarveṣāmārogyādiphalapradaḥ |
deśakālānusāreṇa tathā pātrānusārataḥ || 38 ||

dravyaśraddhānusāreṇa tathā lokānusārataḥ |
tāratamyakramāddevastvārogyādīnprayacchati || 39 ||

śubhādāvaśubhānte ca janmarkṣeṣu gṛhe gṛhī |
ārogyādisamṛddhyarthamādityādīngrahānyajet || 40 ||

tasmādvai devayajanaṃ sarvābhīṣṭaphalapradam |
samantrakaṃ brāhmaṇānāmanyeṣāṃ caiva tāntrikam || 41 ||

yathāśaktyānurūpeṇa kartavyaṃ sarvadā naraiḥ |
saptasvapi ca vāreṣu naraiḥ śubhaphalepsubhiḥ || 42 ||

daridrastapasā devānyajedāḍhyo dhanena hi |
punaścaivaṃvidhaṃ dharmaṃ kurute śraddhayā saha || 43 ||

punaśca bhogānvividhānbhuktvā bhūmau prajāyate |
chāyāṃ jalāśayaṃ brahmapratiṣṭhāṃ dharmasaṃcayam || 44 ||

sarvaṃ ca vittavānkuryātsadā bhogaprasiddhaye |
kālācca puṇyapākena jñānasiddhiḥ prajāyate || 45 ||

ya imaṃ śṛṇute .adhyāyaṃ paṭhate vā naro dvijāḥ |
śravaṇasyopakarttā ca devayajñaphalaṃ labhet || 46 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ caturdaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 14 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

deśādīnkramaśo brūhi sūta sarvārthavittam |

sūta uvāca |

śuddhaṃ gṛhaṃ samaphalaṃ devayajñādikarmasu || 1 ||

tato daśaguṇaṃ goṣṭhaṃ jalatīraṃ tato daśa |
tato daśaguṇaṃ bilvatulasyaśvatthamūlakam || 2 ||

tato devālayaṃ vidyāttīrthatīraṃ tato daśa |
tato daśaguṇaṃ nadyāstīrthanadyāstato daśa || 3 ||

saptagaṃgānadītīraṃ tasyā daśaguṇaṃ bhavet |
gaṃgā godāvarī caiva kāverī tāmraparṇikā || 4 ||

siṃdhuśca sarayū revā saptagaṃgāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |
tato .abdhitīraṃ daśa ca parvatāgre tato daśa || 5 ||

sarvasmādadhikaṃ jñeyaṃ yatra vā rocate manaḥ |
kṛte pūrṇaphalaṃ jñeyaṃ yajñadānādikaṃ tathā || 6 ||

tretāyuge tripādaṃ ca dvāpare .ardhaṃ sadā smṛtam |
kalau pādaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ tatpādonaṃ tatorddhake || 7 ||

śuddhātmanaḥ śuddhadinaṃ puṇyaṃ samaphalaṃ viduḥ |
tasmāddaśaguṇaṃ jñeyaṃ ravisaṃkramaṇe budhāḥ || 8 ||

viṣuve taddaśaguṇamayane taddaśa smṛtam |
taddaśa mṛgasaṃkrāntau taccaṃdragrahaṇe daśa || 9 ||

tataśca sūryagrahaṇe pūrṇakālottame viduḥ |
jagadrūpasya sūryasya viṣayogācca rogadam || 10 ||

atastadviṣaśāntyarthaṃ snānadānajapāṃścaret |
viṣaśāntyarthakālatvātsa kālaḥ puṇyadaḥ smṛtaḥ || 11 ||

janmarkṣe ca vratānte ca sūryarāgopamaṃ viduḥ |
mahatāṃ saṃgakālaśca koṭyarkagrahaṇaṃ viduḥ || 12 ||

taponiṣṭhā jñānaniṣṭhā yogino yatayastathā |
pūjāyāḥ pātramete hi pāpasaṃkṣayakāraṇam || 13 ||

caturviṃśatilakṣaṃ vā gāyatryā japasaṃyutaḥ |
brāhmaṇastu bhavetpātraṃ saṃpūrṇaphalabhogadam || 14 ||

patanāttrāyata iti pātraṃ śāstre prayujyate |
dātuśca pātakāttrāṇātpātramityabhidhīyate || 15 ||

gāyakaṃ trāyate pātādgāyatrītyucyate hi sā |
yathā.arthahino loke .asminparasyārthaṃ na yacchati || 16 ||

arthavāniha yo loke parasyārthaṃ prayacchati |
svayaṃ śuddho hi pūtātmā narānsantrātumarhati || 17 ||

gāyatrījapaśuddho hi śuddhabrāhmaṇa ucyate |
tasmāddāne jape home pūjāyāṃ sarvakarmaṇi || 18 ||

dānaṃ kartuṃ tathā trātuṃ pātraṃ tu brāhmaṇorhati |
annasya kṣudhitaṃ pātraṃ nārīnaramayātmakam || 19 ||

brāhmaṇaṃ śreṣṭhamāhūya yatkāle susamāhitam |
tadarthaṃ śabdamarthaṃ vā sadbodhakamabhīṣṭadam || 20 ||

icchāvataḥ pradānaṃ ca saṃpūrṇaphaladaṃ viduḥ |
yatpraśnānantaraṃ dattaṃ tadardhaṃ phaladaṃ viduḥ || 21 ||

yatsevakāya dattaṃ syāttatpādaphaladaṃ viduḥ |
jātimātrasya viprasya dīnavṛrtterdvijarṣabhāḥ || 22 ||

dattamarthaṃ hi bhogāya bhūrlokedaśavārṣikam |
vedayuktasya viprasya svarge hi daśavārṣikam || 23 ||

gāyatrījapayuktasya satye hi daśavārṣikam |
viṣṇubhaktasya viprasya dattaṃ vaikuṃṭhadaṃ viduḥ || 24 ||

śivabhaktasya viprasya dattaṃ kailāsadaṃ viduḥ |
tattallokopabhogārthaṃ sarveṣāṃ dānamiṣyate || 25 ||

daśāṃgamannaṃ viprasya bhānuvāre dadannaraḥ |
parajanmani cārogyaṃ daśavarṣaṃ samaśnute || 26 ||

bahumānamathāhvānamabhyaṃgaṃ pādasevanam |
vāso gaṃdhādyarcanaṃ ca ghṛtāpūparasottaram || 27 ||

ṣaḍrasaṃ vyaṃjanaṃ caiva tāṃbūlaṃ dakṣiṇottaram |
namaścānugamaścaiva svannadānaṃ daśāṃgakam || 28 ||

daśāṃgamannaṃ viprebhyo daśabhyo vai dadannaraḥ |
arkavāre tathā.a.arogyaṃ śatavarṣaṃ samaśnute || 29 ||

somavārādivāreṣu tattadvāraguṇaṃ phalam |
annadānasya vijñeyaṃ bhūrloke parajanmani || 30 ||

saptasvapi ca vāreṣu daśabhyaśca daśāṃgakam |
annaṃ dattvā śataṃ varṣamārogyādikamaśnute || 31 ||

evaṃ śatebhyo viprebhyo bhānuvāre dadannaraḥ |
sahasravarṣamārogyaṃ śarvaloke samaśnute || 32 ||

sahasrebhyastathā dattvā .ayutavarṣaṃ samaśnute |
evaṃ somādivāreṣu vijñeyaṃ hi vipaścitā || 33 ||

bhānuvāre sahasrāṇāṃ gāyatrīpūtacetasām |
annaṃ dattvā satyaloke hyārogyādi samaśnute || 34 ||

ayutānāṃ tathā dattvā viṣṇuloke samaśnute |
annaṃ dattvā tu lakṣāṇāṃ rudraloke samaśnute || 35 ||

bālānāṃ brahmabuddhyā hi deyaṃ vidyārthibhirnaraiḥ |
yūnāṃ ca viṣṇubuddhyā hi putrakāmārthibhirnaraiḥ || 36 ||

vṛddhānāṃ rudrabuddhyā hi deyaṃ jñānārthibhirnaraiḥ |
bālastrībhāratībuddhyā buddhikāmairnarottamaiḥ || 37 ||

lakṣmībuddhyā yuvastrīṣu bhogakāmairnarottamaiḥ |
vṛddhāsu pārvatībuddhyā deyamātmārthibhirjanaiḥ || 38 ||

śilavṛttyoñchavṛttyā ca gurudakṣiṇayārjitam |
śuddhadravyamiti prāhustatpūrṇaphaladaṃ viduḥ || 39 ||

śuklapratigrahāddattaṃ madhyamaṃ dravyamucyate |
kṛṣivāṇijyakopetamadhamaṃ dravyamucyate || 40 ||

kṣatriyāṇāṃ viśāṃ caiva śauryavāṇijyakārjitam |
uttamaṃ dravyamityāhuḥ śūdrāṇāṃ bhṛtakārjitam || 41 ||

strīṇāṃ dharmārthināṃ dravyaṃ paitṛkaṃ bhartṛkaṃ tathā |
gavādīnāṃ dvādaśīnāṃ caitrādiṣu yathākramam || 42 ||

saṃbhūya vā puṇyakāle dadyādiṣṭasamṛddhaye |
gobhūtilahiraṇyājyavāsodhānyaguḍāni ca || 43 ||

raupyaṃ lavaṇakūṣmāṃḍe kanyādvādaśakaṃ tathā |
godānāddattagavyena gomayenopakāriṇā || 44 ||

dhanadhānyādyāśritānāṃ duritānāṃ nivāraṇam |
jalasnehādyāśritānāṃ duritānāṃ tu gojalaiḥ || 45 ||

kāyikāditrāṇāṃ tu kṣīradadhyājyakaistathā |
tathā teṣāṃ ca puṣṭiśca vijñeyā hi vipaścitā || 46 ||

bhūdānaṃ tu pratiṣṭhārthamiha cā.amutra ca dvijāḥ |
tiladānaṃ balārthaṃ hi sadā mṛtyujayaṃ viduḥ || 47 ||

hiraṇyaṃ jāṭharāgnestu vṛddhidaṃ vīryadaṃ tathā |
ājyaṃ puṣṭikaraṃ vidyādvastramāyuṣkaraṃ viduḥ || 48 ||

dhānyamannaṃ samṛddhyarthaṃ madhurāhāradaṃ guḍam |
raupyaṃ retobhivṛddhyarthaṃ ṣaḍrasārthaṃ tu lāvaṇam || 49 ||

sarvaṃ sarvasamṛddhyarthaṃ kūṣmāṃḍaṃ puṣṭidaṃ viduḥ |
prāptidaṃ sarvabhogānāmiha cā.amutra ca dvijāḥ || 50 ||

yāvajjīvanamuktaṃ hi kanyādānaṃ tu bhogadam |
panasāmrakapitthānāṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ phalameva ca || 51 ||

kadalyādyauṣadhīnāṃ ca phalaṃ gulmodbhavaṃ tathā |
māṣādīnāṃ ca mudgānāṃ phalaṃ śākādikaṃ tathā || 52 ||

marīcisarṣapādyānāṃ śākopakaraṇaṃ tathā |
yadṛtau yatphalaṃ siddhaṃ taddeyaṃ hi vipaścitā || 53 ||

śrotrādīṃdriyatṛptiśca sadā deyā vipaścitā |
śabdādidaśabhogārthaṃ digādīnāṃ ca tuṣṭidā || 54 ||

vedaśāstraṃ samādāya buddhvā gurumukhātsvayam |
karmaṇāṃ phalamastīti buddhirāstikyamucyate || 55 ||

baṃdhurājabhayādbuddhiśraddhā sā ca kanīyasī |
sarvābhāve daridrastu vācā vā karmaṇā yajet || 56 ||

vācikaṃ yajanaṃ vidyānmantrastotrajapādikam |
tīrthayātrāvratādyaṃ hi kāyikaṃ yajanaṃ viduḥ || 57 ||

yena kenāpyupāyena hyalpaṃ vā yadi vā bahu |
devatārpaṇabuddhyā ca kṛtaṃ bhogāya kalpate || 58 ||

tapaścaryā ca dānaṃ ca kartavyamubhayaṃ sadā |
pratiśrayaṃ pradātavyaṃ svavarṇaguṇaśobhitam || 59 ||

devānāṃ tṛptaye .atyarthaṃ sarvabhogapradaṃ budhaiḥ |
ihā.amutrottamaṃ janmasadābhogaṃ labhedbudhaḥ |
īśvarārpaṇabuddhyā hi kṛtvā mokṣaphalaṃ labhet || 69 ||

ya imaṃ paṭhate .adhyāyaṃ yaḥ śṛṇoti sadā naraḥ |
tasya vaidharmabuddhiśca jñānasiddhiḥ prajāyate || 61 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ paṃcadaśodhyāyaḥ || 15 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

pārthivapratimāpūjāvidhānaṃ brūhi sattama |
yena pūjāvidhānena sarvābhiṣṭamavāpyate || 1 ||

sūta uvāca |

susādhupṛṣṭaṃ yuṣmābhiḥ sadā sarvārthadāyakam |
sadyo duḥkhasya śamanaṃ śṛṇuta prabravīmi vaḥ || 2 ||

apamṛtyuharaṃ kālamṛtyoścāpi vināśanam |
sadyaḥ kalatraputrādidhanadhānyapradaṃ dvijāḥ || 3 ||

annādibhojyaṃ vastrādisarvamutpadyate yataḥ |
tato mṛdādipratimāpūjābhīṣṭapradā bhuvi || 4 ||

puruṣāṇāṃ ca nārīṇāmadhikārotra niścitam |
nadyāṃ taḍāge kūpe vā jalāntarmṛdamāharet || 5 ||

saṃśodhya gaṃdhacūrṇena peṣayitvā sumaṃḍape |
hastena pratimāṃ kuryātkṣīreṇa ca susaṃskṛtām || 6 ||

aṃgapratyaṃgakopetāmāyudhaiśca samanvitām |
padmāsanasthitāṃ kṛtvā pūjayedādareṇa hi || 7 ||

vighneśādityaviṣṇūnāmaṃbāyāśca śivasya ca |
śivasyaśivaliṃgaṃ ca sarvadā pūjayeddvija || 8 ||

ṣoḍaśairupacāraiśca kuryāttatphalasiddhaye |
puṣpeṇa prokṣaṇaṃ kuryādabhiṣekaṃ samantrakam || 9 ||

śālyannenaiva naivedyaṃ sarvaṃ kuḍavamānataḥ |
gṛhe tu kuḍavaṃ jñeyaṃ mānuṣe prasthamiṣyate || 10 ||

daive prasthatrayaṃ yogyaṃ svayaṃbhoḥ prasthapaṃcakam |
evaṃ pūrṇaphalaṃ vidyādadhikaṃ vai dvayaṃ trayam || 11 ||

sahasrapūjayā satyaṃ satyalokaṃ labheddvijaḥ |
dvādaśāṃgulamāyāmaṃ dviguṇaṃ ca tato .adhikam || 12 ||

pramāṇamaṃgulasyaikaṃ tadūrdhvaṃ paṃcakatrayam |
ayodārukṛtaṃ pātraṃ śivamityucyate budhaiḥ || 13 ||

tadaṣṭabhāgaḥ prasthaḥ syāttaccatuḥkuḍavaṃ matam |
daśaprasthaṃ śataprasthaṃ sahasraprasthameva ca || 14 ||

jalatailādigaṃdhānāṃ yathāyogyaṃ ca mānataḥ |
mānuṣārṣasvayaṃbhūnāṃ mahāpūjeti kathyate || 15 ||

abhiṣekādātmaśuddhirgaṃdhātpuṇyamavāpyate |
āyustṛptiśca naivedyāddhūpādarthamavāpyate || 16 ||

dīpājjñānamavāpnoti tāṃbūlādbhogamāpnuyāt |
tasmātsnānādikaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ prayatnena prasādhayet || 17 ||

namaskāro japaścaiva sarvābhīṣṭapradāvubhau |
pūjānte ca sadākāryau bhogamokṣārthibhirnaraiḥ || 18 ||

saṃpūjya manasā pūrvaṃ kuryāttattatsadā naraḥ |
devānāṃ pūjayā caiva tattallokamavāpnuyāt || 19 ||

tadavāntaraloke ca yatheṣṭaṃ bhogyamāpyate |
tadviśeṣānpravakṣyāmi śṛṇuta śraddhayā dvijāḥ || 20 ||

vighneśapūjayā samyagbhūrloke .abhīṣṭamāpnuyāt |
śukravāre caturthyāṃ ca site śrāvaṇabhādrake || 21 ||

bhiṣagṛkṣe dhanurmāse vighneśaṃ vidhivadyajet |
śataṃ pūjāsahasraṃ vā tatsaṃkhyākadinairvrajet || 22 ||

devāgniśraddhayā nityaṃ putradaṃ ceṣṭadaṃ nṛṇām |
sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ tattadduritanāśanam || 23 ||

vārapūjāṃśivādīnāmātmaśuddhipradāṃ viduḥ |
tithinakṣatrayogānāmādhāraṃ sārvakāmikam || 24 ||

tathā bṛddhikṣayābhāvātpūrṇabrahmātmakaṃ viduḥ |
udayādudayaṃ vāro brahmaprabhṛti karmaṇām || 25 ||

tithyādau devapūjā hi pūrṇabhogapradā nṛṇām |
pūrvabhāgaḥ pitṝṇāṃ tu niśi yuktaḥ praśasyate || 26 ||

parabhāgastu devānāṃ divā yuktaḥ praśasyate |
udayavyāpinī grāhyā madhyāhne yadi sā tithiḥ || 27 ||

devakārye tathā grāhyāsthiti ṛkṣādikāḥ śubhāḥ |
samyagvicārya vārādīnkuryātpūjājapādikam || 28 ||

pūjāryate hyaneneti vedeṣvarthasya yojanā |
pūrṇabhogaphalasiddhiśca jāyate tena karmaṇā || 29 ||

manobhāvāṃstathā jñānamiṣṭabhogārthayojanāt |
pūjāśabdartha evaṃ hi viśruto lokavedayoḥ || 30 ||

nityanaimittikaṃ kālātsadyaḥ kāmye svanuṣṭhite |
nityaṃ māsaṃ ca pakṣaṃ ca varṣaṃ caiva yathākramam || 31 ||

tattatkarmaphalaprāptistādṛkpāpakṣayaḥ kramāt |
mahāgaṇapateḥ pūjā caturthyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣake || 32 ||

pakṣapāpakṣayakarī pakṣabhogaphalapradā |
caitre caturthyāṃ pūjā ca kṛtā māsaphalapradā || 33 ||

varṣabhogapradā jñeyā kṛtā vai siṃhabhādrake |
śravaṇyādityavāre ca saptamyāṃ hastabhe dine || 34 ||

māghaśukle ca saptamyāmādityayajanaṃ caret |
jyeṣṭhabhādrakasaumye ca dvādaśyāṃ śravarṇakṣake || 35 ||

dvādaśyāṃ viṣṇuyajanamiṣṭaṃsaṃpatkaraṃ viduḥ |
śrāvaṇe viṣṇuyajanamiṣṭārogyapradaṃ bhavet || 36 ||

gavādīndvādaśānarthānsāṃgāndatvā tu yatphalam |
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti dvādaśyāṃ viṣṇutarpaṇāt || 37 ||

dvādaśyāṃ dvādaśānviprānviṣṇordvādaśanāmataḥ |
ṣoḍaśairupacāraiśca yajettatprītimāpnuyāt || 38 ||

evaṃ ca sarvadevānāṃ tattaddvādaśanāmakaiḥ |
dvādaśabrahmayajanaṃ tattatprītikaraṃ bhavet || 39 ||

karkaṭe somavāre ca navamyāṃ mṛgaśīrṣake |
aṃbāṃ yajedbhūtikāmaḥ sarvabhogaphalapradām || 40 ||

āśvayukchuklanavamī sarvābhīṣṭaphalapradā |
ādivāre caturdaśyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe viśeṣataḥ || 41 ||

ārdrāyāṃ ca mahārdrāyāṃ śivapūjā viśiṣyate |
māghakṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ sarvābhīṣṭaphalapradā || 42 ||

āyuṣkarī mṛtyuharā sarvasiddhikarī nṛṇām |
jyeṣṭhamāse mahārdrāyāṃ caturdaśīdinepi ca || 43 ||

mārgaśīrṣārdrakāyāṃ vā ṣoḍaśairupacārakaiḥ |
tattanmūrtiśivaṃ pūjya tasya vai pādadarśanam || 44 ||

śivasya yajanaṃ jñeyaṃ bhogamokṣapradaṃ nṛṇām |
vārādidevayajanaṃ kārtike hi viśiṣyate || 45 ||

kārtike māsi saṃprāpte sarvāndevānyajedbudhaḥ |
dānena tapasā homairjapena niyamena ca || 46 ||

ṣoḍaśairupacāraiśca pratimā vipramantrakaiḥ |
brāhmaṇānāṃ bhojanena niṣkāmārtikaro bhavet || 47 ||

kārtike devayajanaṃ sarvabhogapradaṃ bhavet |
vyādhīnāṃ haraṇaṃ caiva bhavedbhūtagrahakṣayaḥ || 48 ||

kārtikādityavāreṣu nṛṇāmādityapūjanāt |
tailakārpāsadānāttu bhavetkuṣṭhādisaṃkṣayaḥ || 49 ||

harītakīmarīcīnāṃ vastrakṣīrādidānataḥ |
brahmapratiṣṭhayā caiva kṣayarogakṣayo bhavet || 50 ||

dīpasarṣapadānācca apasmārakṣayo bhavet |
kṛttikāsomavāreṣu śivasya yajanaṃ nṛṇām || 51 ||

mahādāridryaśamanaṃ sarvasaṃpatkaraṃ bhavet |
gṛhakṣetrādidānācca gṛhopakaraṇādinā || 52 ||

kṛttikābhaumavāreṣu skaṃdasya yajanānnṛṇām |
dīpaghaṃṭādidānādvai vāksiddhiracirādbhavet || 53 ||

kṛttikāsaumyavāreṣu viṣṇorvai yajanaṃ nṛṇām |
dadhyodanasya dānaṃ ca satsantānakaraṃ bhavet || 54 ||

kṛtikāguruvāreṣu brahmaṇo yajanāddhanaiḥ |
madhusvarṇājyadānena bhogavṛddhirbhavennṛṇām || 55 ||

kṛttikāśukravāreṣu gajakomeḍayājanāt |
gaṃdhapuṣpānnadānena bhogyavṛddhirbhavennṛṇām || 56 ||

vaṃdhyā suputraṃ labhate svarṇaraupyādidānataḥ |
kṛttikāśanivāreṣu dikpālānāṃ ca vaṃdanam || 57 ||

diggajānāṃ ca nāgānāṃ setupānāṃ ca pūjanam |
tryaṃbakasya ca rudrasya viṣṇoḥ pāpaharasya ca || 58 ||

jñānadaṃ brahmaṇaścaiva dhanvantaryaśvinostathā |
rogāpamṛtyuharaṇaṃ tatkālavyādhiśāntidam || 59 ||

lavaṇāyasatailānāṃ māṣādīnāṃ ca dānataḥ |
trikaṭuphalagaṃdhānāṃ jalādīnāṃ ca dānataḥ || 60 ||

dravāṇāṃ kaṭhinānāṃ ca prasthena palamānataḥ |
svargaprāptirdhanurmāse hyuṣaḥkāle ca pūjanam || 61 ||

śivādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ kramādvai sarvasiddhaye |
śālyannasya haviṣyasya naivedyaṃ śastamucyate || 62 ||

vividhānnasya naivedyaṃ dhanurmāse viśiṣyate |
mārgaśīrṣe .annadasyaiva sarvamiṣṭaphalaṃ bhavet || 63 ||

pāpakṣayaṃ ceṣṭasiddhiṃ cārogyaṃ dharmameva ca |
samyagvedaparijñānaṃ sadanuṣṭhānameva ca || 64 ||

ihāmutra mahābhogānante yogaṃ ca śāśvatam |
vedāntajñānasiddhiṃ ca mārgaśīrṣānnado labhet || 65 ||

mārgaśīrṣe hyuṣaḥkāle dinatrayamathāpi vā |
yajeddevānbhogakāmo nādhanurmāsiko bhavet || 66 ||

yāvatsaṃgavakālaṃ tu dhanurmāso vidhīyate |
dhanurmāse nirāhāro māsamātraṃ jiteṃdriyaḥ || 67 ||

āmadhyāhnajapedvipro gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram |
paṃcākṣarādikānmantrānpaścādāsaptikaṃ japet || 68 ||

jñānaṃ labdhvā ca dehānte vipro muktimavāpnuyāt |
anyeṣāṃ naranārīṇāṃ triḥsnānena japena ca || 69 ||

sadā paṃcākṣarasyaiva viśuddhaṃ jñānamāpyate |
iṣṭamantrānsadājaptvā mahāpāpakṣayaṃ labhet || 70 ||

dhanurmāse viśeṣeṇa mahānaivedyamācaret |
śālitaṃḍulabhāreṇa marīcaprasthakena ca || 71 ||

gaṇanāddvādaśaṃ sarvaṃ madhvājyakuḍavena hi |
droṇayuktena mudgena dvādaśavyaṃjanena ca || 72 ||

ghṛtapakvairapūpaiśca modakaiḥ śālikādibhiḥ |
dvādaśaiśca dadhikṣīrairdvādaśaprasthakena ca || 73 ||

nārikelaphalādīnāṃ tathā gaṇanayā saha |
dvādaśakramukairyuktaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśatpatrakairyutam || 74 ||

karpūrakhuracūrṇena paṃcasaugaṃdhikairyutam |
tāṃbūlayuktaṃ tu yadā mahānaivedyalakṣaṇam || 75 ||

mahānaivedyametadvai devatārpaṇapūrvakam |
varṇānukramapūrveṇa tadbhaktebhyaḥ pradāpayet || 76 ||

evaṃ caudananaivedyādbhūmau rāṣṭrapatirbhavet |
mahānaivedyadānena naraḥ svargamavāpnuyāt || 77 ||

mahānaivedyadānena sahasreṇa dvijarṣabhāḥ |
satyaloke ca talloke pūrṇamāyuravāpnuyāt || 78 ||

sahasrāṇāṃ ca triṃśatyā mahānaivedyadānataḥ |
tadūrdhvalokamāpyaiva na punarjanmabhāgbhavet || 79 ||

sahasrāṇāṃ ca ṣaṭtriṃśajjanma naivedyamīritam |
tāvannaivedyadānaṃ tu mahāpūrṇaṃ taducyate || 80 ||

mahāpūrṇasya naivedyaṃ janmanaivedyamiṣyate |
janmanaivedyadānena punarjanma na vidyate || 81 ||

ūrje māsi dine puṇye janma naivedyamācaret |
saṃkrāntipātajanmarkṣapaurṇamāsyādisaṃyute || 82 ||

abdajanmadine kuryājjanmanaivedyamuttamam |
māsāntareṣu janmarkṣapūrṇayogadinepi ca || 83 ||

melane ca śanairvāpi tāvatsāhasramācaret |
janmanaivedyadānena janmārpaṇaphalaṃ labhet || 84 ||

janmārpaṇācchivaḥ prītiḥ svasāyujyaṃ dadāti hi |
idaṃ tajjanmanaivedyaṃ śivasyaiva pradāpayet || 85 ||

yoniliṃgasvarūpeṇa śivo janmanirūpakaḥ |
tasmājjanmanivṛttyarthaṃ janma pūjā śivasya hi || 86 ||

biṃdunādātmakaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṃgamam |
biṃduḥ śaktiḥ śivo nādaḥ śivaśaktyātmakaṃ jagat || 87 ||

nādādhāramidaṃ biṃdurbiṃdvādhāramidaṃ jagat |
jagadādhārabhūtau hi biṃdunādau vyavasthitau || 88 ||

vindunādayutaṃ sarvaṃ sakalīkaraṇaṃ bhavet |
sakalīkaraṇājjanmajagatprāpnotyasaṃśayaḥ || 89 ||

biṃdunādātmakaṃ liṃgaṃ jagatkāraṇamucyate |
biṃdurdevīśivo nādaḥ śivaliṃgaṃ tu kathyate || 90 ||

tasmājjanmanivṛttyarthaṃ śivaliṃgaṃ prapūjayet |
mātā devī biṃdurūpā nādarūpaḥ śivaḥ pitā || 91 ||

pūjitābhyāṃ pitṛbhyāṃ tu paramānaṃda eva hi |
paramānaṃdalābhārthaṃ śivaliṃgaṃ prapūjayet || 92 ||

sā devī jagatāṃ mātā sa śivo jagataḥ pitā / |
pitroḥ śuśrūṣake nityaṃ kṛpādhikyaṃ hi vardhate || 93 ||

kṛpayāntargataiśvaryaṃ pūjakasya dadāti hi |
ṭasmādantargatānaṃdalābhārthaṃ munipuṃgavāḥ || 94 ||

pitṛmātṛsvarūpeṇa śivaliṃgaṃ prapūjayet |
bhargaḥ puruṣarūpo hi bhargāprakṛtirucyate || 95 ||

avyaktāntaradhiṣṭhānaṃ garbhaḥ puruṣa ucyate |
suvyaktāntaradhiṣṭhānaṃ garbhaḥ prakṛtirucyate || 96 ||

puruṣatvādigarbho h igarbhavāñjanako yataḥ |
puruṣātprakṛto yuktaṃ prathamaṃ janma kathyate || 97 ||

prakṛtervyaktatāṃ yātaṃ dvitīyaṃ janma kathyate |
janma janturmṛtyujanma puruṣātpratipadyate || 98 ||

anyato bhāvyate .avaśyaṃ māyayā janma kathyate |
jīryate janmakālādyattasmājjīva iti smṛtaḥ || 99 ||

janyate tanyate pāśairjīvaśabdārtha eva hi |
janmapāśanivṛttyarthaṃ janmaliṃgaṃ prapūjayet || 100 ||

bhaṃ vṛddhiṃ gacchatītyarthādbhagaḥ prakṛtirucyate |
prākṛtaiḥ śabdamātrādyaiḥ prākṛteṃdriyabhojanāt || 101 ||
