bhagasyedaṃ bhogamiti śabdārtho mukhyataḥ śrutaḥ |
mukhyo bhagastu prakṛtirbhagavāñchiva ucyate || 102 ||

bhagavānbhogadātā hi nā.anyo bhogapradāyakaḥ |
bhagasvāmī ca bhagavānbharga ityucyate budhaiḥ || 103 ||

bhagena sahitaṃ liṃgaṃ bhagaṃliṃgena saṃyutam |
ihāmutra ca bhogārthaṃ nityabhogārthameva ca || 104 ||

bhagavantaṃ mahādevaṃ śivaliṃgaṃ prapūjayet |
lokaprasavitā sūryastaccihnaṃ prasavādbhavet || 105 ||

liṃgeprasūtikartāraṃ liṃginaṃ puruṣo yajet |
liṃgārthagamakaṃ cihnaṃ liṃgamityabhidhīyate || 106 ||

liṃgamarthaṃ hi puruṣaṃ śivaṃ gamayatītyadaḥ |
śivaśaktyośca cihnasya melanaṃ liṃgamucyate || 107 ||

svacihnapūjanātprītaścihnakāryaṃ na vīyate |
cihnakāryaṃ tu janmādijanmādyaṃ vinivartate || 108 ||

prākṛtaiḥ puruṣaiścāpi bāhyābhyantarasaṃbhavaiḥ |
ṣoḍaśairupacāraiśca śivaliṃgaṃ prapūjayet || 109 ||

evamādityavāre hi pūjā janmanivartikā |
ādivāre mahāliṃgaṃ praṇavenaiva pūjayet || 110 ||

ādivāre paṃcagavyairabhiṣeko viśiṣyate |
gomayaṃ gojalaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhyājyaṃ paṃcagavyakam || 111 ||

kṣīrādyaṃ ca pṛthakccaiva madhunā cekṣusārakaiḥ |
gavyakṣīrānnanaivedyaṃ praṇavenaiva kārayet || 112 ||

praṇavaṃ dhvaniliṃgaṃ tu nādaliṃgaṃ svayaṃbhuvaḥ |
biṃduliṃgaṃ tu yantraṃ syānmakāraṃ tu pratiṣṭhitam || 113 ||

ukāraṃ caraliṃgaṃ syādakāraṃ guruvigraham |
ṣaḍliṃgaṃ pūjayā nityaṃ jīvanmukto na saṃśayaḥ || 114 ||

śivasya bhaktyā pūjā hi janmamuktikarī nṛṇām |
rudrākṣadhāraṇātpādamardhaṃ vaibhūtidhāraṇāt || 115 ||

tripādaṃ mantrajāpyācca pūjayā pūrṇabhaktimān |
śivaliṃgaṃ ca bhaktaṃ ca pūjya mokṣaṃ labhennaraḥ || 116 ||

ya imaṃ paṭhate .adhyāyaṃ śṛṇuyādvā samāhitaḥ |
tasyaiva śivabhaktiśca vardhate sudṛḍhā dvijāḥ || 117 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ ṣoḍaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 16 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

praṇavasya ca māhātmyaṃ ṣaḍliṃgasya mahāmune |
śivabhaktasya pūjāṃ ca kramaśo brūhi naḥprabho || 1 ||

sūta uvāca |

tapodhanairbhavadbhiśca samyakpraśnastvayaṃ kṛtaḥ |
asyottaraṃ mahādevo jānāti sma na cāparaḥ || 2 ||

athāpi vakṣye tamahaṃ śivasya kṛpayaiva hi |
śivo .asmākaṃ ca yuṣmākaṃ rakṣāṃ gṛhṇātu bhūriśaḥ || 3 ||

pro hi prakṛtijātasya saṃsārasya mahodadheḥ |
navaṃ nāvāntaramiti praṇavaṃ vai vidurbudhāḥ || 4 ||

praḥ prapaṃco na nāstivo yuṣmākaṃ praṇavaṃ viduḥ |
prakarṣeṇa nayedyasmānmokṣaṃ vaḥ praṇavaṃ viduḥ || 5 ||

svajāpakānāṃ yogināṃ svamantrapūjakasya ca |
sarvakarmakṣayaṃ kṛtvā divyajñānaṃ tu nūtanam || 6 ||

tameva māyārahitaṃ nūtanaṃ paricakṣate |
prakarṣeṇa mahātmānaṃ navaṃ śuddhasvarūpakam || 7 ||

nūtanaṃ vai karotīti praṇavaṃ taṃ vidurbudhāḥ |
praṇavaṃ dvividhaṃ proktaṃ sūkṣmasthūlavibhedataḥ || 8 ||

sūkṣmamekākṣaraṃ vidyātsthūlaṃ paṃcākṣaraṃ viduḥ |
sūkṣmamavyaktapaṃcārṇaṃ suvyaktārṇaṃ tathetarat || 9 ||

jīvanmuktasya sūkṣmaṃ hi sarvasāraṃ hi tasya hi |
mantreṇārthānusaṃdhānaṃ svadehavilayāvadhi || 10 ||

svadehegalite pūrṇaṃ śivaṃ prāpnoti niścayaḥ |
kevalaṃ mantrajāpī tu yogaṃ prāpnoti niścayaḥ || 11 ||

ṣaṭtriṃśatkoṭijāpī tu niścayaṃ yogamāpnuyāt |
sūkṣmaṃ ca dvividhaṃ jñeyaṃ hrasvadīrghavibhedataḥ || 12 ||

akāraśca ukāraśca makāraśca tataḥ param |
biṃdunādayutaṃ taddhi śabdakālakalānvitam || 13 ||

dīrghapraṇavamevaṃ hi yogināmeva hṛdgatam |
makāraṃ tantritattvaṃ hi hrasvapraṇava ucyate || 14 ||

śivaḥ śaktistayoraikyaṃ makāraṃ tu trikātmakam |
hrasvamevaṃ hi jāpyaṃ syātsarvapāpakṣayaiṣiṇām || 15 ||

bhūvāyukanakārṇodyoḥśabdādyāśca tathā daśa |
āśānvayedaśapunaḥ pravṛttā iti kathyate || 16 ||

hrasvameva pravṛttānāṃ nivṛttānāṃ tu dīrghakam |
vyāhṛtyādau ca mantrādau kāmaṃ śabdakalāyutam || 17 ||

vedādau ca prayojyaṃ syādvaṃdane saṃdhyayorapi |
navakauṭijapāñjaptvā saṃśuddhaḥ puruṣo bhavet || 18 ||

punaśca navakoṭyā tu pṛthivījayamāpnuyāt |
punaśca navakoṭyā tu hyapāṃjayamavāpnuyāt || 19 ||

punaśca navakoṭyā tu tejasāṃjayamāpnuyāt |
punaśca navakoṭyā tu vāyorjayamavāpnuyāt |
ākāśajayamāpnoti navakoṭijapena vai || 20 ||

gaṃdhādīnāṃkrameṇaivanavakoṭijapeṇavai |
ahaṃkārasya ca punarnava koṭijapena vai || 21 ||

sahasramantrajaptena nityaśuddho bhavetpumān |
tataḥ paraṃ svasiddhyarthaṃ japo bhavati hi dvijāḥ || 22 ||

evamaṣṭottaraśatakoṭijaptena vai punaḥ |
praṇavena prabuddhastu śuddhayogamavāpnuyāt || 23 ||

śuddhayogena saṃyukto jīvanmukto na saṃśayaḥ |
sadā japansadādhyāyañchivaṃ praṇavarūpiṇam || 24 ||

samādhistho mahāyogīśiva eva na saṃśayaḥ |
ṛṣicchaṃdodevatādi nyasya dehepunarjapet || 25 ||

praṇavaṃ mātṛkāyuktaṃ dehe nyasya ṛṣirbhavet |
daśamātṛṣaḍadhvādi sarvaṃ nyāsaphalaṃ labhet || 26 ||

pravṛttānāṃ ca miśrāṇāṃ sthūlapraṇavamiṣyate |
kriyātapojapairyuktāstrividhāḥ śivayoginaḥ || 27 ||

dhanādivibhavaiścaiva karādyaṃgairnamādibhiḥ |
kriyayā pūjayā yuktaḥ kriyāyogīti kathyate || 28 ||

pūjāyuktaśca mitabhugbāhyeṃdriyajayānvitaḥ |
paradrohādirahitastapoyogīti kathyate || 29 ||

etairyuktaḥ sadā kruddhaḥ sarvakāmādivarjitaḥ |
sadā japaparaḥ śāntojapayogīti taṃ viduḥ || 30 ||

upacāraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ pūjayā śivayoginām |
sālokyādikrameṇaiva śuddho muktiṃ labhennaraḥ || 31 ||

japayogamatho vakṣye gadataḥ śṛṇuta dvijāḥ |
tapaḥkarturjapaḥ prokto yajjapanparimārjate || 32 ||

śivanāma namaḥpūrvaṃ caturthyāṃ paṃcatattvakam |
sthūlapraṇavarūpaṃ hi śivapaṃcākṣaraṃ dvijāḥ || 33 ||

paṃcākṣarajapenaiva sarvasiddhiṃ labhennaraḥ |
praṇavenādisaṃyuktaṃ sadā paṃcākṣaraṃ japet || 34 ||

gurūpadeśaṃ saṃgamya sukhavāse subhūtale |
pūrvapakṣe samārabhya kṛṣṇabhūtāvadhi dvijāḥ || 35 ||

māghaṃ bhādraṃ viśiṣṭaṃ tu sarvakālottamottamam |
ekavāraṃ mitāśītu vāgyato niyateṃdriyaḥ || 36 ||

svasya rājapitṝṇāṃ ca śuśrūṣaṇaṃ ca nityaśaḥ |
sahasrajapamātreṇa bhavecchuddho .anyathā ṛṇī || 37 ||

paṃcākṣaraṃ paṃcalakṣaṃ japecchivamanusmaran |
padmāsanasthaṃ śivadaṃ gaṃgācaṃdrakalānvitam || 38 ||

vāmorusthitaśaktyā ca virājaṃ taṃ mahāgaṇaiḥ |
mṛgaṭaṃkadharaṃ devaṃ varadābhayapāṇikam || 39 ||

sadānugrahakarttāraṃ sadā śivamanusmaran |
saṃpūjya manasā pūrvaṃ hṛdivāsūryamaṃḍale || 40 ||

japetpaṃcākṣarīṃ vidyāṃ prāṅmukhaḥ śuddhakarmakṛt |
prātaḥ kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ nityakarmasamāpya ca || 41 ||

manorame śucau deśe niyataḥ śuddhamānasaḥ |
paṃcākṣarasya mantrasya sahasraṃ dvādaśaṃ japet || 42 ||

varayecca sapatnīkāñchaivānvai brāhmaṇottamān |
ekaṃ guruvaraṃ śiṣṭaṃ varayetsāṃbamūrtikam || 43 ||

īśānaṃ cātha puruṣamaghoraṃ vāmameva ca |
sadyojātaṃ ca paṃcaiva śivabhaktāndvijottamān || 44 ||

pūjādravyāṇi saṃpādya śivapūjāṃ samārabhet |
śivapūjāṃ ca vidhivatkṛtvā homaṃ samārabhet || 45 ||

mukhāntaṃ ca svasūtreṇa kṛtvā homaṃ samārabhet |
daśaikaṃ vā śataikaṃ vā sahasraikamathāpi vā || 46 ||

kāpilena ghṛtenaiva juhuyātsvayameva hi |
kārayecchivabhaktairvāpyaṣṭottaraśataṃ budhaḥ || 47 ||

homānte dakṣiṇā deyā gurorgomithunaṃ tathā |
īśānādisvarūpāṃstānguruṃ sāṃbaṃ vibhāvya ca || 48 ||

teṣāṃ patsiktatoyena svaśiraḥ snānamācaret |
ṣaṭtriṃśatkoṭitīrtheṣu sadyaḥ snānaphalaṃ labhet || 49 ||

daśāṃgamannaṃ teṣāṃ vai dadyādvaibhaktipūrvakam |
parābuddhyā guroḥ patnīmīśānādikrameṇa tu || 50 ||

paramānnena saṃpūjya yathāvibhavavistaram |
rudrākṣavastrapūrvaṃ ca vaṭakāpūpakairyutam || 51 ||

balidānaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā bhūribhojanamācaret |
tataḥ saṃprārthya deveśaṃ japaṃ tāvatsamāpayet || 52 ||

puraścaraṇamevaṃ tu kṛtvā mantrībhavennaraḥ |
punaśca paṃcalakṣeṇa sarvapāpakṣayo bhavet || 53 ||

atalādi samārabhya satyalokāvadhikramāt |
paṃcalakṣajapāttattallokaiśvaryamavāpnuyāt || 54 ||

madhye mṛtaścedbhogānte bhūmau tajjāpako bhavet |
punaśca paṃcalakṣeṇa brahmasāmīpyamāpnuyāt || 55 ||

punaśca paṃcalakṣeṇa sārūpyaiśvaryamāpnuyāt |
āhatya śatalakṣeṇa sākṣādbrahmasamo bhavet || 56 ||

kāryabrahmaṇa evaṃ hi sāyujyaṃ pratipadya vai |
yatheṣṭaṃ bhogamāpnoti tadbrahmapralayāvadhi || 57 ||

punaḥ kalpāntare vṛtte brahmaputraḥ sajāyate |
punaśca tapasā dīptaḥ kramānmukto bhaviṣyati || 58 ||

pṛthvyādikāryabhūtebhyo lokā vai nirmitāḥ kramāt |
pātālādi ca satyāntaṃ brahmalokāścaturdaśa || 59 ||

satyādūrdhvaṃ kṣamāntaṃ vaiviṣṇulokāścaturdaśa |
kṣamaloke kāryaviṣṇurvaikuṃṭhe varapattane || 60 ||

kāryalakṣmyā mahābhogirakṣāṃ kṛtvā .adhitiṣṭhati |
tadūrdhvagāśca śucyantāṃ lokāṣṭāviṃśatiḥ sthitāḥ || 61 ||

śucau loke tu kailāse rudro vai bhūtahṛtsthitaḥ |
ṣaḍuttarāśca paṃcāśadahiṃsāntāstadūrdhvagāḥ || 62 ||

ahiṃsālokamāsthāya jñānakailāsake pure |
kāryeśvarastirobhāvaṃ sarvānkṛtvādhitiṣṭhati || 63 ||

tadante kālacakraṃ h ikālātītastataḥ param |
śivenādhiṣṭhitastatra kālaścakreśvarāhvayaḥ || 64 ||

māhiṣaṃ dharmamāsthāya sarvānkālena yuṃjati |
asatyaścāśuciścaiva hiṃsā caivātha nirghṛṇā || 65 ||

asatyādicatuṣpādaḥ sarvāṃśaḥ kāmarūpadhṛk |
nāstikyalakṣmīrduḥsaṃgo vedabāhyadhvaniḥ sadā || 66 ||

krodhasaṃgaḥ kṛṣṇavarṇo mahāmahiṣaveṣavān |
tāvanmaheśvaraḥ proktastirodhāstāvadeva hi || 67 ||

tadarvākkarmabhogo hi tadūrdhvaṃ jñānabhogakam |
tadarvākkarmamāyā hi jñānamāyā tadūrdhvakam || 68 ||

mā lakṣmīḥ karmabhogo vai yāti māyeti kathyate |
mā lakṣmīrjñānabhogo vai yāti māyeti kathyate || 69 ||

tadūrdhvaṃ nityabhogo hi tadarvāṅnaśvaraṃ viduḥ |
tadarvākca tirodhānaṃ tadūrdhvaṃ na tirodhanam || 70 ||

tadarvākpāśabaṃdho hi tadūrdhvaṃ na hi baṃdhanam |
tadarvākparivartante kāmyakarmānusāriṇaḥ || 71 ||

niṣkāmakarmabhogastu tadūrdhvaṃ parikīrtitaḥ |
tadarvākparivartante biṃdupūjāparāyaṇāḥ || 72 ||

tadūrdhvaṃ hi vrajantyeva niṣkāmā liṃgapūjakāḥ |
tadarvākparivartante śivānyasurapūjakāḥ || 73 ||

śivaikaniratā ye ca tadūrdhvaṃ saṃprayānti te |
tadarvāgjīvakoṭiḥ syāttadūrdhvaṃ parakoṭikāḥ || 74 ||

sāṃsārikāstadarvākca muktāḥ khalu tadūrdhvagāḥ |
tadarvākparivartante prākṛtadravyapūjakāḥ || 75 ||

tadūrdhvaṃ hi vrajantyete pauruṣadravyapūjakāḥ |
tadarvākchaktiliṃgaṃ tu śivaliṃgaṃ tadūrdhvakam || 76 ||

tadarvāgāvṛtaṃ liṃgaṃ tadūrdhvaṃ hi nirāvṛti |
tadarvākkalpitaṃ liṃgaṃ tadūrdhvaṃ vai na kalpitam || 77 ||

tadarvāgbāhyaliṃgaṃ syādantaraṃgaṃ tadūrdhvakam |
tadarvākchaktilokā hi śataṃ vai dvādaśādhikam || 78 ||

tadarvāgbiṃdurūpaṃ hi nādarūpaṃ taduttaram |
tadarvākkarmalokastu tadūrdhvaṃ jñānalokakaḥ || 79 ||

namaskārastadūrdhvaṃ hi madāhaṃkāranāśanaḥ |
janijaṃ vai tirodhānaṃ nāniṣiddhyātate iti || 80 ||

jñānaśabdārtha evaṃ hi tirodhānanivāraṇāt |
tadarvākparivartante hyādhibhautikapūjakāḥ || 81 ||

ādhyātmikārcakā eva tadūrdhvaṃ saṃprayāntivai |
tāvadvai vedibhāgaṃ tanmahālokātmaliṃgake || 82 ||

prakṛtyādyaṣṭabaṃdhopi vedyante saṃpratiṣṭhataḥ |
evametādṛśaṃ jñeyaṃ sarvaṃ laukikavaidikam || 83 ||

adharmamahiṣārūḍhaṃ kālacakraṃ taranti te |
satyādidharmayuktā ye śivapūjāparāśca ye || 84 ||

tadūrdhvaṃ vṛṣabho dharmo brahmacaryasvarūpadhṛk |
satyādipādayuktastu śivalokāgrataḥ sthitaḥ || 85 ||

kṣamāśṛṅgaḥ śamaśrotro vedadhvanivibhūṣitaḥ |
āstikyacakṣurniśvāsagurubuddhimanā vṛṣaḥ || 86 ||

kriyādivṛṣabhā jñeyāḥ kāraṇādiṣu sarvadā |
taṃ kriyāvṛṣabhaṃ dharmaṃ kālātītodhitiṣṭhati || 87 ||

brahmaviṣṇumaheśānāṃ svasvāyurdinamucyate |
tadūrdhvaṃ na dinaṃ rātrirna janmamaraṇādikam || 88 ||

punaḥ kāraṇasatyāntāḥ kāraṇabrahmaṇastathā |
gaṃdhādibhyastu bhūtebhyastadūrdhvaṃ nirmitāḥ sadā || 89 ||

sūkṣmagaṃdhasvarūpā hi sthitā lokāścaturdaśa |
punaḥ kāraṇaviṣṇorvai sthitā lokāścaturdaśa || 90 ||

punaḥkāraṇarudrasya lokāṣṭāviṃśakā matāḥ |
punaśca kāraṇeśasya ṣaṭpaṃcāśattadūrdhvagāḥ || 91 ||

tataḥ paraṃ brahmacaryalokākhyaṃ śivasaṃmatam |
tatraiva jñānakailāse paṃcāvaraṇasaṃyute || 92 ||

paṃcamaṃḍalasaṃyuktaṃ paṃcabrahmakalānvitam |
ādiśaktisamāyuktamādiliṃgaṃ tu tatra vai || 93 ||

śivālayamidaṃ proktaṃ śivasya paramātmanaḥ |
paraśaktyāsamāyuktastatraiva parameśvaraḥ || 94 ||

sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiśca saṃhārastirobhāvopyanugrahaḥ |
paṃcakṛtyapravīṇo .asau saccidānaṃdavigrahaḥ || 95 ||

dhyānadharmaḥ sadā yasya sadānugrahatatparaḥ |
samādhyāsanamāsīnaḥ svātmārāmo virājate || 96 ||

tasya saṃdarśanaṃ sāṃdhyaṃ karmadhyānādibhiḥ kramāt |
nityādikarmayajanācchivakarmamatirbhavet || 97 ||

kriyādiśivakarmabhyaḥ śivajñānaṃ prasādhayet |
taddarśanagatāḥ sarve muktā eva na saṃśayaḥ || 98 ||

muktirātmasvarūpeṇa svātmārāmatvameva hi |
kriyātapojapajñānadhyānadharmeṣu susthitaḥ || 99 ||

śivasya darśanaṃ labdhā svātmārāmatvameva hi |
yathā raviḥ svakiraṇādaśuddhimapaneṣyati || 100 ||

kṛpāvicakṣaṇaḥ śaṃbhurajñānamapaneṣyati |
ajñānavinivṛttau tu śivajñānaṃ pravartate || 101 ||

śivajñānātsvasvarūpamātmārāmatvameṣyati |
ātmārāmatvasaṃsiddhau kṛtakṛtyo bhavennaraḥ || 102 ||

punaśca śatalakṣeṇa brahmaṇaḥ padamāpnuyāt |
punaśca śatalakṣeṇa viṣṇoḥ padamavāpnuyāt || 103 ||

punaśca śatalakṣeṇa rudrasya padamāpnuyāt |
punaśca śatalakṣeṇa aiśvaryaṃ padamāpnuyāt || 104 ||

punaścaivaṃvidhenaiva japena susamāhitaḥ |
śivalokādibhūtaṃ hi kālacakramavāpnuyāt || 105 ||

kālacakraṃ paṃcacakramekaikena kramottare |
sṛṣṭimohau brahmacakraṃ bhogamohau tu vaiṣṇavam || 106 ||

kopamohau raudracakraṃ bhramaṇaṃ caiśvaraṃ viduḥ |
śivacakraṃ jñānamohau paṃcacakraṃ vidurbudhāḥ || 107 ||

punaśca daśakoṭyā hi kāraṇabrahmaṇaḥ padam |
punaśca daśakoṭyā hi tatpadaiśvaryamāpnuyāt || 108 ||

evaṃ krameṇa viṣṇvādeḥ padaṃ labdhvā mahaujasaḥ |
krameṇa tatpadaiśvaryaṃ labdhvā caiva mahātmanaḥ || 109 ||

śatakoṭimanuṃ japtvā paṃcottaramataṃdritaḥ |
śivalokamavāpnoti paṃcamāvaraṇādbahiḥ || 110 ||

rājasaṃ maṃḍapaṃ tatra naṃdīsaṃsthānamuttamam |
taporūpaśca vṛṣabhastatraiva paridṛśyate || 111 ||

sadyojātasya tatsthānaṃ paṃcamāvaraṇaṃ param |
vāmadevasya ca sthānaṃ caturthāvaraṇaṃ punaḥ || 112 ||

aghoranilayaṃ paścāttṛtīyāvaraṇaṃ param |
puruṣasyaiva sāṃbasya dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śubham || 113 ||

īśānasya parasyaiva prathamāvaraṇaṃ tataḥ |
dhyānadharmasya ca sthānaṃ paṃcamaṃ maṃḍapaṃ tataḥ || 114 ||

balināthasya saṃsthānaṃ tatra pūrṇāmṛtapradam |
caturthaṃ maṃḍapaṃ paścāccaṃdraśekharamūrtimat || 115 ||

somaskaṃdasya ca sthānaṃ tṛtīyaṃ maṃḍapaṃ param |
dvitīyaṃ maṃḍapaṃ nṛtyamaṃḍapaṃ prāhurāstikāḥ || 116 ||

prathamaṃ mūlamāyāyāḥ sthānaṃ tatraiva śobhanam |
tataḥ paraṃ garbhagṛhaṃ liṃgasthānaṃ paraṃ śubham || 117 ||

naṃdisaṃsthānataḥ paścānna viduḥ śivavaibhavam |
naṃdīśvaro bahistiṣṭhanpaṃcākṣaramupāsate || 118 ||

evaṃ gurukramāllabdhaṃ naṃdīśācca mayā punaḥ |
tataḥ paraṃ svasaṃvedyaṃ śive naivānubhāvitam || 119 ||

śivasya kṛpayā sākṣācchiva lokasya vaibhavam |
vijñātuṃ śakyate sarvairnānyathetyāhurāstikāḥ || 120 ||

evaṃkrameṇamuktāḥ syurbrāhmaṇā vai jiteṃdriyaḥ |
anyeṣāṃ ca kramaṃ vakṣye gadataḥ śṛṇutādarāt || 121 ||

gurūpadeśājjāpyaṃ vai brāhmaṇānāṃ namo .antakam |
paṃcākṣaraṃ paṃcalakṣamāyuṣyaṃ prajapedvidhiḥ || 122 ||

strītvāpanayanārthaṃ tu paṃcalakṣaṃ japetpunaḥ |
mantreṇa puruṣo bhūtvā kramānmukto bhavedbudhaḥ || 123 ||

kṣatriyaḥ paṃcalakṣeṇa kṣattratvamapaneṣyati |
punaśca paṃcalakṣeṇa kṣattriyo brāhmaṇo bhavet || 124 ||

mantrasiddhirjapāccaiva kramānmukto bhavainnaraḥ |
vaiśyastu paṃcalakṣeṇa vaiśyatvamapaneṣyati || 125 ||

punaśca paṃcalakṣeṇa mantrakṣattriya ucyate |
punaśca paṃcalakṣeṇa kṣattratvamapaneṣyati || 126 ||

punaśca paṃcalakṣeṇa mantrabrāhmaṇa ucyate |
śūdraścaiva namoṃtena paṃcaviṃśatilakṣataḥ || 127 ||

mantravipratvamāpadya paścācchuddho bhaveddvijaḥ |
nārīvātha naro vātha brāhmaṇo vānya eva vā || 128 ||

namontaṃ vā namaḥpūrvamāturaḥ sarvadā japet |
tataḥ strīṇāṃ tathaivohyagururnirdarśayetkramāt || 129 ||

sādhakaḥ paṃcalakṣānte śivaprītyarthameva hi |
mahābhiṣeka naivedyaṃ kṛtvā bhaktāṃśca pūjayet || 130 ||

pūjayā śivabhaktasya śivaḥ prītataro bhavet |
śivasya śivabhaktasya bhedo nāsti śivo hi saḥ || 131 ||

śivasvarūpamantrasya dhāraṇācchiva eva hi |
śivabhaktaśarīre hi śive tatparamo bhavet || 132 ||

śivabhaktāḥ kriyāḥ sarvā vedasarvakriyāṃ viduḥ |
yāvadyāvacchivaṃ mantraṃ yena japtaṃ bhavetkramāt || 133 ||

tāvadvai śivasānnidhyaṃ tasmindehe na saṃśayaḥ |
devīliṃgaṃ bhavedrūpaṃ śivabhaktastriyāstathā || 134 ||

yāvanmantraṃ japeddevyāstāvatsānnidhyamasti hi |
śivaṃ saṃpūjayeddhīmānsvayaṃ vai śabdarūpabhāk || 135 ||

svayaṃ caiva śivo bhūtvā parāṃ śaktiṃ prapūjayet |
śaktiṃ beraṃ ca liṃgaṃ ca hyālekhyā māyayā yajet || 136 ||

śivaliṃgaṃ śivaṃ matvā svātmānaṃ śaktirūpakam |
śaktiliṃgaṃ ca devīṃ ca matvā svaṃ śivarūpakam || 137 ||

śivaliṃgaṃ nādarūpaṃ biṃdurūpaṃ tu śaktikam |
upapradhānabhāvena anyonyāsaktaliṃgakam || 138 ||

pūjayecca śivaṃ śaktiṃ sa śivo mūlabhāvanāt |
śivabhaktāñchivamantrarūpakāñchivarūpakān || 139 ||

ṣoḍaśairupacāraiśca pūjayediṣṭamāpnuyāt |
yena śuśrūṣaṇādyaiśca śivabhaktasya liṃginaḥ || 140 ||

ānaṃdaṃ janayedvidvāñchivaḥ prītataro bhavet |
śivabhaktānsapatnīkānpatnyā saha sadaiva tat || 141 ||

pūjayedbhojanādyaiśca paṃca vā daśa vā śatam |
dhane dehe ca mantre ca bhāvanāyāmavaṃcakaḥ || 142 ||

śivaśaktisvarūpeṇa na punarjāyate bhuvi |
nābheradho brahmabhāgamākaṃṭhaṃ viṣṇubhāgakam || 143 ||

mukhaṃ liṃgamiti proktaṃ śivabhaktaśarīrakam |
mṛtāndāhādiyuktānvā dāhādirahitānmṛtān || 144 ||

uddiśya pūjayedādipitaraṃ śivameva hi |
pūjāṃ kṛtvādimātuśca śivabhaktāṃśca pūjayet || 145 ||

pitṛlokaṃ samāsādyakramānmukto bhavenmṛtaḥ |
kriyāyuktadaśabhyaśca tapoyukto viśiṣyate || 146 ||

tapoyuktaśatebhyaśca japayukto viśiṣyate |
japayuktasahasrebhyaḥ śivajñānī viśiṣyate || 147 ||

śivajñāniṣu lakṣeṣu dhyānayukto viśiṣyate |
dhyānayukteṣu koṭibhyaḥ samādhistho viśiṣyate || 148 ||

uttarottara vai śiṣṭyātpūjāyāmuttarottaram |
phalaṃ vaiśiṣṭyarūpaṃ ca durvijñeyaṃ manīṣibhiḥ || 149 ||

tasmādvai śivabhaktasya māhātmyaṃ vetti ko naraḥ |
śivaśaktyoḥ pūjanaṃ ca śivabhaktasya pūjanam || 150 ||

kurute yo naro bhaktyā sa śivaḥ śivamedhate |
ya imaṃ paṭhate .adhyāyamarthavadvedasaṃmatam || 151 ||

śivajñānī bhavedvipraḥ śivena saha modate |
śrāvayecchivabhaktāṃśca viśeṣajño manīśvarāḥ || 152 ||

śivaprasādaśiddhiḥ syācchivasya kṛpayā budhāḥ // 153 |

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ saptadaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 17 ||

ṛṣya ūcuḥ |

baṃdhamokṣasvarūpaṃ hi brūhi sarvārthavittama |

sūta uvāca |

baṃdhamokṣaṃ tathopāyaṃ vakṣye .ahaṃ śṛṇutādarāt || 1 ||

prakṛtyādyaṣṭabaṃdhena baddho jīvaḥ sa ucyate |
prakṛtyādyaṣṭabaṃdhena nirmukto mukta ucyate || 2 ||

prakṛtyādivaśīkāro mokṣa ityucyate svataḥ |
baddhajīvastu nirmukto muktajīvaḥ sa kathyate || 3 ||

prakṛtyagre tato buddhirahaṃkāro guṇātmakaḥ |
paṃcatanmātramityete prakṛtyādyaṣṭakaṃ viduḥ || 4 ||

prakṛṭyādyaṣṭajo deho dehajaṃ karma ucyate |
punaśca karmajo deho janmakarma punaḥ punaḥ || 5 ||

śarīraṃ trividhaṃ jñeyaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ ca kāraṇam |
sthūlaṃ vyāpāradaṃ proktaṃ sūkṣmamiṃdriyabhogadam || 6 ||

kāraṇaṃ tvātmabhogārthaṃ jīvakarmānurūpataḥ |
sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ puṇyapāpaiḥ karmabhiḥ phalamaśnute || 7 ||

tasmāddhi karmarajjvā hi baddho jīvaḥ punaḥ punaḥ |
śarīratrayakarmabhyāṃ cakravadbhrāmyate sadā || 8 ||

cakrabhramanivṛtyarthaṃ cakrakartāramīḍayet |
prakṛtyādi mahācakraṃ prakṛteḥ parataḥ śivaḥ || 9 ||

cakrakartā maheśo hi prakṛteḥ paratoyataḥ |
pibati vātha vamati jīvanbālo jalaṃ yathā || 10 ||

śivastathā prakṛtyādi vaśīkṛtyādhitiṣṭhati |
sarvaṃ vaśīkṛtaṃ yasmāttasmācchiva iti smṛtaḥ |
śiva eva hi sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaśca niḥspṛhaḥ || 20 ||

sarvajñatā tṛptiranādibodhaḥ svatantratā nityamaluptaśaktiḥ |
anantaśaktiśca maheśvarasya yanmānasaiśvaryamavaiti vedaḥ || 12 ||

ataḥ śivaprasādena prakṛtyādivaśaṃ bhavet |
śivaprasādalābhārthaṃ śivameva prapūjayet || 13 ||

niḥspṛhasya ca pūrṇasya tasya pūjā kathaṃ bhavet |
śivoddeśakṛtaṃ karma prasādajanakaṃ bhavet || 14 ||

liṃge bere bhaktajane śivamuddiśya pūjayet |
kāyena manasā vācā dhanenāpi prapūjayet || 15 ||

pujayā tu maheśo hi prakṛteḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ |
prasādaṃ kurute satyaṃ pūjakasya viśeṣataḥ || 16 ||

śivaprasādātkarmādyaṃ krameṇa svavaśaṃ bhavet |
karmārabhya prakṛtyantaṃ yadāsarvaṃ vaśaṃ bhavet || 17 ||

tadāmukta iti proktaḥ svātmārāmo virājate |
prasādātparameśasya karma deho yadāvaśaḥ || 18 ||

tadā vai śivaloke tu vāsaḥ sālokyamucyate |
sāmīpyaṃ yāti sāṃbasya tanmātre ca vaśaṃ gate || 19 ||

tadā tu śivasāyujyamāyudhādyaiḥ kriyādibhiḥ |
mahāprasādalābhe ca buddhiścāpi vaśā bhavet || 20 ||

buddhistu kāryaṃ prakṛtestatsṛṣṭiriti kathyate |
punarmahāprasādena prakṛtirvaśameṣyati || 21 ||

śivasya mānasaiśvaryaṃ tadā .ayatnaṃ bhaviṣyati |
sārvajñādyaṃ śivaiśvaryaṃ labdhvā svātmani rājate || 22 ||

tatsāyujyamiti prāhurvedāgamaparāyaṇāḥ |
evaṃ krameṇa muktiḥ syālliṃgādau pūjayā svataḥ || 23 ||

ataḥ śivaprasādārthaṃ kriyādyaiḥ pūjayecchivam |
śivakriyā śivatapaḥ śivamantrajapaḥ sadā || 24 ||

śivajñānaṃ śivadhyānamuttarottaramabhyaset |
āsupterāmṛteḥ kālaṃ nayedvai śivaciṃtayā || 25 ||

sadyādibhiśca kusumairarcayecchivameṣyati |

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

liṃgādau śivapūjāyā vidhānaṃ brūhi sarvataḥ || 26 ||

sūta uvāca |

liṃgānāṃ ca kramaṃ vakṣye yathāvacchṛṇuta dvijāḥ |
tadeva liṃgaṃ prathamaṃ praṇavaṃ sārvakāmikam || 27 ||

sūkṣmapraṇavarūpaṃ hi sūkṣmarūpaṃ tu niṣphalam |
sthūlaliṃgaṃ hi sakalaṃ tatpaṃcākṣaramucyate || 28 ||

tayoḥ pūjā tapaḥ proktaṃ sākṣānmokṣaprade ubhe |
pauruṣaprakṛtibhūtāni liṃgānisubahūni ca || 29 ||

tāni vistarato vaktuṃ śivo vetti na cāparaḥ |
bhūvikārāṇi liṃgāni jñātāni prabravīmi vaḥ || 30 ||

svayaṃ bhūliṃgaṃ prathamaṃ biṃduliṃgaṃdvitīyakam |
pratiṣṭhitaṃ caraṃcaiva guruliṃgaṃ tu paṃcamam || 31 ||

devarṣitapasā tuṣṭaḥ sānnidhyārthaṃ tu tatra vai |
pṛthivyantargataḥ śarvo bījaṃ vai nādarūpataḥ || 32 ||

sthāvarāṃkuravadbhūmimudbhidya vyakta eva saḥ |
svayaṃbhūtaṃ jātamiti svayaṃbhūriti taṃ viduḥ || 33 ||

talliṃgapūjayā jñānaṃ svayameva pravarddhate |
suvarṇarajatādau vā pṛthivyāṃ sthiṃḍilepi vā || 34 ||

svahastāllikhitaṃ liṃgaṃ śuddhapraṇavamantrakam |
yantraliṃgaṃ samālikhya pratiṣṭhāvāhanaṃ caret || 35 ||

biṃdunādamayaṃ liṃgaṃ sthāvaraṃ jaṃgamaṃ ca yat |
bhāvanāmayametaddhi śivadṛṣṭaṃ na saṃśayaḥ || 36 ||

yatra viśvasya te śaṃbhustatra tasmai phalapradaḥ |
svahastāllikhyate yantre sthāvarādāvakṛtrime || 37 ||

āvāhya pūjayecchaṃbhuṃ ṣoḍaśairupacārakaiḥ |
svayamaiśvaryamāpnoti jñānamabhyāsato bhavet || 38 ||

devaiśca ṛṣibhiścāpi svātmasiddhyarthameva hi |
samantreṇātmahastena kṛtaṃ yacchuddhamaṃḍale || 39 ||

śuddhabhāvanayā caiva sthāpitaṃ liṃgamuttamam |
talliṃgaṃ pauruṣaṃ prāhustatpratiṣṭhitamucyate || 40 ||

talliṃgapūjayā nityaṃ pauruṣaiśvaryamāpnuyāt |
mahadbhirbrāhmaṇaiścāpi rājabhiśca mahādhanaiḥ || 41 ||

śilpinākalpitaṃ liṃgaṃ mantreṇa sthāpitaṃ ca yat |
pratiṣṭhitaṃ prākṛtaṃ hi prākṛtaiśvaryabhogadam || 42 ||

yadūrjitaṃ ca nityaṃ ca taddhi pauruṣamucyate |
yaddurbalamanityaṃ ca taddhi prākṛtamucyate || 43 ||

liṃgaṃ nābhistathā jihvā nāsāgrañca śikhā kramāt |
kaṭyādiṣu trilokeṣu liṃgamādhyātmikaṃ caram || 44 ||

parvataṃ pauruṣaṃ proktaṃ bhūtalaṃ prākṛtaṃ viduḥ |
vṛkṣādi pauruṣaṃ jñeyaṃ gulmādi prākṛtaṃ viduḥ || 45 ||

ṣāṣṭikaṃ prākṛtaṃ jñeyaṃ śāligodhūmapauruṣam |
aiśvaryaṃ pauruṣaṃ vidyādaṇimādyaṣṭasiddhidam || 46 ||

sustrīdhanādiviṣayaṃ prākṛtaṃ prāhurāstikāḥ |
prathamaṃ caraliṃgeṣu rasaliṃgaṃ prakathyate || 47 ||

rasaliṃgaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ sarvābhīṣṭapradaṃ bhavet |
bāṇaliṃgaṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahārājyapradaṃ śubham || 48 ||

svarṇaliṃgaṃ tu vaiśyānāṃ mahādhanapatitvadam |
śilāliṃgaṃ tu śūdrāṇāṃ mahāśuddhikaraṃ śubham || 49 ||

sphāṭikaṃ bāṇaliṃgaṃ ca sarveṣāṃsarvakāmadam |
svīyābhāve .anyadīyaṃ tu pūjāyāṃ na niṣiddhyate || 50 ||

strīṇāṃ tu pārthivaṃ liṃgaṃ sabhartṝṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ |
vidhavānāṃ pravṛttānāṃ sphāṭikaṃ parikīrtitam || 51 ||

vidhavānāṃ nivṛttānāṃ rasaliṃgaṃ viśiṣyate |
bālyevāyauvanevāpi vārddhakevāpi suvratāḥ || 52 ||

śuddhasphaṭikaliṃgaṃ tu strīṇāṃ tatsarvabhogadam |
pravṛttānāṃ pīṭhapūjā sarvābhīṣṭapradā bhuvi || 53 ||

pātreṇaiva pravṛttastu sarvapūjāṃ samācaret |
abhiṣekānte naivedyaṃ śālyannena samācaret || 54 ||

pūjānte sthāpayelliṃgaṃ saṃpuṭeṣu pṛthaggṛhe |
karapūjāni vṛttānāṃ svabhojyaṃ tu nivedayet || 55 ||

nivṛttānāṃ paraṃ sūkṣmaliṃgameva viśiṣyate |
vibhūtyabhyarcanaṃ kuryādvibhūtiṃ ca nivedayet || 56 ||

pūjāṃ kṛtvātha talliṃgaṃ śirasā dhārayetsadā |
vibhūtistrividhā proktā lokavedaśivāgnibhiḥ || 57 ||

lokāgnijamatho bhasmadravyaśuddhyarthamāvahet |
mṛddāruloharūpāṇāṃ dhānyānāṃ ca tathaiva ca || 58 ||

tilādīnāṃ ca dravyāṇāṃ vastrādīnāṃ tathaiva ca |
tathā paryuṣitānāṃ ca bhasmanā śiddhiriṣyate || 59 ||

śvādibhirdūṣitānāṃ ca bhasmanā śuddhiriṣyate |
sajalaṃ nirjalaṃ bhasma yathāyogyaṃ tu yojayet || 60 ||

vedāgnijaṃ tathā bhasma tatkarmānteṣu dhārayet |
mantreṇa kriyayā janyaṃ karmāgnau bhasmarūpadhṛk || 61 ||

tadbhasmadhāraṇātkarma svātmanyāropitaṃ bhavet |
aghoreṇātmamantreṇa bilvakāṣṭhaṃ pradāhayet || 62 ||

śivāgniriti saṃproktastena dagdhaṃ śivāgnijam |
kapilāgomayaṃ pūrvaṃ kevalaṃ gavyameva vā || 63 ||

śamyasvatthapalāśānvā vaṭāramvadhabilvakān |
śivāgninā dahecchuddhaṃ tadvai bhasma śivāgnijam || 64 ||

darbhāgnau vā dahetkāṣṭhaṃ śivamantraṃ samuccaran |
samyaksaṃśodhya vastreṇa navakuṃbhe nidhāpayet || 65 ||

dīptyarthaṃ tattu saṃgrāhyaṃ manyate pūjyatepi ca |
bhasmaśabdārtha evaṃ hi śivaḥ pūrvaṃ tathā .akarot || 66 ||

yathā svaviṣaye rājā sāraṃ gṛhṇāti yatkaram |
yathā manuṣyāḥ sasyādīndagdhvā sāraṃ bhajanti vai || 67 ||

yathā hi jāṭharāgniśca bhakṣyādīnvividhānbahūn |
dagdhvā sārataraṃ sārātsvadehaṃ paripuṣyati || 68 ||

tathā prapaṃcakartāpi sa śivaḥ parameśvaraḥ |
svādhiṣṭheyaprapaṃcasya dagdhvā sāraṃ gṛhītavān || 69 ||

dagdhvā prapaṃcaṃ tadbhasm asvātmanyāropayacchivaḥ |
uddhūlanena vyājena jagatsāraṃ gṛhītavān || 70 ||

svaratnaṃ sthāpayāmāsa svakīye hi śarīrake |
keśamākāśasāreṇa vāyusāreṇa vai mukham || 71 ||

hṛdayaṃ cāgnisāreṇa tvapāṃ sāreṇa vaikaṭim |
jānu cāvanisāreṇa tadvatsarvaṃ tadaṃgakam || 72 ||

brahmaviṣṇvośca rudrāṇāṃ sāraṃ caiva tripuṃḍrakam |
tathā tilakarūpeṇa lalāṭānte maheśvaraḥ || 73 ||

bhavṛddhyā sarvametaddhi manyate svayamaityasau |
prapaṃcasārasarvasvamanenaiva vaśīkṛtam || 74 ||

tasmādasya vaśīkartā nāstīti sa śivaḥ smṛtaḥ |
yathā sarvamṛgāṇāṃ ca hiṃsako mṛgahiṃsakaḥ || 75 ||

asya hiṃsāmṛgo nāsti tasmātsiṃha itīritaḥ |
śaṃ nityaṃ sukhamānaṃdamikāraḥ puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ || 76 ||

vakāraḥ śaktiramṛtaṃ melanaṃ śiva ucyate |
tasmādevaṃ svamātmānaṃ śivaṃ kṛtvārcayecchivam || 77 ||

tasmāduddhūlanaṃ pūrvaṃ tripuṃḍraṃ dhārayetparam |
pūjākāle hi sajalaṃ śuddhyarthaṃ nirjalaṃ bhavet || 78 ||

divā vā yadi vārātrau nārī vātha naropi vā |
pūjārthaṃ sajalaṃ bhasma tripuṃḍreṇaiva dhārayet || 79 ||

tripuṃḍraṃ sajalaṃ bhasma dhṛtvā pūjāṃ karoti yaḥ |
śivapūjāṃ phalaṃ sāṃgaṃ tasyaiva hi suniścitam || 80 ||

bhasma vai śivamantreṇa dhṛtvā hyatyāśramī bhavet |
śivāśramīti saṃproktaḥ śivaikaparamo yataḥ || 81 ||

śivavrataikaniṣṭhasya nāśaucaṃ na ca sūtakam |
lalāṭe .agre sitaṃ bhasma tilakaṃ dhārayenmṛdā || 82 ||

svahastādguruhastādvāśivabhaktasya lakṣaṇam |
guṇānruṃdha iti prokto guruśabdasya vigrahaḥ || 83 ||

savikārānrājasādīnguṇānruṃdhe vyapohati |
guṇātītaḥ paraśivo gururūpaṃ samāśritaḥ || 84 ||

guṇatrayaṃ vyapohyāgre śivaṃ bodhayatīti saḥ |
viśvastānāṃ tu śiṣyāṇāṃ gururityabhidhīyate || 85 ||

tasmādguruśarīraṃ tu guruliṃgaṃ bhavedbudhaḥ |
guruliṃgasya pūjā tu guruśuśrūṣaṇaṃ bhavet || 86 ||

śrutaṃ karoti śuśrūṣā kāyena manasā girā |
uktaṃ yadguruṇā pūrvaṃ śakyaṃ vā .aśakyameva vā || 87 ||

karotyeva hi pūtātmā prāṇairapi dhanairapi |
tasmādvai śāsane yogyaḥ śiṣya ityabhidhīyate || 88 ||

śarīrādyarthakaṃ sarvaṃ gurordattvā suśiṣyakaḥ |
agrapākaṃ nivedyāgrebhuṃjīyādgurvanujñayā || 89 ||

śiṣyaḥ putra iti proktaḥ sadāśiṣyatvayogataḥ |
jihvāliṃgānmantraśukraṃ karṇayonau niṣicyavai || 90 ||

jātaḥ putro mantraputraḥ pitaraṃ pūjayedgurum |
nimajjayati putraṃ vai saṃsāre janakaḥ pitā || 91 ||

santārayati saṃsārādgururvai bodhakaḥ pitā |
ubhayorantaraṃ jñātvā pitaraṃ gurumarcayet || 92 ||

aṃgaśuśrūṣayā cāpi dhanādyaiḥ svārjitairgurum |
pādādikeśaparyantaṃ liṃgānyaṃgāni yadguroḥ || 93 ||

dhanarūpaiḥ pādukādyaiḥ pādasaṃgraṇādibhiḥ |
snānābhiṣekanaivedyairbhojanaiśca prapūjayet || 94 ||

gurupūjaiva pūjā syācchivasya paramātmanaḥ |
guruśeṣaṃ tu yatsarvamātmaśuddhikaraṃ bhavet || 95 ||

guroḥ śeṣaḥ śivocchiṣṭaṃ jalamannādinirmitam |
śiṣyāṇāṃ śivabhaktānāṃ grāhyaṃ bhojyaṃ bhaveddvijāḥ || 96 ||

gurvanujñāvirahitaṃ coravatsakalaṃ bhavet |
gurorapi viśeṣajñaṃ yatnādgṛhṇīta vai gurum || 97 ||

ajñānamocanaṃ sādhyaṃ viśeṣajño hi mocakaḥ |
ādau ca vighnaśamanaṃ kartavyaṃ karma pūrtaye || 98 ||

nirvighnena kṛtaṃ sāṃgaṃ karma vai saphalaṃ bhavet |
tasmātsakalakarmādau vighneśaṃ pūjayed budhaḥ || 99 ||

sarvabādhānivṛttyarthaṃ sarvāndevānyajedbudhaḥ |
jvarādigranthirogāśca bādhā hyādhyātmikā matā || 100 ||

piśācajaṃbukādīnāṃ valmīkādyudbhave tathā |
akasmādeva godhādijantūnāṃ patanepi ca || 101 ||

gṛhe kacchapasarpastrīdurjanādarśanepi ca |
vṛkṣanārīgavādīnāṃ prasūtiviṣayepi ca || 102 ||

bhāviduḥkhaṃ samāyāti tasmātte bhautikā matā |
amedhyā śanipātaśca mahāmārī tathaiva ca || 103 ||

jvaramārī viṣūciśca gomārī ca masūrikā |
janmarkṣagrahasaṃkrāntigrahayogāḥ svarāśike || 104 ||

duḥsvapnadarśanādyāśca matā vai hyadhidaivikāḥ |
śavacāṃḍālapatitasparśādyeṃtargṛhe gate || 105 ||

etādṛśe samutpanne bhāviduḥkhasya sūcake |
śāntiyajñaṃ tu matimānkuryāttaddoṣaśāntaye || 106 ||

devālaye .atha goṣṭhe vā caitye vāpi gṛhāṃgaṇe |
prādeśonnatadhiṣṇye vai dvihaste ca svalaṃkṛte || 107 ||

bhāramātravrīhidhānyaṃ prasthāpya parisṛtya ca |
madhye vilikhyakamalaṃ tathā dikṣuvilikhya vai || 108 ||

tantunā veṣṭitaṃ kuṃbhaṃ navagugguladhūpitam |
madhye sthāpya mahākuṃbhaṃ tathā dikṣvapi vinyaset || 109 ||

sanālāmrakakūrcādīnkalaśāṃśca tathāṣṭasu |
pūrayenmantrapūtena paṃcadravyayutena hi || 110 ||

prakṣipennava ratnāni nīlādīnkramaśastathā |
karmajñaṃ ca sapatnīkamācāryaṃ varayedbudhaḥ || 111 ||

suvarṇapratimāṃ viṣṇoriṃdrādīnāṃ ca nikṣipet |
saśiraske madhyakuṃbhe viṣṇumābāhya pūjayet || 112 ||

prāgādiṣu yathāmantramiṃdrādīnkramaśo yajet |
tattannāmnā caturthyāṃ ca namonte na yathākramam || 113 ||

āvāhanādikaṃ sarvamācāryeṇaiva kārayet |
ācārya ṛtvijā sārdhaṃ tanmātrānprajapecchatam || 114 ||

kuṃbhasya paścime bhāge japānte homamācaret |
koṭiṃ lakṣaṃ sahasraṃ vā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ budhāḥ || 115 ||

ekāhaṃ vā navāhaṃ vā tathā maṃḍalameva vā |
yathāyogyaṃ prakurvīta kāladeśānusārataḥ || 116 ||

śamīhomaśca śāntyarthe vṛttyarthe ca palāśakam |
samidannājyakairdravyairnāmnā mantreṇa vā hunet || 117 ||

prāraṃbhe yatkṛtaṃ dravyaṃ tatkriyāntaṃ samācaret |
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvānte dine saṃprokṣyayejjalaiḥ || 118 ||

brāhmaṇānbhojayetpaścādyāvadāhutisaṃkhyayā |
ācāryaśca haviṣyāśīṛtvijaśca bhavedbudhāḥ || 119 ||

ādityādīngrahāniṣṭvā sarvahomānta eva hi |
ṛtvibhyo dakṣiṇāṃ dadyānnavaratnaṃ yathākramam || 120 ||

daśadānaṃ tataḥ kuryādbhūridānaṃ tataḥ param |
bālānāmupanītānāṃ gṛhiṇāṃ vanināṃ dhanam || 121 ||

kanyānāṃ ca sabhartṝṇāṃ vidhavānāṃ tataḥ param |
tantropakaraṇaṃ sarvamācāryāya nivedayet || 122 ||

utpātānāṃ ca mārīṇāṃ duḥkhasvāmī yamaḥ smṛtaḥ |
tasmādyamasya prītyarthaṃ kāladānaṃ pradāpayet || 123 ||

śataniṣkeṇa vā kuryāddaśaniṣkeṇa vā punaḥ |
pāśāṃkuśadharaṃ kālaṃ kuryātpuruṣarūpiṇam || 124 ||

tatsvarṇapratimādānaṃ kuryāddakṣiṇayā saha |
tiladānaṃ tataḥ kuryātpūrṇāyuṣyaprasiddhaye || 125 ||

ājyāvekṣaṇadānaṃ ca kuryādvyādhinivṛttaye |
sahasraṃ bhojayedviprāndaridraḥ śatameva vā || 126 ||

vittābhāve daridrastu yathāśakti samācaret |
bhairavasya mahāpūjāṃ kuryādbhūtādiśāntaye || 127 ||

mahābhiṣekaṃ naivedyaṃ śivasyānte tukārayet |
brāhmaṇānbhojayetpaścādbhūribhojanarūpataḥ || 128 ||

evaṃ kṛtena yajñena doṣaśāntimavāpnuyāt |
śāntiyajñamimaṃ kuryādvarṣe varṣe tu phālgune || 129 ||

durdarśanādau sadyo vai māsamātre samācaret |
mahāpāpādisaṃprāptau kuryādbhairavapūjanam || 130 ||

mahāvyādhisamutpattau saṃkalpaṃ punarācaret |
sarvabhāve daridrastu dīpadānamathācaret || 131 ||

tadapyaśaktaḥ snātvā vai yatkiṃciddānamācaret |
divākaraṃ namaskuryānmantreṇāṣṭottaraṃ śatam || 132 ||

sahasramayutaṃ lakṣaṃ koṭiṃ vā kārayed budhaḥ |
namaskārātmayajñena tuṣṭāḥ syuḥ sarvadevatāḥ || 133 ||

tvatsvarūperpitā buddhirnate .aśūnye ca rocati |
yā cāstyasmadahanteti tvayi dṛṣṭe vivarjitā || 134 ||

namro .ahaṃ hi svadehena bho mahāṃstvamasi prabho |
na śūnyo matsvarūpo vai tava dāso .asmi sāṃpratam || 135 ||

yathāyogyaṃ svātmayajñaṃ namaskāraṃ prakalpayet |
athātra śivanaivedyaṃ dattvā tāṃbūlamāharet || 136 ||

śivapradakṣiṇaṃ kuryātsvayamaṣṭottaraṃ śatam |
sahasramayutaṃ lakṣaṃ koṭimanyena kārayet || 137 ||

śivapradakṣiṇātsarvaṃ pātakaṃ naśyati kṣaṇāt |
duḥkhasya mūlaṃ vyādhirhi vyādhermūlaṃ hi pātakam || 138 ||

dharmeṇaiva hi pāpānāmapanodanamīritam |
śivoddeśakṛto dharmaḥ kṣamaḥ pāpavinodane || 139 ||

adhyakṣaṃ śivadharmeṣu pradakṣiṇamitīritam |
kriyayā japarūpaṃ hi praṇavaṃ tu pradakṣiṇam || 140 ||

jananaṃ maraṇaṃ dvaṃdvaṃ māyācakramitīritam |
śivasya māyācakraṃ hi balipīṭhaṃ taducyate || 141 ||

balipīṭhaṃ samārabhya prādakṣiṇyakrameṇa vai |
pade padāntaraṃ gatvā balipīṭhaṃ samāviśet || 142 ||

namaskāraṃ tataḥ kuryātpradakṣiṇamitīritam |
nirgamājjananaṃ prāptaṃ namastvātmasamarpaṇam || 143 ||

jananaṃ maraṇaṃ dvaṃdvaṃ śivamāyāsamarpitam |
śivamāyārpitadvaṃdvo na punastvātmabhāgbhavet || 144 ||

yāvaddehaṃ kriyādhīnaḥ sajīvo baddha ucyate |
dehatrayavaśīkāre mokṣa ityucyate budhaiḥ || 145 ||

māyācakrapraṇetā hi śivaḥ paramakāraṇam |
śivamāyārpitadvaṃdvaṃ śivastu parimārjati || 146 ||

śivena kalpitaṃ dvaṃdvaṃ tasminneva samarpayet |
śivasyātipriyaṃ vidyātpradakṣiṇaṃ namo budhāḥ || 147 ||

pradakṣiṇanamaskārāḥ śivasya paramātmanaḥ |
ṣoḍaśairupacāraiśca kṛtapūjā phalapradā || 148 ||

pradakṣiṇā .avināśyaṃ hi pātakaṃ nāsti bhūtale |
tasmātpradakṣiṇenaiva sarvapāpaṃ vināśayet || 149 ||

śivapūjāparo maunī satyādiguṇasaṃyutaḥ |
kriyātapojapajñānadhyāneṣvekaikamācaret || 150 ||

aiśvaryaṃ divyadehaśca jñānamajñānasaṃśayaḥ |
śivasānnidhyamityete kriyādīnāṃ phalaṃ bhavet || 151 ||

karaṇena phalaṃ yāti tamasaḥ parihāpanāt |
janmanaḥ parimārjitvājjñabuddhyā janitāni ca || 152 ||

yathādeśaṃ yathākālaṃ yathādehaṃ yathādhanam |
yathāyogyaṃ prakurvīta kriyādīñchivabhaktimān || 153 ||

nyāyārjitasuvittena vasetprājñaḥ śivasthale |
jīvahiṃsādirahitamatikleśavivarjitam || 154 ||

paṃcākṣareṇa japtaṃ ca toyamannaṃ viduḥ sukham |
athavā .ahurdaridrasya bhikṣānnaṃjñānadaṃ bhavet || 155 ||

śivabhaktasya bhikṣānnaṃśivabhaktivivardhanam |
śaṃbhusatramiti prāhurbhikṣānnaṃśivayoginaḥ || 156 ||

yena kenāpyupāyena yatra kutrāpi bhūtale |
śuddhānnabhuksadā maunīrahasyaṃ na prakāśayet || 157 ||

prakāśayettu bhaktānāṃ śivamāhātmyameva hi |
rahasyaṃ śivamantrasya śivo jānāti nāparaḥ || 158 ||

śivabhakto vasennityaṃ śivaliṃgaṃ samāśritaḥ |
sthāṇuliṃgāśrayeṇaiva sthāṇurbhavati bhūsurāḥ || 159 ||

pūjayā caraliṃgasya kramānmukto bhaveddhruvam |
sarvamuktaṃ samāsena sādhyasādhanamuttamam || 160 ||

vyāsena yatpurāproktaṃ yacchrutaṃ hi mayā purā |
bhadramastu hi vo .asmākaṃ śivabhaktirdṛḍhā .astusā || 161 ||

ya imaṃ paṭhate .adhyāyaṃ yaḥ śṛṇoti naraḥ sadā |
śivajñānaṃ sa labhateśivasya kṛpayā budhāḥ || 162 ||

iti śrīśaivemahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ sādhyasādhanakhaṃḍe śivaliṃgamahimāvarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭādaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 18 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

sūta sūta ciraṃjīva dhanyastvaṃ śivabhaktimān |
samyaguktastvayā liṃgamahimā satphalapradaḥ || 1 ||

yatra pārthivamāheśaliṃgasya mahimādhunā |
sarvotkṛṣṭaśca kathito vyāsato brūhi taṃ punaḥ || 2 ||

sūta uvāca |

śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ sarve sadbhaktyā harato khilāḥ |
śivapārthivaliṃgasya mahimā procyate mayā || 3 ||

ukteṣveteṣu liṃgeṣu pārthivaṃ liṃgamuttamam |
tasya pūjanato viprā bahavaḥ siddhimāgatāḥ || 4 ||

harirbrahmā ca ṛṣayaḥ saprajāpatayastathā |
saṃpūjya pārthivaṃ liṃgaṃ prāpuḥsarvepsitaṃ dvijāḥ || 5 ||

devāsuramanuṣyāśca gaṃdharvoragarākṣasāḥ |
anyepi bahavastaṃ saṃpūjya siddhiṃ gatāḥ param || 6 ||

kṛte ratnamayaṃ liṃgaṃ tretāyāṃ hemasaṃbhavam |
dvāpare pāradaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ pārthivaṃ tu kalau yuge || 7 ||

aṣṭamūrtiṣu sarvāsu mūrtirvai pārthivī varā |
ananyapūjitā viprāstapastasmānmahatphalam || 8 ||

yathā sarveṣu deveṣu jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭho maheśvaraḥ |
evaṃ sarveṣu liṃgeṣu pārthivaṃ śreṣṭamucyate || 9 ||

yathā nadīṣu sarvāsu jyeṣṭhā śreṣṭhā surāpagā |
tathā sarveṣu liṃgeṣu pārthivaṃ śreṣṭhamucyate || 10 ||

yathā sarveṣu mantreṣu praṇavo hi mahānsmṛtaḥ |
tathedaṃ pārthivaṃ śreṣṭhamārādhyaṃ pūjyameva hi || 11 ||

yathā sarveṣu varṇeṣu brāhmaṇaḥśreṣṭha ucyate |
tathā sarveṣu liṃgeṣu pārthivaṃ śreṣṭhamucyate || 12 ||

yathā purīṣu sarvāsu kāśīśreṣṭhatamā smṛtā |
tathā sarveṣu liṃgeṣu pārthivaṃ śreṣṭhamucyate || 13 ||

yathā vrateṣu sarveṣu śivarātrivrataṃ param |
tathā sarveṣu liṃgeṣu pārthivaṃ śreṣṭhamucyate || 14 ||

yathā devīṣu sarvāsu śaivīśaktiḥ parāsmṛtā |
tathā sarveṣu liṃgeṣu pārthivaṃ śreṣṭhamucyate || 15 ||

prakṛtyapārthivaṃ liṃgaṃ yonyadevaṃ prapūjayet |
vṛthā bhavati sā pūjā snānadānādikaṃ vṛthā || 16 ||

pārthivārādhanaṃ puṇyaṃ dhanyamāyurvivardhanam |
tuṣṭidaṃ puṣṭidaṃśrīdaṃ kāryaṃ sādhakasattamaiḥ || 17 ||

yathā labdhopacāraiśca bhaktyā śraddhāsamanvitaḥ |
pūjayetpārthivaṃ liṃgaṃ sarvakāmārthasiddhidam || 18 ||

yaḥ kṛtvā pārthivaṃ liṃge pūjayecchubhavedikam |
ihaiva dhanavāñchrīmānante rudro bhijāyate || 19 ||

trisaṃdhyaṃ yorcayaṃlliṃgaṃ kṛtvā bilvena pārthivam |
daśaikādaśakaṃyāvattasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu || 20 ||

anenaiva svadehena rudraloke mahīyate |
pāpahaṃ sarvamartyānāṃ darśanātsparśanādapi || 21 ||

jīvanmuktaḥ sa vaijñānī śiva eva na saṃśayaḥ |
tasya darśanamātreṇa bhuktirmuktiśca jāyate || 22 ||

śivaṃ yaḥ pūjayennityaṃ kṛtvā liṃgaṃ tu pārthivam |
yāvajjīvanaparyantaṃ sa yāti śivamandiram || 23 ||

mṛḍenāpramitānvarṣāñchivalokehi tiṣṭhati |
sakāmaḥ punarāgatya rājendro bhārate bhavet || 24 ||

niṣkāmaḥ pūjayennityaṃ pārthivaṃliṃgamuttamam |
śivaloke sadā tiṣṭhettataḥ sāyujyamāpnuyāt || 25 ||

pārthivaṃ śivaliṃgaṃ ca vipro yadi na pūjayet |
sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ śūlaprotaṃ sudāruṇam || 26 ||

yathākathaṃcidvidhinā ramyaṃ liṃgaṃ prakārayet |
paṃcasūtravidhānāṃ ca pārthivena vicārayet || 27 ||

akhaṇḍaṃ taddhi kartavyaṃ na vikhaṇḍaṃ prakārayet |
dvikhaṇḍaṃ tu prakurvāṇo naiva pūjāphalaṃ labhet || 28 ||

ratnajaṃ hemajaṃ liṃgaṃ pāradaṃ sphāṭikaṃ tathā |
pārthivaṃ puṣparāgotthamakhaṃḍaṃ tu prakārayet || 29 ||

akhaṃḍaṃ tu caraṃ liṃgaṃ dvikhaṃḍamacaraṃ smṛtam |
khaṃḍākhaṃḍavicāroyaṃ sacarācarayoḥ smṛtaḥ || 30 ||

vedikā tu mahāvidyā liṃgaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ |
ato hi sthāvare liṃge smṛtā śreṣṭhādikhaṃḍitā || 31 ||

dvikhaṃḍaṃ sthāvaraṃ liṃgaṃ kartavyaṃ hi vidhānataḥ |
akhaṃḍaṃ jaṃgamaṃ proktaṃś aivasiddhāntavedibhiḥ || 32 ||

dvikhaṃḍaṃ tu carāṃ liṃgaṃ kurvantyajñānamohitāḥ |
naiva siddhāntavettāro munayaḥ śāstrakovidāḥ || 33 ||

akhaṃḍaṃ sthāvaraṃ liṃgaṃ dvikhaṃḍaṃ carameva ca |
yekurvantinarāmūḍhānapūjāphalabhāginaḥ || 34 ||

tasmācchāstroktavidhinā akhaṃḍaṃ carasaṃjñakam |
dvikhaṃḍaṃ sthāvaraṃ liṃgaṃ kartavyaṃ parayā mudā || 35 ||

akhaṃḍe tu care pūjā sampūrṇaphaladāyinī |
dvikhaṃḍe tu care pūjāmahāhānipradā smṛtā || 36 ||

akhaṃḍe sthāvare pūjā na kāmaphaladāyinī |
pratyavāyakarī nityamityuktaṃ śāstravedibhiḥ || 37 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ sādhyasādhanakhaṃḍe pārthivaśivaliṃgapūjanamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonaviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 19 ||

sūta uvāca |

atha vaidikabhaktānāṃ pārthivārcāṃ nigadyate |
vaidikenaiva mārgeṇa bhuktimuktipradāyinī || 1 ||

sūtroktavidhinā snātvā saṃdhyāṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi |
brahmayajñaṃ vidhāyādau tatastarppaṇamācaret || 2 ||

naityikaṃ sakalaṃ kāmaṃ vidhāyānantaraṃ pumān |
śivasmaraṇapūrvaṃ hi bhasmarudrākṣadhārakaḥ || 3 ||

vedoktāvidhinā samyaksaṃpūrṇaphalasiddhaye |
pūjayetparayā bhaktyā pārthivaṃ liṃgamuttamam || 4 ||

nadītīre taḍāge ca parvate kānane .api ca |
śivālaye śucau deśe pārthivārcā vidhīyate || 5 ||

śuddhapradeśasaṃbhūtāṃ mṛdamāhṛtya yatnataḥ |
śivaliṃgaṃ prakalpeta sāvadhānatayā dvijāḥ || 6 ||

vipre gaurā smṛtā śoṇā bāhuje pītavarṇakā |
vaiśye kṛṣṇā pādajāte hyathavā yatra yā bhavet || 7 ||

saṃgṛhya mṛttikāṃ liṃganirmāṇārthaṃ prayatnataḥ |
atīva śubhadeśe ca sthāpayettāṃ mṛdaṃ śubhām || 8 ||

saṃśodhya ca jalenāpi piṃḍīkṛtya śanaiḥ śanaiḥ |
vidhīyeta śubhaṃ liṃgaṃ pārthivaṃ vedamārgataḥ || 9 ||

tataḥ saṃpūjayedbhaktyā bhuktimuktiphalāptaye |
tatprakāramahaṃ vacmi śṛṇudhvaṃ saṃvidhānataḥ || 10 ||

namaḥ śivāya mantreṇārcanadravyaṃ ca prokṣayet |
bhūrasīti ca mantreṇa kṣetrasiddhiṃ prakārayet || 11 ||

āposmāniti mantreṇa jalasaṃskāramācaret |
namaste rudramantreṇa phāṭikābaṃdhamucyate || 12 ||

śaṃbhavāyeti mantreṇa kṣetraśuddhiṃ prakārayet |
namaḥ pūrveṇa kuryātpaṃcāmṛtasyāpi prokṣaṇam || 13 ||

nīlagrīvāya mantreṇa namaḥpūrveṇa bhaktimān |
carecchaṃkaraliṃgasya pratiṣṭhāpanamuttamam || 14 ||

bhaktitastata etatte rudrāyeti ca mantrataḥ |
āsanaṃ ramaṇīyaṃ vai dadyādvaidikamārgakṛt || 15 ||

māno mahantamiti ca mantreṇāvāhanaṃ caret |
yāte rudreṇa mantreṇa saṃcaredupaveśanam || 16 ||

mantreṇa yāmiṣumiti nyāsaṃ kuryyācchivasya ca |
adhyavocaditi premṇādhivāsaṃ manunācaret || 17 ||

manunā saujīva iti devatānyāsamācaret |
asau yovasarpatīti cācaredapasarpaṇam || 18 ||

namostu nīlagrīvāyeti pādyaṃ manunāharet |
arghyaṃ ca rudragāyatryā .acamanaṃ tryaṃbakeṇa ca || 19 ||

payaḥ pṛthivyāmiti ca payasā snānamācaret |
dadhikrāvṇetimantreṇa dadhisnānaṃ ca kārayet || 20 ||

ghṛṭaṃ snāne khalu ghṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ yāveti mantrataḥ |
madhuvātā madhunaktaṃ madhumānna iti tryṛcā || 21 ||

madhukhaṃḍasnapanaṃ proktamiti paṃcāmṛtaṃ smṛtam |
athavā pādyamantreṇa snānaṃ paṃcāmṛtena ca || 22 ||

mānastoke iti premṇā mantreṇa kaṭibaṃdhanam |
namo dhṛṣṇave iti vā uttarīyaṃ ca dhāpayet || 23 ||

yā te hetiriti premṇā ṛkcatuṣkeṇa vaidikaḥ |
śivāya vidhinā bhaktaścaredvastrasamarpaṇam || 24 ||

namaḥ śvabhya iti premṇā gaṃdhaṃ dadyādṛcā sudhīḥ |
namastakṣabhya iti cākṣatānmantreṇa cārpayet || 25 ||

namaḥ pāryāya iti vā puṣpa mantreṇa cārpayet |
namaḥ parṇyāya iti vā bilbapatrasamarpaṇam || 26 ||

namaḥ kapardine ceti dhūpaṃ dadyādyathāvidhi |
dīpaṃ dadyādyathoktaṃ tu nama āśava ityṛcā || 27 ||

namo jyeṣṭhāya mantreṇa dadyānnaivedyamuttamam |
manunā tryambakamiti punarācamanaṃ smṛtam || 28 ||

imā rudrāyeti ṛcā kuryātphalasamarpaṇam |
namo vrajyāyeti ṛcā sakalaṃ śaṃbhaverpayet || 29 ||

māno mahāntamiti ca mānastoke iti tataḥ |
mantradvayenaikadaśākṣatai rudrānprapūjayet || 30 ||

hiraṇyagarbha iti tryṛcā dakṣiṇāṃ hi samarpayet |
devasya tveti mantreṇa hyabhiṣekaṃ caredbudhaḥ || 31 ||

dīpamantreṇa vā śaṃbhornīrājanavidhiṃ caret |
puṣpāṃjaliṃ caredbhaktyā imā rudrāya ca tryṛcā || 32 ||

māno mahāntamiti ca caretprājñaḥ pradakṣiṇām |
mānastoketi mantreṇa sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇametsudhīḥ || 33 ||

eṣate iti mantreṇa śivamudrāṃ pradarśayet |
yatoyata ityabhayāṃ jñānākhyāṃ tryaṃbakeṇa ca || 34 ||

namaḥseneti mantreṇa mahāmudrāṃ pradarśayet |
darśayeddhenumudrāṃ ca namo gobhya ṛcānayā || 35 ||

paṃcamudrāḥ pradarśyātha śivamantrajapaṃ caret |
śatarudriyamantreṇa japedvedavicakṣaṇaḥ || 36 ||

tataḥ paṃcāṅgapāṭhaṃ ca kuryyādvedavicakṣaṇaḥ |
devāgātviti mantreṇa kuryācchaṃbhorvisarjanam || 37 ||

ityuktaḥ śivapūjāyā vyāsato vaidikovidhiḥ |
samāsataśca śṛṇuta vaidikaṃ vidhimuttamam || 38 ||

ṛcā sadyojātamiti mṛdāharaṇamācaret |
vāmadevāya iti ca jalaprakṣepamācaret || 39 ||

aghoreṇa ca mantreṇa liṃganirmāṇamācaret |
tatpuruṣāya mantreṇāhvānaṃ kuryādyathāvidhi || 40 ||

saṃyojayedvedikāyāmīśānamanunā haram |
anyatsarvaṃ vidhānaṃ ca kuryyātsaṃkṣepataḥ sudhīḥ || 41 ||

paṃcākṣareṇa mantreṇa gurudattena vā tathā |
kuryātpūjāṃ ṣoḍaśopacāreṇa vidhivatsudhīḥ || 42 ||

bhavāya bhavanāśāya mahādevāya dhīmahi |
ugrāya ugranāśāya śarvāya śaśimauline || 43 ||

anena manunā vāpi pūjayecchaṃkaraṃ sudhīḥ |
subhaktyā ca bhramaṃ tyaktvā bhaktyaiva phaladaḥ śivaḥ || 44 ||

ityapi proktamādṛtya vaidikakramapūjanam |
procyatenyavidhiḥ samyaksādhāraṇatayā dvijaḥ || 45 ||

pūjā pārthivaliṃgasya saṃproktā śivanāmabhiḥ |
tāṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ sarvakāmapradāyinīm || 46 ||

haro maheśvaraḥ śaṃbhuḥ śūlapāṇiḥ pinākadhṛk |
śivaḥ paśupatiścaiva mahādeva iti kramāt || 47 ||

mṛdāharaṇasaṃghaṭṭapratiṣṭhāhvānameva ca |
snapanaṃ pūjanaṃ caiva kṣamasveti visarjanam || 48 ||

oṃkārādicaturthyantairnamontairnāmabhiḥ kramāt |
kartavyā ca kriyā sarvā bhaktyā paramayā mudā || 49 ||

kṛtvā nyāsavidhiṃ samyakṣaḍaṅgakarayostathā |
ṣaḍakṣareṇa mantreṇa tato dhyānaṃ samācaret || 50 ||

kailāsapīṭhāsanamadhyasaṃsthaṃ bhaktaiḥ sanaṃdādibhirarcyamānam |
bhaktārtidāvānalamaprameyaṃ dhyāyedumāliṃgitaviśvabhūṣaṇam || 51 ||

dhyāyennityaṃ maheśaṃ rajatagirinibhaṃ cārucaṃdrāvataṃsaṃ ratnākalpojjvalāṃgaṃ paraśumṛgavarābhītihastaṃ prasannam |
padmāsīnaṃ samantātsthitamamaragaṇairvyāghrakṛttiṃ vasānaṃ viśvādyaṃ viśvabījaṃ nikhilabhayaharaṃ paṃcavaktraṃ trinetram || 52 ||

iti dhyātvā ca saṃpūjya pārthivaṃ liṃgamuttamam |
japetpaṃcākṣaraṃ mantraṃ gurudattaṃ yathāvidhi || 53 ||

stutibhiścaiva deveśaṃ stuvīta praṇamansudhīḥ |
nānābhidhābhirviprendrāḥ paṭhedvai śatarudriyam || 54 ||

tataḥ sākṣatapuṣpāṇi gṛhītvāṃjalinā mudā |
prārthayecchaṃkaraṃ bhaktyā mantrairebhiḥ subhaktitaḥ || 55 ||

tāvakastvadguṇaprāṇastvaccittohaṃ sadā mṛḍa |
kṛpānidha iti jñātvā bhūtanātha prasīda me || 56 ||

ajñānādyadi vā jñānājjapa pūjādikaṃ mayā |
kṛtaṃ tadastu saphalaṃ kṛpayā tava śaṃkara || 57 ||

ahaṃ pāpī mahānadya pāvanaśca bhavānmahān |
iti vijñāya gaurīśa yadicchasi tathā kuru || 58 ||

vedaiḥ purāṇaiḥ siddhāntairṛṣibhirvividhairapi |
na jñātosi mahādeva kutohaṃ tvaṃ mahāśiva || 59 ||

yathā tathā tvadīyosmi sarvabhāvairmaheśvara |
rakṣaṇīyastvayāhaṃ vai prasīda parameśvara || 60 ||

ityevaṃ cākṣatānpuṣpānāropya ca śivopari |
praṇamedbhaktitaśśaṃbhuṃ sāṣṭāṃgaṃ vidhivanmune || 61 ||

tataḥ pradakṣiṇāṃ kuryādyathoktavidhinā sudhīḥ |
punaḥ stuvīta deveśaṃ stutibhiḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ || 62 ||

tato galaravaṃ kṛtvā praṇamecchucinamradhīḥ |
kuryādvijñaptimādṛtya visarjanamathācaret || 63 ||

ityuktā muniśārdūlāḥ pārthivārcā vidhānataḥ |
bhuktidā muktidā caiva śivabhaktivivardhinī || 64 ||

ityadhyāyaṃ sucittena yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādapi |
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmāsarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt || 65 ||

āyurāyogyadaṃ caiva yaśasyaṃ svargyameva ca |
putrapautrādisukhadamākhyānamidamuttamam || 66 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe pra.. vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ sādhyasādhanakhaṇḍe pārthivaśivaliṃgapūjāvidhivarṇanaṃ nāma viṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 20 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

sūta sūta mahābhāga vyāsaśiṣya namostu te |
samyaguktaṃ tvayā tāta pārthivārcāvidhānakam || 1 ||

kāmanābhedamāśritya saṃkhyāṃ brūhi vidhānataḥ |
śivapārthivaliṃgānāṃ kṛpayā dīnavatsala || 2 ||

sūta uvāca |

śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ sarve pārthivārcāvidhānakam |
yasyānuṣṭhānamātreṇa kṛtakṛtyo bhavennaraḥ || 3 ||

akṛtvā pārthivaṃ liṃgaṃ yonyadevaṃ prapūjayet |
vṛthā bhavati sā pūjā damadānādikaṃ vṛthā || 4 ||

saṃkhyā pārthivaliṃgānāṃ yathākāmaṃ nigadyate |
saṃkhyā sadyo muniśreṣṭha niścayena phalapradā || 5 ||

prathamāvāhanaṃ tatra pratiṣṭhā pūjanaṃ pṛthak |
liṃgākāraṃ samaṃ tatra sarvaṃ jñeyaṃ pṛthakpṛthak || 6 ||

vidyārthī puruṣaḥ prītyā sahasramitapārthivam |
pūjayecchivaliṃgaṃ hi niścayāttatphalapradam || 7 ||

naraḥ pārthivaliṃgānāṃ dhanārthī ca tadarddhakam |
putrārthī sārddhasāhasraṃ vastrārthī śatapaṃcakram || 8 ||

mokṣārthī koṭiguṇitaṃ bhūkāmaśca sahasrakam |
dayārthī ca trisāhasraṃ tīrthārthī dvisahasrakam || 9 ||

suhṛtkāmī trisāhasraṃ vaśyārthī śatamaṣṭakam |
māraṇārthī saptaśataṃ mohanārthī śatāṣṭakam || 10 ||

uccāṭanaparaścaiva sahasraṃ ca yathoktataḥ |
staṃbhanārthī sahasraṃ tu dveṣaṇārthī tadarddhakam || 11 ||

nigaḍānmuktikāmastu sahasraṃ sarddhamuttamam |
mahārājabhaye paṃcaśataṃ jñeyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ || 12 ||

caurādisaṃkaṭe jñeyaṃ pārthivānāṃ śatadvayam |
ḍākinyādibhaye paṃcaśatamuktaṃ japārthivam || 13 ||

dāridrye paṃcasāhasramayutaṃ sarvakāmadam |
atha nityavidhiṃ vakṣye śṛṇudhvaṃ munisattamāḥ || 14 ||

ekaṃ pāpaharaṃ proktaṃ dviliṃgaṃ cārthasiddhidam |
triliṃgaṃ sarvakāmānāṃ kāraṇaṃ paramīritam || 15 ||

uttarottaramevaṃ syātpūrvoktagaṇanāvidhi |
matāntaramatho vakṣye saṃkhyāyāṃ munibhedataḥ || 16 ||

liṃgānāmayutaṃ kṛtvā pārthivānāṃ subuddhimān |
nirbhayo hi bhavennūnaṃ mahārājabhayaṃ haret || 17 ||

kārāgṛhādimuktyarthamayutaṃ kārayedbudhaḥ |
ḍākinyādibhaye saptasahasraṃ kārayettathā || 18 ||

sahasrāṇi paṃcapaṃcāśadaputraḥ prakārayet |
liṃgānāmayutenaiva kanyakāsantatiṃ labhet || 19 ||

liṃgānāmayutenaiva viṣṇvādaiśvaryamāpnuyāt |
liṃgānāṃ prayutenaiva hyatulāṃ śriyamāpnuyāt || 20 ||

koṭimekāṃ tu liṃgānāṃ yaḥ karoti naro bhuvi |
śiva eva bhavetsopi nātra kāryyā vicāraṇā || 21 ||

arcā pārthivaliṃgānāṃ koṭiyajñaphalapradā |
bhuktidā muktidā nityaṃ tataḥ kāmarthināṃ nṛṇām || 22 ||

vinā liṃgārcanaṃ yasya kālo gacchati nityaśaḥ |
mahāhānirbhavettasya durvṛttasya durātmanaḥ || 23 ||

ekataḥ sarvadānāni vratāni vividhāni ca |
tīrthāni niyamā yajñā liṃgārcā caikataḥ smṛtā || 24 ||

kalau liṃgārcanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tathā loke pradṛśyate |
tathā nāstīti śāstrāṇāmeṣa siddhāntaniścayaḥ || 25 ||

bhuktimuktipradaṃ liṃgaṃ vividhāpannivāraṇam |
pūjayitvā naro nityaṃ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt || 26 ||

śivānāmamayaṃ liṃgaṃ nityaṃ pūjyaṃ maharṣibhiḥ |
yataśca sarvaliṃgeṣu tasmātpūjyaṃ vidhānataḥ || 27 ||

uttamaṃ madhyamaṃ nīcaṃ trividhaṃ liṃgamīritam |
mānato muniśārdūlāstacchṛṇudhvaṃ vadāmyaham || 28 ||

caturaṃgulamucchrāyaṃ ramyaṃ vedikayā yutam |
uttamaṃ liṃgamākhyātaṃ munibhiḥ śāstrakovidaiḥ || 29 ||

tadarddhaṃ madhyamaṃ proktaṃ tadarddhamaghamaṃ smṛtam |
itthaṃ trividhamākhyātamuttarottarataḥ param || 30 ||

anekaliṃgaṃ yo nityaṃ bhaktiśraddhāsamanvitaḥ |
pūjayetsa labhetkāmānmanasā mānasepsitān || 31 ||

na liṃgārādhanādanyatpuṇyaṃ vedacatuṣṭaye |
vidyate sarvaśāstrāṇāmeṣa eva viniścayaḥ || 32 ||

sarvametatparityajya karmajālamaśeṣataḥ |
bhaktyā paramayā vidvĀlliṃgamekaṃ prapūjayet || 33 ||

liṃgercitercitaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṃgamam |
saṃsārāṃbudhimagnānāṃ nānyattāraṇasādhanam || 34 ||

ajñānatimirāṃdhānāṃ viṣayāsaktacetasām |
plavo nānyosti jagati liṃgārādhanamantarā || 35 ||

haribrahmādayo devā munayo yakṣarākṣasāḥ |
gaṃdharvāścaraṇāssiddhā daiteyā dānavāstathā || 36 ||

nāgāḥ śeṣaprabhṛtayo garuḍādyāḥkhagāstathā |
saprajāpatayaścānye manavaḥ kinnarā narāḥ || 37 ||

pūjayitvā mahābhaktyā liṃgaṃ sarvārthasiddhidam |
prāptāḥ kāmānabhīṣṭāṃśca tāṃstānsarvānhṛdi sthitān || 38 ||

brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ śūdro vā pratilomajaḥ |
pūjayetsatataṃ liṃgaṃ tattanmantreṇa sādaram || 39 ||

kiṃ bahūktena munayaḥ strīṇāmapi tathānyataḥ |
adhikārosti sarveṣāṃ śivaliṃgārcane dvijāḥ || 40 ||

dvijānāṃ vaidikenāpi mārgeṇārādhanaṃ varam |
anyeṣāmapi jantūnāṃ vaidikena na saṃmatam || 41 ||

vaidikānāṃ dvijānāṃ ca pūjā vaidikamārgataḥ |
kartavyānānyamārgeṇa ityāha bhagavāñchivaḥ || 42 ||

dadhīcigautamādīnāṃ śāpenādagdhacetasām |
dvijānāṃ jāyate śraddhānaiva vaidikakarmaṇi || 43 ||

yo vaidikamanādṛtya karma smārtamathāpi vā |
anyatsamācarenmartyo na saṃkalpaphalaṃ labhet || 44 ||

itthaṃ kṛtvārcanaṃ śaṃbhornaivedyāntaṃ vidhānataḥ |
pūjayedaṣṭamūrtīśca tatraiva trijaganmayīḥ || 45 ||

kṣitirāponalo vāyurākāśaḥ sūryyasomakau |
yajamāna iti tvaṣṭau mūrtayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ || 46 ||

śarvo bhavaśca rudraśca ugrobhīma itīśvaraḥ |
mahādevaḥ paśupatiretānmūrtibhirarcayet || 47 ||

pūjayetparivāraṃ ca tataḥ śaṃbhoḥ subhaktitaḥ |
īśānādikramāttatra caṃdanākṣatapatrakaiḥ || 48 ||

īśānaṃ naṃdinaṃ caṃḍaṃ mahākālaṃ ca bhṛṃgiṇam |
vṛṣaṃ skaṃdaṃ kapardīśaṃ somaṃ śukraṃ ca tatkramāt || 49 ||

agrato vīrabhadraṃ ca pṛṣṭhe kīrtimukhaṃ tathā |
tata ekādaśānrudrānpūjayedvidhinā tataḥ || 50 ||

tataḥ paṃcākṣaraṃ japtvā śatarudriyameva ca |
stutīrnānāvidhāḥ kṛtvā paṃcāṃgapaṭhanaṃ tathā || 51 ||

tataḥ pradakṣiṇāṃ kṛtvā natvā liṃgaṃ visarjayet |
iti proktamaśeṣaṃ ca śivapūjanamādarāt || 52 ||

rātrāvudaṅmukhaḥ kuryāddevakāryaṃ sadaiva hi |
śivārcanaṃ sadāpyevaṃ śuciḥ kuryādudaṅmukhaḥ || 53 ||

na prācīmagrataḥ śaṃbhornodīcīṃ śaktisaṃhitān |
na pratīcīṃ yataḥ pṛṣṭhamato grāhyaṃ samāśrayet || 54 ||

vinā bhasmatripuṃḍreṇa vinā rudrākṣamālayā |
bilvapatraṃ vinā naiva pūjayecchaṃkaraṃ budhaḥ || 55 ||

bhasmāprāptau muniśreṣṭhāḥ pravṛtte śivapūjane |
tasmānmṛdāpi kartavyaṃ lalāṭe ca tripuṃḍrakam || 56 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe prathamāyāṃ vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ sādhyasādhanakhaṇḍe pārthivapūjanavarṇanaṃ nāmaikaviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 21 ||

ṛṣya ūcuḥ |

agrāhyaṃ śivanaivedyamiti pūrvaṃ śrutaṃ vacaḥ |
brūhi tannirṇayaṃ bilvamāhātmyamapi sanmune || 1 ||

sūta uvāca |

śṛṇudhvaṃ munayaḥ sarve sāvadhānatayādhunā |
sarvaṃ vadāmi saṃprītyā dhanyā yūyaṃ śivavratāḥ || 2 ||

śivabhaktaḥ śuciḥ śuddhaḥ sadvratīdṛḍhaniścayaḥ |
bhakṣayecchivanaivedyaṃ tyajedagrāhyabhāvanām || 3 ||

dṛṣṭvāpi śivanaivedye yānti pāpāni dūrataḥ |
bhakte tu śivanaivedye puṇyānyā yānti koṭiśaḥ || 4 ||

alaṃ yāgasahasreṇāpyalaṃ yāgārbudairapi |
bhakṣite śivanaivedye śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt || 5 ||

yadgṛhe śivanaivedyapracāropi prajāyate |
tadgṛhaṃ pāvanaṃ sarvamanyapāvanakāraṇam || 6 ||

āgataṃ śivanaivedyaṃ gṛhītvā śirasā mudā |
bhakṣaṇīyaṃ prayatne na śivasmaraṇapūrvakam || 7 ||

āgataṃ śivanaivedyamanyadā grāhyamityapi |
vilaṃbe pāpasaṃbaṃdho bhavatyeva hi mānave || 8 ||

na yasya śivanaivedyagrahaṇecchā prajāyate |
sapāpiṣṭho gariṣṭhaḥ syānnarakaṃ yātyapi dhruvam || 9 ||

hṛdaye candrakānte ca svarṇarūpyādinirmite |
śivadīkṣāvatā bhaktenedaṃ bhakṣyamitīryyate || 10 ||

śivadīkṣānvito bhakto mahāprasādasaṃjñakam |
sarveṣāmapi liṃgānāṃ naivedyaṃ bhakṣayecchubham || 11 ||

anyadīkṣāyujāṃ nṝṇāṃ śivabhaktiratātmanām |
śṛṇudhvaṃ nirṇayaṃprītyāśivanaivedyabhakṣaṇe || 12 ||

śālagrāmodbhave liṃge rasaliṃge tathā dvijāḥ |
pāṣāṇe rājate svarṇe surasiddhapratiṣṭhite || 13 ||

kāśmīre sphāṭike rātne jyotirliṃgeṣu sarvaśaḥ |
cāndrāyaṇasamaṃ proktaṃ śaṃbhornaivedyabhakṣaṇam || 14 ||

brahmahāpi śucirbhūtvā nirmālyaṃ yastu dhārayet |
bhakṣayitvā drutaṃ tasya sarvapāpaṃ praṇaśyati || 15 ||

caṃḍādhikāro yatrāsti tadbhāktavyaṃ na mānavaiḥ |
caṃḍādhikāro no yatra bhoktavyaṃ tacca bhaktitaḥ || 16 ||

bāṇaliṃge ca lauhe ca siddhe liṃge svayaṃbhuvi |
pratimāsu ca sarvāsu na caṃḍodhikṛto bhavet || 17 ||

snāpayitvā vidhānena yo liṃgasnāpanodakam |
triḥpibettrividhaṃ pāpaṃ tasyehāśu vinaśyati || 18 ||

agrāhyaṃ śivanaivedyaṃ patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ jalam |
śālagrāmaśilāsaṃgātsarvaṃ yāti pavitritām || 19 ||

loṃgopari ca yaddravyaṃ tadagrāhyaṃ munīśvarāḥ |
supavitraṃ ca tajjñeyaṃ yalliṃgasparśabāhyataḥ || 20 ||

naivedyanirṇayaḥ prokta itthaṃ vo munisattamāḥ |
śṛṇudhvaṃ bilvamāhātmyaṃ sāvadhānatayā .adarāt || 21 ||

mahādevasvarūpoyaṃ bilvo devairapi stutiḥ |
yathākathaṃcidetasya mahimā jñāyate katham || 22 ||

puṇyatīrthāni yāvanti lokeṣu prathitānyapi |
tāni sarvāṇi tīrthānibilvamūleva santi hi || 23 ||

bilvamūle mahādevaṃ liṃgarūpiṇamavyayam |
yaḥ pūjayati puṇyātmā sa śivaṃ prāpnuyāddhruvam || 24 ||

bilvamūle jalairyastu mūrddhānamabhiṣiṃcati |
sa sarvatīrthasnātaḥ syātsa eva bhuvi pāvanaḥ || 25 ||

etasya bilvamūlasyāthālavālamanuttamam |
jalākulaṃ mahādevo dṛṣṭvā tu ṣṭobhavatyalam || 26 ||

pūjayedbilvamūlaṃ yo gaṃdhapuṣpādibhirnaraḥ |
śivalokamavāpnoti santatirvarddhate sukham || 27 ||

bilvamūle dīpamālāṃ yaḥ kalpayati sādaram |
sa tattvajñānasaṃpanno maheśāntargato bhavet || 28 ||

bilvaśākhāṃ samādāya hastena navapallavam |
gṛhītvā pūjayedbilvaṃ sa ca pāpaiḥ pramucyate || 29 ||

bilvamūle śivarataṃ bhojayedyastu bhaktitaḥ |
ekaṃ vā koṭiguṇitaṃ tasya puṇyaṃ prajāyate || 30 ||

bilvamūle kṣīramuktamannamājyena saṃyutam |
yo dadyācchivabhaktāya sa daridro na jāyate || 31 ||

sāṃgopāṃgamiti proktaṃ śivaliṃgaprapūjanam |
pravṛttānāṃ nivṛttānāṃ bhedato dvividhaṃ dvijāḥ || 32 ||

pravṛttānāṃ pīṭhapūjāṃ sarvapūjāṃ samācaret |

abhiṣekānte naivedyaṃ śālyannena samācaret |
pūjānte sthāpayelliṃgaṃ puṭe śuddhe pṛthaggṛhe || 34 ||

karapūjānivṛttānāṃ svabhojyaṃ tu nivedayet |
nivṛttānāṃ paraṃ sūkṣmaṃ liṃgameva viśiṣyate || 35 ||

vibhūtyabhyarcanaṃ kuryādvibhūtiṃ ca nivedayet |
pūjāṃ kṛtvā tathā liṃgaṃ śirasādhārayetsadā || 36 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ sādhyasādhanakhaṇḍe śivanaivedyavarṇanonāmadvāviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 22 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

sūta sūta mahābhāga vyāsaśiṣya namostu te |
tadeva vyāsato brūhi bhasmamāhātmyamuttamam || 1 ||

tathā rudrākṣamāhātmyaṃ nāma māhātmyamuttamam |
tritayaṃ brūhi suprītyā mamānaṃdayacetasam || 2 ||

sūta uvāca |

sādhupṛṣṭaṃ bhavadbhiśca lokānāṃ hitakārakam |
bhavanto vai mahādhanyāḥ pavitrāḥ kulabhūṣaṇāḥ || 3 ||

yeṣāṃ caiva śivaḥ sākṣāddaivataṃ paramaṃ śubham |
sadā śivakathā loke vallabhā bhavatāṃ sadā || 4 ||

te dhanyāśca kṛtārthāśca saphalaṃ dehadhāraṇam |
uddhṛtañca kulaṃ teṣāṃ ye śivaṃ samupāsate || 5 ||

mukhe yasya śivanāma sadāśivaśiveti ca |
pāpāni na spṛśantyeva khadirāṃgāraṃkayathā || 6 ||

śrīśivāya namastubhyaṃ mukhaṃ vyāharate yadā |
tanmukhaṃ pāvanaṃ tīrthaṃ sarvapāpavināśanam || 7 ||

tanmukhañca tathā yo vai paśyatiprītimānnaraḥ |
tīrthajanyaṃ phalaṃ tasya bhavatīti suniścitam || 8 ||

yatra trayaṃ sadā tiṣṭhedetacchubhataraṃ dvijā |
tasya darśanamātreṇa veṇīsnānaphalaṃlabhet || 9 ||

śivanāmavibhūtiśca tathā rudrākṣa eva ca |
etattrayaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ triveṇīsadṛśaṃ smṛtam || 10 ||

etattrayaṃ śarīre ca yasya tiṣṭhati nityaśaḥ |
tasyaiva darśanaṃ loke durlabhaṃ pāpahārakam || 11 ||

taddarśanaṃ yathā veṇī nobhayorantaraṃ manāk |
evaṃ yonavijānāti sapāpiṣṭho na saṃśayaḥ || 12 ||

vibhūtiryasya no bhāle nāṃge rudrākṣadhāraṇam |
nāsye śivamayī vāṇī taṃ tyajedadhamaṃ yathā || 13 ||

śaivaṃ nāma yathā gaṃgā vibhūtiryamunā matā |
rudrākṣaṃ vidhinā proktā sarvapāpāvināśinī || 14 ||

śarīre ca trayaṃ yasya tatphalaṃ caikataḥ sthitam |
ekato veṇikāyāśca snānajantuphalaṃ budhaiḥ || 15 ||

tadevaṃ tulitaṃ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇāhitakāriṇā |
samānaṃ caiva tajjātaṃ tasmāddhāryaṃ sadā budhaiḥ || 16 ||

taddinaṃ hi samārabhya brahmaviṣṇvādibhiḥ saraiḥ |
dhāryate tritayaṃ tacca darśanātpāpahārakam || 17 ||

ṛṣya ūcuḥ |

īdṛśaṃ hi phalaṃ proktaṃ nāmāditritayodbhavam |
tanmāhātmyaṃ viśeṣeṇa vaktumarhasi suvrata || 18 ||

sūta uvāca |

ṛṣayo hi mahāprājñāḥ sacchaivā jñānināṃ varāḥ |
tanmāhātmyaṃ hi sadbhaktyā śṛṇutādarato dvijāḥ || 19 ||

sugūḍhamapi śāstreṣu purāṇeṣu śrutiṣvapi |
bhavatsnehānmayā viprāḥ prakāśaḥ kriyate .adhunā || 20 ||

kastattritayamāhātmyaṃ saṃjānāti dvijottamāḥ |
maheśvaraṃ vinā sarvaṃ brahmāṇḍe sadasatparam || 21 ||

vacmyahaṃ nāma māhātmyaṃ yathābhakti samāsataḥ |
śṛṇuta prītito viprāḥ sarvapāpaharaṃ param || 22 ||

śiveti nāmadāvāgnermahāpātakaparvatāḥ |
bhasmībhavantyanāyāsātsatyaṃsatyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ || 23 ||

pāpamūlāni duḥkhāni vividhānyapi śaunaka |
śivanāmaikanaśyāni nānyanaśyāni sarvathā || 24 ||

sa vaidikaḥ sa puṇyātmā sa dhanyassa budho mataḥ |
śivanāmajapāsakto yo nityaṃ bhuvi mānava || 25 ||

bhavanti vividhā dharmāsteṣāṃ sadyaḥ phalonmukhāḥ |
yeṣāṃ bhavati viśvāsaḥ śivanāmajape mune || 26 ||

pātakāni vinaśyanti yāvanti śivanāmataḥ |
bhuvi tāvanti pāpāni kriyante na narairmune || 27 ||

brahmahatyādipāpānāṃ rāśīnapramitānmune |
śivanāma drutaṃ proktaṃ nāśayatyakhilānnaraiḥ || 28 ||

śivanāmatarīṃ prāpya saṃsārābdhiṃ taranti ye |
saṃsāramūlapāpāni tāni naśyantyasaṃśayam || 29 ||

saṃsāramūlabhūtānāṃ pātakānāṃ mahāmune |
śivanāmakuṭhāreṇa vināśo jāyate dhruvam || 30 ||

śivanāmāmṛtaṃ peyaṃ pāpadāvānalārditaiḥ |
pāpadāvāgnitaptānāṃ śāntistena vinā na hi || 31 ||

śiveti nāmapīyūṣavarṣadhārāpariplutāḥ |
saṃsāradavamadhyepi na śocanti kadācana || 32 ||

śivanāmni mahadbhaktirjātā yeṣāṃ mahātmanām |
tadvidhānāṃ tu sahasā muktirbhavati sarvathā || 33 ||

anekajanmabhiryena tapastaptaṃ munīśvara |
śivanāmni bhavedbhaktiḥ sarvapāpāpahāriṇī || 34 ||

yasyā sādhāraṇaṃ śaṃbhunāmni bhaktirakhaṃḍitā |
tasyaiva mokṣaḥ sulabho nānyasyeti matirmama || 35 ||

kṛtvāpyanekapāpāni śivanāmajapādaraḥ |
sarvapāpavinirmukto bhavatyeva na saṃśayaḥ || 36 ||

bhavanti bhasmasādvṛkṣā davadagdhā yathā vane |
tathā tāvanti dagdhāni pāpāni śivanāmataḥ || 37 ||

yo nityaṃ bhasmapūtāṃgaḥ śivanāmajapādaraḥ |
santaratyeva saṃsāraṃ saghoramapi śaunaka || 38 ||

brahmasvaharaṇaṃ kṛtvā hatvāpi brāhmaṇānbahūn |
na lipyate naraḥ pāpaiḥ śivanāmajapādaraḥ || 39 ||

vilokya vedānakhilāñchivanāmajapaḥ param |
saṃsāratāraṇopāya iti pūrvairviniścitaḥ || 40 ||

kiṃ bahūktyā muniśreṣṭhāḥ ślokenaikena vacmyaham |
śivanāmno mahimānaṃ sarvapāpāpahāriṇam || 41 ||

pāpānāṃ haraṇe śaṃbhornāmaḥ śaktirhi pāvanī |
śaknoti pātakaṃ tāvatkartuṃ nāpi naraḥ kvacit || 42 ||

śivanāmaprabhāveṇa lebhe sadgatimuttamām |
indradyumnanṛpaḥ pūrvaṃ mahāpāpaḥ purāmune || 43 ||

tathā kāciddvijāyoṣā sau mune bahupāpinī |
śivanāmaprabhāveṇa lebhe sadgatimuttamām || 44 ||

ityuktaṃ vo dvijaśreṣṭhā nāmamāhātmyamuttamam |
śṛṇudhvaṃ bhasmamāhātmyaṃ sarvapāvanapāvanam || 45 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ sādhyasādhanakhaṇḍe śivanamamāhātmyavarṇanonāmatrayoviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 23 ||

sūta uvāca |

dvividhaṃ bhasma saṃproktaṃ sarvamaṃgaladaṃ param |
tatprakāramahaṃ vakṣye sāvadhānatayā śṛṇu || 1 ||

ekaṃ jñeyaṃ mahābhasma dvitīyaṃ svalpasaṃjñakam |
mahābhasma iti proktaṃ bhasma nānāvidhaṃ param || 2 ||

tadbhasma trividhaṃ proktaṃ śrotaṃ smārtaṃ ca laukikam |
bhasmaiva svalpasaṃjñaṃ hi bahudhā parikīrtitam || 3 ||

śrautaṃ bhasma tathā smārtaṃ dvijānāmeva kīrtitam |
anyeṣāmapi sarveṣāmaparaṃ bhasma laukikam || 4 ||

dhāraṇaṃ mantrataḥ proktaṃ dvijānāṃ munipuṃgavaiḥ |
kevalaṃ dhāraṇaṃ jñeyamanyeṣāṃ mantravarjitam || 5 ||

āgneyamucyate bhasma dagdhagomayasaṃbhavam |
tadāpi dravyamityuktaṃ tripuṃḍrasya mahāmune || 6 ||

agnihotrotthitaṃ bhasmasaṃgrāhyaṃ vā manīṣibhiḥ |
anyayajñotthitaṃ vāpi tripuṇḍrasya ca dhāraṇe || 7 ||

agnirityādibhirmantrairjābālopaniṣadgateḥ |
saptabhidhūlanaṃ kāryaṃ bhasmanā sajalena ca || 8 ||

varṇānāmāśramāṇāṃ ca mantrato mantratopi ca |
tripuṃḍroddhūlanaṃ proktajābālairādareṇa ca || 9 ||

bhasmanoddhūlanaṃ caiva yathā tiryaktripuṃḍrakam |
pramādādapi mokṣārthī na tyajediti viśrutiḥ || 10 ||

śivena viṣṇunā caiva tathā tiryaktripuṃḍrakam |
umādevī ca lakṣmīṃśca vācānyābhiśca nityaśaḥ || 11 ||

brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyairvaiśyaiḥ śūdrairapi ca saṃskaraiḥ |
apabhraṃśairdhṛtaṃ bhasmatripuṃḍroddhūlanātmanā || 12 ||

uddhūlanaṃ tripuṃḍraṃ ca śraddhayā nācaranti ye |
teṣāṃ nāsti samācāro varṇāśramasamanvitaḥ || 13 ||

uddhūlanaṃ tripuṃḍraṃ ca śraddhayā nācaranti ye |
teṣāṃ nāsti vinirmuktissaṃsārājjanmakoṭibhiḥ || 14 ||

uddhūlanaṃ tripuṃḍraṃ ca śraddhayā nācaranti ye |
teṣāṃ nāsti śivajñānaṃ kalpakoṭiśatairapi || 15 ||

uddhūlanaṃ tripuṃḍraṃ ca śraddhayā nācaranti ye |
te mahāpātakairyuktā iti śāstrīyanirṇayaḥ || 16 ||

uddhūlanaṃ tripuṃḍraṃ ca śraddhayā nācaranti ye |
teṣāmācaritaṃ sarvaṃ viparītaphalāya hi || 17 ||

mahāpātakayuktānāṃ jantūnāṃ śarvavidviṣām |
tripuṃḍroddhūlanadveṣo jāyate sudṛḍhaṃ mune || 18 ||

śivāgnikāryaṃ yaḥ kṛtvā kuryāttriyāyuṣātmavit |
mucyate sarvapāpaistu spṛṣṭena bhasmanā naraḥ || 19 ||

sitena bhasmanā kuryyāttrisandhyaṃ yastripuṇḍrakam |
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śivena saha modate || 20 ||

sitena bhasmanā kuryāllāṭe tu tripuṇḍrakam |
yo sāvanādibhūtānhi lokānāpto mṛto bhavet || 21 ||

akṛtvā bhasmanā snānaṃ na japedvai ṣaḍakṣaram |
tripuṃḍraṃ ca racitvā tu vidhinā bhasmanā japet || 22 ||

adayo vādhamo vāpi sarvapāpānvitopi vā |
uṣaḥpāpānvito vāpi mūrkho vā patitopi vā || 23 ||

yasmindeśeva sennityaṃ bhūtiśāsanasaṃyutaḥ |
sarvatīrthaiśca kratubhiḥ sāṃnidhyaṃ kriyate sadā || 24 ||

tripuṃḍrasahito jīvaḥ pūjyaḥ sarvaiḥ surāsuraiḥ |
pāpānvitopi śuddhātmā kiṃ punaḥ śraddhayā yutaḥ || 25 ||

yasmindeśe śivajñānī bhūtiśāsanasaṃyutaḥ |
gato yadṛcchayādyāpi tasmistīrthāḥ samāgatāḥ || 26 ||

bahunātra kimuktena dhāryaṃ bhasma sadā budhaiḥ |
liṃgārcanaṃ sadā kāryaṃ japyo mantraḥ ṣaḍakṣaraḥ || 27 ||

brahmaṇā viṣṇunā vāpi rudreṇa munibhiḥ suraiḥ |
bhasmadhāraṇamāhātmyaṃ na śakyaṃ paribhāṣitum || 28 ||

iti varṇāśramācāro luptavarṇakriyopi ca |
pāpātsakṛttripuṃḍrasya dhāraṇātsopi mucyate || 29 ||

ye bhasmadhāriṇaṃ tyaktvā karma kurvanti mānavāḥ |
teṣāṃ nāsti vinirmokṣaḥ saṃsārājjanmakoṭibhiḥ || 30 ||

te nādhītaṃ guroḥ sarvaṃ te na sarvamanuṣṭhitam |
yena vipreṇa śirasi tripuṃḍraṃ bhasmanā kṛtam || 31 ||

ye bhasmadhāriṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā narāḥ kurvanti tāḍanam |
teṣāṃ caṃḍālato janma brahmannūhyaṃ vipaścitā || 32 ||

mānastokena mantreṇa mantritaṃ bhasma dhārayet |
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaścaiva prokteṣvaṃgeṣu bhaktimān || 33 ||

vaiśyastriyaṃ bakenaiva śūdraḥ paṃcākṣareṇa tu |
anyāsāṃ vidhavāstrīṇāṃ vidhiḥ proktaśca śūdravat || 34 ||

paṃcabrahmādimanubhirgṛhasthasya vidhīyate |
triyaṃbakena manunā vidhirvai brahmacāriṇaḥ || 35 ||

aghoreṇātha manunā vipinasthavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |
yatistu praṇavenaiva tripuṃḍrādīni kārayet || 36 ||

ativarṇāśramī nityaṃ śivohaṃ bhāvanātparāt |
śivayogī ca niyatamīśānenāpi dhārayet || 37 ||

na tyājyaṃ sarvavarṇaiśca bhasmadhāraṇamuttamam |
anyairapi yathājīvaissadeti śivaśāsanam || 38 ||

bhasmasnānena yāvantaḥ kaṇāḥ svāṅge pratiṣṭhitāḥ |
tāvanti śivaliṃgāni tanau dhatte hi dhārakaḥ || 39 ||

brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāścāpi ca saṃkarāḥ |
striyotha vidhavā bālāḥ prāptāḥ pākhaṃḍikāstathā || 40 ||

brahmacārī gṛhī vanyaḥ saṃnyāsī vā vratī tathā |
nāryo bhasma tripuṃḍrāṃkā muktā eva na saṃśayaḥ || 41 ||

jñānājñānadhṛto vāpi vahnidāhasamo yathā |
jñānājñānadhṛtaṃ bhasma pāvayetsakalaṃ naram || 42 ||

nāśnīyājjalamannamalpamapi vā bhasmākṣadhṛtyā vinā bhuktvāvātha gṛhī vanīpatiyatirvarṇī tathā saṃkaraḥ |
enobhuṅnarakaṃ prayāti sata dāgāyatrijāpena tadvarṇānāṃ tu yatestu mukhyapraṇavājapena muktaṃbhavet || 43 ||

tripuṃḍraṃ ye viniṃdanti nindanti śivameva te |
dhārayanti ca ye bhaktyā dhārayanti tameva te || 44 ||

dhigbhasmarahitaṃ bhālaṃ dhiggrāmamaśivālayam |
dhiganīśārcanaṃ janma dhigvidyāmaśivāśrayām || 45 ||

ye niṃdanti maheśvaraṃ trijagatāmādhārabhūtaṃ haraṃ ye nindanti tripuṃḍradhāraṇakaraṃ doṣastu taddarśane |
te vai saṃkarasūkarāsurakharaśvakroṣṭukīṭopamā jātā eva bhavanti pāpaparamāstenārakāḥ kevalam || 46 ||

te dṛṣṭvā śaśibhāskarau niśi dine svapnepi no kevalaṃ paśyantu śrutirudrasūktajapato mucyeta tenādṛtāḥ |
satsaṃbhāṣaṇato bhaveddhi narakaṃ nistāravānāsthitaṃ ye bhasmādividhāraṇaṃ hi puruṣaṃ niṃdanti maṃdā hi te || 47 ||

na tāntrikastvadhikṛto norddhvapuṃḍradharo mune |
santaptacakracihnotra śivayajñe bahiṣkṛtaḥ || 48 ||

tatraite bahavo lokā bṛhajjābālacoditāḥ |
te vicāryāḥ prayatnena tato bhasmarato bhavet || 49 ||

yaccaṃdanaiścaṃdanakepi miśraṃ dhāryaṃ hi bhasmaiva tripuṃḍrabhasmanā |
vibhūtibhālopari kiṃcanāpi dhāryaṃ sadā no yadi santibuddhayaḥ || 50 ||

strībhistripuṇḍramalakāvadhi dhāraṇīyaṃ bhasma dvijādibhiratho vidhavābhirevam |
tadvatsadāśramavatāṃ viśadāvibhūtirdhāryāpavargaphaladā sakalāghahantrī || 51 ||

tripuṇḍraṃ kurute yastu bhasmanā vidhipūrvakam |
mahāpātakasaṃghātairmucyate copapātakaiḥ || 52 ||

brahmacārī gṛhastho vā vānaprasthotha vā yatiḥ |
brahmakṣattrāśca viṭśūdrāstathānye patitādhamāḥ || 53 ||

uddhūlanaṃ tripuṃḍraṃ ca dhṛtvā śuddhā bhavanti ca |
bhasmano vidhinā samyakpāparāśiṃ vihāya ca || 54 ||

bhasmadhārī viśeṣeṇa strīgohatyādipātakaiḥ |
vīrahatyāśvahatyābhyāṃ mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ || 55 ||

paradravyāpaharaṇaṃ paradārābhimarśanam |
paranindā parakṣetraharaṇaṃ parapīḍanam || 56 ||

sasyārāmādiharaṇaṃ gṛhadāhādikarma ca |
gohiraṇyamahiṣyāditilakambalavāsasām || 57 ||

annadhānyajalādīnāṃ nīcebhyaśca parigrahaḥ |
daśaveśyāmataṃgīṣu vṛṣalīṣu naṭīṣu ca || 58 ||

rajasvalāsu kanyāsu vidhavāsu ca maithunam |
māṃsacarmarasādīnāṃ lavaṇasya ca vikrayaḥ || 59 ||

paiśunyaṃ kūṭavādaśca sākṣimithyābhilāṣiṇām |
evamādīnyasaṃkhyāni pāpāni vividhāni ca |
sadya eva vinaśyanti tripuṃḍrasya ca dhāraṇāt || 60 ||

śivadravyāpaharaṇaṃ śivaniṃdā ca kutracit |
niṃdā ca śivabhaktānāṃ prāyaścittairna śuddhyati || 61 ||

rudrākṣaṃ yasya gātreṣu lalāṭe tu tripaṃḍrakam |
sacāṃḍālopi saṃpūjyassarvavarṇottamottamaḥ || 62 ||

yāni tīrthāni lokesmingaṃgādyāssaritaśca yāḥ |
snāto bhavati sarvatra lalāṭe yastripuṃḍrakam || 63 ||

saptakoṭi mahāmantrāḥ paṃcākṣarapurassarāḥ |
tathānye koṭiśo mantrāḥ śaivakaivalyahetavaḥ || 64 ||

anye mantrāśca devānāṃ sarvasaukhyakarā mune |
te sarve tasya vaśyāḥ syuryo bibharti tripuṃḍrakam || 65 ||

sahasraṃ pūrvajātānāṃ sahasraṃ janayiṣyatām |
svavaṃśajānāṃ jñātīnāmuddharedyastripuṃḍrakṛt || 66 ||

iha bhuktvā khilānbhogāndīrghāyurvyādhivarjitaḥ |
jīvitānte ca maraṇaṃ sukhenaiva prapadyate || 67 ||

aṣṭaiśvaryaguṇopetaṃ prāpya divyavapuḥ śivam |
divyaṃ vimānamāruhya divyatridaśasevitam || 68 ||

vidyādharāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ gaṃdharvāṇāṃ mahaujasām |
iṃdrādilokapālānāṃ lokeṣu ca yathākramam || 69 ||

bhuktvā bhogānsuvipulānprajeśānāṃ padeṣu ca |
brahmaṇaḥ padamāsādya tatra kanyāśataṃ ramet || 70 ||

tatra brahmāyuṣo mānaṃ bhuktvā bhogānanekaśaḥ |
viṣṇorloke labhedbhogaṃ yāvadbrahmaśatātyayaḥ || 71 ||

śivalokaṃ tataḥ prāpya labdhveṣṭaṃ kāmamakṣayam |
śivasāyujyamāpnoti saṃśayo nātra jāyate || 72 ||

sarvopaniṣadāṃ sāraṃ samālokya muhurmuhuḥ |
idameva hi nirṇītaṃ paraṃ śreyastripuṃḍrakam || 73 ||

vibhūtiṃ niṃdate yo vai brāhmaṇaḥ sonyajātakaḥ |
yāti ca narake ghore yāvadbrahmā caturmukhaḥ || 74 ||

śrāddhe yajñe jape home vaiśvadeve surārcane |
dhṛtatripuṃḍraḥ pūtātmā mṛtyuṃ jayati mānavaḥ || 75 ||

jalasnānaṃ malatyāge bhasmasnānaṃ sadā śuci |
mantrasnānaṃ haretpāpaṃ jñānasnāne paraṃ padam || 76 ||

sarvatīrtheṣu yatpuṇyaṃ sarvatīrtheṣu yatphalam |
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti bhasmasnānakaro naraḥ || 77 ||

bhasmasnānaṃ paraṃ tīrthaṃ gaṃgāsnānaṃ dine dine |
bhasmarūpī śivaḥ sākṣādbhasma trailokyapāvanam || 78 ||

na tadūnaṃ na taddhyānaṃ na taddānaṃ japo na saḥ |
tripuṃḍreṇa vināyena vipreṇa yadanuṣṭhitam || 79 ||

vānaprasthasya kanyānāṃ dīkṣāhīnanṛṇāṃ tathā |
madhyāhnātprāgjalairyuktaṃ parato jalavarjitam || 80 ||

evaṃ tripuṃḍraṃ yaḥ kuryyānnityaṃ niyatamānasaḥ |
śivabhaktaḥ savijñeyo bhuktiṃ muktiṃ ca viṃdati || 81 ||

yasyāṃgenaiva rudrākṣa ekopi bahupuṇyadaḥ |
tasya janmanirarthaṃ syāttripuṃḍrarahito yadi || 82 ||

evaṃ tripuṃḍramāhātmyaṃ samāsātkathitaṃ mayā |
rahasyaṃ sarvajantūnāṃ gopanīyamidaṃ tvayā || 83 ||

tisro rekhā bhavantyeva sthāneṣu munipuṃgavāḥ |
lalāṭādiṣu sarveṣu yathokteṣu budhairmune || 84 ||

bhruvormadhyaṃ samārabhya yāvadanto bhavedbhruvoḥ |
tāvatpramāṇaṃ saṃdhāryaṃ lalāṭe ca tripuṃḍrakam || 85 ||

madhyamānāmikāṃgulyā madhye tu pratilomataḥ |
aṃguṣṭhena kṛtā rekhā tripuṃḍrākhyā bhidhīyate || 86 ||

madhyeṃgulibhirādāya tisṛbhirbhasma yatnataḥ |
tripuṇḍradhārayedbhaktyā bhuktimuktipradaṃ param || 87 ||

tisṛṇāmapi rekhānāṃ pratyekaṃ navadevatāḥ |
sarvatrāṃgeṣu tā vakṣye sāvadhānatayā śṛṇu || 88 ||

akāro gārhapatyāgnirbhūdharmaśca rajoguṇaḥ |
ṛgvedaśca kriyāśaktiḥ prātaḥsavanameva ca || 89 ||

mahadevaśca rekhāyāḥ prathamāyāśca devatā |
vijñeyā muniśārdūlāḥ śivadīkṣāparāyaṇaiḥ || 90 ||

ukāro dakṣiṇāgniśca nabhastattvaṃ yajustathā |
madhyaṃdinaṃ ca savanamicchāśaktyantarātmakau || 91 ||

maheśvaraśca rekhāyā dvitīyāyāśca devatā |
vijñeyā muniśārdūla śivadīkṣāparāyaṇaiḥ || 92 ||

makārāhavanīyau ca paramātmā tamodivau |
jñānaśaktiḥ sāmavedastṛtīyaṃ savanaṃ tathā || 93 ||

śivaścaiva ca rekhāyāstṛtiyāyāśca devatā |
vijñeyā muniśārdūla śivadīkṣāparāyaṇau || 94 ||

evaṃ nityaṃ namaskṛtya sadbhaktyā sthānadevatāḥ |
tripuṃḍraṃ dhārayecchuddho bhuktiṃ muktiṃ ca viṃdati || 95 ||

ityuktāḥ sthānadevāśca sarvāṃgeṣu munīśvaraḥ |
teṣāṃ saṃbaṃdhino bhaktyā sthānāni śṛṇu sāṃpratam || 96 ||

dvātriṃśatsthānake vārddhaṣoḍaśasthānakepi ca |
aṣṭasthāne tathā caiva paṃcasthānepi nānyaset || 97 ||

uttamāṃge lalāṭe ca karṇayornetrayostathā |
nāsāvaktragaleṣvevaṃ hastadvaya ataḥ param || 98 ||

kūrpare maṇibaṃdhe ca hṛdaye pārśvayordvayoḥ |
nābhau muṣkadvaye caivamūrvorgulphe ca jānuni || 99 ||

jaṃghādvayepadadvandve dvātriṃśatsthānamuttamam |
agnyabbhūvāyudigdeśadikpālānvasubhiḥ saha || 100 ||

dharā dhruvaśca somaśca apaścevānilonalaḥ |
pratyūṣaśca prabhāsaśca vasavoṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ || 101 ||

eteṣāṃ nāmamātreṇa tripuṃḍraṃ dhārayedbudhāḥ |
kuryādvā ṣoḍaśasthāne tripuṇḍraṃ tu samāhitaḥ || 102 ||

śīrṣake ca lalāṭeca kaṃṭhe cāṃsadvaye bhuje |
kūrpare maṇibaṃdhe ca hṛdaye nābhipārśvake || 103 ||

pṛṣṭhe caivaṃ pratiṣṭhāya yajettatrāśvidaivate |
śivaśaktiṃ tathā rudramīśaṃ nāradameva ca || 104 ||

vāmādinavaśaktīśca etāḥ ṣoḍaśadevatāḥ |
nāsatyo dasrakaścaiva aśvinau dvau prakīrtitau || 105 ||

athavā mūrddhni keśe ca karmayorvadane tathā |
bāhudvaye ca hṛdaye nābhyāmūruyuge tathā || 106 ||

jānudvaye ca padayoḥ pṛṣṭhabhāge ca ṣoḍaśa |
śivaścandraśca rudraḥ ko vighneśo viṣṇureva vā || 107 ||

śrīścaiva hṛdaye śambhustathā nābhau prajāpatiḥ |
nāgaśca nāgakanyāśca ubhayorṛṣikanyakāḥ || 108 ||

pādayośca samudrāśca tīrthāḥ pṛṣṭhe viśālataḥ |
ityeva ṣoḍaśasthānamaṣṭasthānamathocyate || 109 ||

guhyasthānaṃ lalāṭaśca karṇadvayamanuttamam |
aṃsayugmaṃ ca hṛdayaṃ nābhirityevamaṣṭakam || 110 ||

brahmā ca ṛṣayaḥ saptadevatāśca prakīrtitāḥ |
ityevaṃ tu samuddiṣṭaṃ bhasmavidbhirmunīśvarāḥ || 111 ||

atha vā mastakaṃ bāhūhṛdayaṃ nābhireva ca |
paṃcasthānānyamūnyāhurdhāraṇe bhasmavijjanāḥ || 112 ||

yathāsaṃbhavanaṃ kuryyāddeśakālādyapekṣayā |
uddhūlanepyaśaktiścettripuṇḍrādīni kārayet || 113 ||

trinetraṃ triguṇādhāraṃ trivedajanakaṃ śivam |
smarannamaḥ śivāyeti lalāṭe tu tripuṇḍrakam || 114 ||

īśābhyāṃ nama ityuktvāpārśvayośca tripuṇḍrakam |
bījābhyāṃ nama ityuktvā dhārayettu prakoṣṭhayoḥ || 115 ||

kuryādadhaḥ pitṛbhyāṃ ca umeśābhyāṃ tathopari |
bhīmāyeti tataḥ pṛṣṭhe śirasaḥ paścime tathā || 116 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ bhasmadhāraṇavarṇanonāma caturviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 24 ||

sūta uvāca |

śainakarṣe mahāprājña śivarūpamahāpate |
śṛṇu rudrākṣamāhātmyaṃ samāsātkathayāmyaham || 1 ||

śivapriyatamo jñeyo rudrākṣaḥ parapāvanaḥ |
darśanātsparśanājjāpyātsarvapāpaharaḥ smṛtaḥ || 2 ||

purā rudrākṣamahimā devyagre kathito mune |
lokopakaraṇārthāya śivena paramātmanā || 3 ||

śiva uvāca |

śṛṇu devimaheśāni rudrākṣamahimā śive |
kathayāmi tavaprītyā bhaktānāṃ hitakāmyayā || 4 ||

divyavarṣasahasrāṇi maheśāni punaḥ purā |
tapaḥ prakurvatastrastaṃ manaḥ saṃyamya vai mama || 5 ||

svatantreṇa pareśena lokopakṛtikāriṇā |
līlayā parameśāni cakṣurunmīlitaṃ mayā || 6 ||

puṭābhyāṃ cārucakṣurbhyāṃ patitā jalabiṃdavaḥ |
tatrāśrubindavo jātā vṛkṣā rudrākṣasaṃjñakāḥ || 7 ||

sthāvaratvamanuprāpya bhaktānugrahakāraṇāt |
te dattā viṣṇubhaktebhyaścaturvarṇebhya eva ca || 8 ||

bhūmau gauḍodbhavāṃścakre rudrākṣāñchivavallabhān |
mathurāyāmayodhyāyāṃ laṃkāyāṃ malaye tathā || 9 ||

sahyādrau ca tathā kāśyāṃ daśeṣvanyeṣu vā tathā |
parānasahyapāpaughabhedanāñchrutinodanāt || 10 ||

brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrā jātā mamājñayā |
rudrākṣāste pṛthivyāṃ tu tajjātīyāḥ śubhākṣakāḥ || 11 ||

śvetaraktāḥ pītakṛṣṇā varṇājñeyāḥ kramādbudhaiḥ |
svajātīyaṃ nṛbhirdhāryaṃ rudrākṣaṃ varṇataḥ kramāt || 12 ||

varṇaistu tatphalaṃ dhāryaṃ bhuktimuktiphalepsubhiḥ |
śivabhaktairviśeṣeṇa śivayoḥ prītaye sadā || 13 ||

dhātrīphalapramāṇaṃ yacchreṣṭhametadudāhṛtam |
badarīphalamātraṃ tu madhyamaṃ saṃprakīrttitam || 14 ||

adhamaṃ caṇamātraṃ syātprakriyaiṣā parocyate |
śṛṇu pārvati suprītyā bhaktānāṃ hitakāmyayā || 15 ||

badarīphalamātraṃ ca yatsyātkila maheśvari |
tathāpi phaladaṃ loke sukhasaubhāgyavarddhanam || 16 ||

dhātrīphalasamaṃ yatsyātsarvāriṣṭavināśanam |
guṃjayā sadṛśaṃ yatsyātsarvārthaphalasādhanam || 17 ||

yathā yathā laghuḥ syādvai tathādhikaphalapradam |
ekaikataḥ phalaṃ proktaṃ daśāṃśairadhikaṃ budhaiḥ || 18 ||

rudrākṣadhāraṇaṃ proktaṃ pāpanāśanahetave |
tasmācca dhāraṇī yo vai sarvārthasādhano dhruvam || 19 ||

yathā ca dṛśyate loke rudrākṣaphaladaḥ śubhaḥ |
na tathā dṛśyate .anyā ca mālikā parameśvari || 20 ||

samāḥ snigdhā dṛḍhāḥ sthūlāḥ kaṃṭakaiḥ saṃyutāḥ śubhāḥ |
rudrākṣāḥ kāmadā devi bhuktimuktipradāḥ sadā || 21 ||

krimiduṣṭaṃ chinnabhinnaṃ kaṃṭakairhīnameva ca |
vraṇayuktamavṛttaṃ ca rudrākṣānṣaḍvivarjayet || 22 ||

svayameva kṛtadvāraṃ rudrākṣaṃ syādihottamam |
yattu pauruṣayatnena kṛtaṃ tanmadhyamaṃ bhavet || 23 ||

rudrākṣadhāraṇaṃ prāptaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam |
rudrasaṃkhyāśataṃ dhṛtvā rudrarūpo bhavennaraḥ || 24 ||

ekādaśaśatānīha dhṛtvā yatphalamāpyate |
tatphalaṃ śakyate naiva vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi || 25 ||

śatārddhena yutaiḥ paṃcaśatairvai mukuṭaṃ matam |
rudrākṣairviracetsamyagbhaktimānpuruṣo varaḥ || 26 ||

tribhiḥ śataiḥ ṣaṣṭiyuktaistrirāvṛttyā tathā punaḥ |
rudrākṣairupavītaṃ va nirmīyādbhaktitatparaḥ || 27 ||

śikhāyāṃ ca trayaṃ proktaṃ rudrakṣāṇāṃ maheśvari |
karṇayoḥ ṣaṭ ca ṣaṭcaiva vāmadakṣiṇayostathā || 28 ||

śatamekottaraṃ kaṃṭhe bāhvorvai rudrasaṃkhyayā |
kūrparadvārayostatra maṇibaṃdhe tathā punaḥ || 29 ||

upavīte trayaṃ dhāryaṃ śivabhaktiratairnaraiḥ |
śeṣānurvaritānpaṃca sammitāndhārayetkaṭau || 30 ||

etatsaṃkhyā dhṛtā yena rudrākṣāḥ parameśvari |
tadrūpaṃ tu praṇamyaṃ hi stutyaṃ sarvairmaheśavat || 31 ||

evaṃbhūtaṃ sthitaṃ dhyāne yadā kṛtvāsanairjanam |
śiveti vyāharaṃścaiva dṛṣṭvā pāpaiḥ pramucyate || 32 ||

śatādikasahasrasya vidhireṣa prakīrtitaḥ |
tadabhāve prakāronyaḥ śubhaḥ saṃprocyate mayā || 33 ||

śikhāyāmekarudrākṣaṃ śirasā triṃśataṃ vahet |
paṃcāśacca gale dadhyādbāhvoḥ ṣoḍaśa ṣoḍaśa || 34 ||

maṇibaṃdhe dvādaśadviskaṃdhe paṃcaśataṃ vahet |
aṣṭottaraśatairmālyamupavītaṃ prakalpayet || 35 ||

evaṃ sahasrarudrākṣāndhārayedyo dṛḍhavrataḥ |
taṃ namanti surāḥ sarve yathā rudrastathaiva saḥ || 36 ||

ekaṃ śikhāyāṃ rudrākṣaṃ catvāriṃśattu mastake |
dvātriṃśatkaṇṭhadeśe tu vakṣasyaṣṭottaraṃ śatam || 37 ||

ekaikaṃ karṇayoḥ ṣaṭṣaḍbāhvoḥ ṣoḍaśa ṣoḍaśa |
karayoravimānena dviguṇena munīśvara || 38 ||

saṃkhyā prītirdhṛtā yena sopi śaivajanaḥ paraḥ |
śivavatpūjanīyo hi vaṃdyassarvairabhīkṣṇaśaḥ || 39 ||

śirasīśānamantreṇa karṇe tatpuruṣeṇa ca |
aghoreṇa gale dhāryaṃ tenaiva hṛdayepi ca || 40 ||

aghorabījamantreṇa karayordhārayetsudhīḥ |
paṃcadaśākṣagrathitāṃ vāmadevena codare || 41 ||

paṃca brahmabhiraṃgaśca trimālāṃ paṃcasapta ca |
athavā mūlamantreṇa sarvānakṣāṃstudhārayet || 42 ||

madyaṃ māṃsaṃ tu laśunaṃ palāṇḍuṃ śigrumeva ca |
śleṣmāntakaṃ viḍvarāhaṃ bhakṣaṇe varjayettataḥ || 43 ||

valakṣaṃ rudrākṣaṃ dvijatanubhireveha vihitaṃ suraktaṃ kṣattrāṇāṃ pramuditamume pītamasakṛt // 44 |

chinnaṃ khaṃḍitaṃ bhinnaṃ vidīrṇa /

tato vaiśyairdhāryaṃ pratidivasabhāvaśyakamaho tathā kṛṣṇaṃ śūdraiḥ śrutigaditamārgoyamagaje || 44 ||

varṇī vanī gṛhayatīrniyamena dadhyādetadrahasyaparamo na hi jātu tiṣṭhet |
rudrākṣadhāraṇamidaṃ sukṛtaiśca labhyaṃ tyaktvedametadakhilānnarakānprayānti || 45 ||

ādāvāmalakātsvato laghutarā rugṇāstataḥ kaṃṭakaiḥ saṃdaṣṭāḥ kṛmibhistanūpakaraṇacchidreṇa hīnāstathā |
dhāryā naiva śubhepsubhiścaṇakavadrudrākṣamapyantato rudrākṣomama liṃgamaṃgalamume sūkṣmaṃ praśastaṃ sadā || 46 ||

sarvāśramāṇāṃ varṇānāṃ strīśūdrāṇāṃ śivājñayā |
dhāryāḥ sadaiva rudrākṣā yatīnāṃ praṇavena hi || 47 ||

divā bibhradrātrikṛtai rātrau vibhraddivākṛtaiḥ |
prātarmadhyāhnasāyāhne mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ || 48 ||

ye tripuṇḍradharā loke jaṭādhāriṇa eva ye |
ye rudrākṣadharāste vai yamalokaṃ prayānti na || 49 ||

rudrākṣamekaṃ śirasā bibharti tathā tripuṇḍraṃ ca lalāṭamadhye |
paṃcākṣaraṃ ye hi japanti mantraṃ pūjyā bhavadbhiḥ khalu te hi sādhavaḥ || 50 ||

yasyāṅge nāsti rudrākṣastripuṇḍraṃ bhālapaṭṭake |
mukhe paṃcākṣaraṃ nāsti tamānaya yamālayam || 51 ||

jñātvā jñātvā tatprabhāvaṃ bhasmarudrākṣadhāriṇaḥ |
te pūjyāḥ sarvadāsmākaṃ no netavyāḥ kadācana || 52 ||

evamājñāpayāmāsa kālopi nijakiṅkarān |
tatheti mattvā te sarve tūṣṇīmāsansuvismitāḥ || 53 ||

ata eva mahādevi rudrākṣotyaghanāśanaḥ |
taddharo matpriyaḥ śuddho .atyaghavānapi pārvati || 54 ||

haste bāhau tathā mūrdhni rudrākṣaṃ dhārayettu yaḥ |
avadhyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ rudrarūpī caredbhuvi || 55 ||

surāsurāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ vaṃdanīyaḥ sadā sa vai |
pūjanīyo hi dṛṣṭasya pāpahā ca yathā śivaḥ || 56 ||

dhyānajñānāvamuktopi rudrākṣaṃ dhārayettu yaḥ |
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim || 57 ||

rudrākṣeṇa japanmantraṃ puṇyaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet |
daśakoṭiguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ dhāraṇāllabhate naraḥ || 58 ||

yāvatkālaṃ hi jīvasya śarīrastho bhavetsa vai |
tāvatkālaṃ svalpamṛtyurna taṃ devi vibādhate || 59 ||

tripuṃḍreṇa ca saṃyuktaṃ rudrākṣāvilasāṃgakam |
mṛtyuṃjayaṃ japantaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā rudraphalaṃ labhet || 60 ||

paṃcadevapriyaścaiva sarvadevapriyastathā |
sarvamantrāñjapedbhakto rudrākṣamālayā priye || 61 ||

viṣṇvādidevabhaktāśca dhārayeyurna saṃśayaḥ |
rudrabhakto viśeṣeṇa rudrākṣāndhārayetsadā || 62 ||

rudrākṣā vividhāḥ proktāsteṣāṃ bhedānvadāmyaham |
śṛṇu pārvati sadbhaktyā bhuktimuktiphalapradān || 63 ||

ekavaktraḥ śivaḥ sākṣādbhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ |
tasya darśanamātreṇa brahmahatyā vyapohati || 64 ||

yatra saṃpūjitastatra lakṣmīrdūratarā na hi |
naśyantyupadravāḥ sarve sarvakāmā bhavanti hi || 65 ||

dvivaktro devadeveśassarvakāmaphalapradaḥ |
viśeṣataḥ sa rudrākṣo govadhaṃ nāśayeddrutam || 66 ||

trivaktro yo hi rudrākṣaḥ sākṣātsādhanadassadā |
tatprabhāvādbhaveyurvai vidyāḥ sarvāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ || 67 ||

caturvaktraḥ svayaṃ brahmā narahatyāṃ vyapohati |
darśanātsparśanātsadyaścaturvargaphalapradaḥ || 68 ||

paṃcavaktraḥ svayaṃ rudraḥ kālāgnirnāmataḥ prabhuḥ |
sarvamuktipradaścaiva sarvakāmaphalapradaḥ || 69 ||

agamyāgamanaṃ pāpamabhakṣyasya ca bhakṣaṇam |
ityādisarvapāpāni paṃcavaktro vyapohati || 70 ||

ṣaḍvaktraḥ kārtikeyastudhāraṇāddakṣiṇe bhuje |
brahmahatyādikaiḥ pāpairmucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ || 71 ||

saptavaktro maheśāni hyanaṃgo nāma nāmataḥ |
dhāraṇāttasya deveśidaridropīśvaro bhavet || 72 ||

rudrākṣaścāṣṭavaktraśca vasumūrtiśca bhairavaḥ |
dhāraṇāttasya pūrṇāyurmṛto bhavati śūlabhṛt || 73 ||

bhairavo navavaktraśca kapilaśca muniḥ smṛtaḥ |
durgā vāta dadhiṣṭhātrī navarūpā maheśvarī || 74 ||

taṃ dhārayedvāmahaste rudrākṣaṃ bhaktitatparaḥ |
sarveśvaro bhavennūnaṃ mama tulyo na saṃśayaḥ || 75 ||

daśavaktro maheśāni svayaṃ devo janārdanaḥ |
dhāraṇāttasya deveśi sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt || 76 ||

ekādaśamukho yastu rudrākṣaḥ parameśvari |
sa rudro dhāraṇāttasya sarvatra vijayī bhavet || 77 ||

dvādaśāsyaṃ tu rudrākṣaṃ dhārayetkeśadeśake |
ādityāścaiva te sarvedvādaśaiva sthitāstathā || 78 ||

trayodaśamukho viśvedevastaddhāraṇānnaraḥ |
sarvānkāmānavāpnoti saubhāgyaṃ maṃgalaṃlabhet || 79 ||

caturdaśamukho yo hi rudrākṣaḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ |
dhārayenmūrdhni taṃ bhaktyā sarvapāpaṃ praṇaśyati || 80 ||

iti rudrākṣabhedā hi proktā vai mukhabhedataḥ |
tattanmantrāñchṛṇu prītyā kramācchailleśvarātmaje || 81 ||

oṃ hrīṃ namaḥ 1 oṃ namaḥ 2 oṃ klīṃ namaḥ 3 oṃ hrīṃ namaḥ 4 oṃ hrīṃ namaḥ 5 oṃ hrīṃ huṃ namaḥ 6 oṃ huṃnamaḥ 7 oṃ huṃ namaḥ 8 oṃ hrīṃ huṃ namaḥ 9 oṃ hrīṃ namaḥ namaḥ 10 oṃ hrīṃ huṃ namaḥ 11 oṃ krauṃ kṣauṃ rauṃ namaḥ 12 oṃ hrīṃ namaḥ 13 oṃ nama 14

bhaktiśraddhā yutaścaiva sarvakāmārthasiddhaye |
rudrākṣāndhārayenmantrairdevanālasya varjitaḥ || 82 ||

vinā mantreṇa ho dhatte rudrākṣaṃ bhuvi mānavaḥ |
sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ yāvadindrāścaturdaśa || 83 ||

rudrākṣamālinaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhūtapretapiśācakāḥ |
ḍākinīśākinī caiva ye cānye drohakārakāḥ || 84 ||

kṛtrimaṃ caiva yatkiṃcidabhicārādikaṃ ca yat |
tatsarvaṃ dūrato yāti dṛṣṭvā śaṃkitavigraham || 85 ||

rudrākṣamālinaṃ dṛṣṭvā śivo viṣṇuḥ prasīdati |
devīgaṇapatissūryaḥ surāścānyepi pārvati || 86 ||

evaṃ jñātvā tu māhātmyaṃ rudrākṣasya maheśvari |
samyagdhāryāssamantrāśca bhaktyādharmavivṛddhaye || 87 ||

ityuktaṃ girijāgre hi śivena paramātmanā |
bhasmarūdrākṣamāhātmyaṃ bhuktimuktiphalapradam || 88 ||

śivasyātipriyau jñeyau bhasmarudrākṣadhāriṇau |
taddhāraṇaprabhāvaddhi bhuktirmuktirna saṃśayaḥ || 89 ||

bhasmarudrākṣadhārī yaḥ śivabhaktassa ucyate |
paṃcākṣarajapāsaktaḥ paripūrṇaśca sanmukhe || 90 ||

vinā bhasmatripuṃḍreṇa vinā rudrākṣamālayā |
pūjitopi mahādevo nābhīṣṭaphaladāyakaḥ || 91 ||

tatsarvaṃ ca samākhyātaṃ yatpṛṣṭaṃ hi munīśvara |
bhasmarudrākṣamāhātmyaṃ sarvakāmasamṛddhidam || 92 ||

etadyaḥ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ māhātmyaṃ paramaṃ śubham |
rudrākṣabhasmanorbhaktyā sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt || 93 ||

iha sarvasukhaṃ bhuktvā putrapautrādisaṃyutaḥ |
labhetparatra sanmokṣaṃ śivasyātipriyo bhavet || 94 ||

vidyeśvarasaṃhiteyaṃ kathitā vo munīśvarāḥ |
sarvasiddhipradā nityaṃ muktidā śivaśāsanāt || 95 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe prathamāyāṃ vidyeśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ sādhyasādhanakhaṇḍe rudrākṣamahātmyavarṇanonāma pañcaviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 25 ||
